### [1] [Predictivity and Utility of Neural Surrogates of Multiscale PDEs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20061)
*Karthik Duraisamy*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 论文指出科学机器学习（scientific machine learning）作为多尺度偏微分方程（multi-scale partial differential equations）通用模拟器的局限性，特别是由于谱偏置（spectral bias）和粗粒化（coarse-graining）导致的高频信息丢失问题，并通过两个简单示例进行说明。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然科学机器学习常被视为多尺度偏微分方程经典数值求解器的通用模拟器，但大多数表面成功案例实际上受到根本性限制。论文旨在揭示这些限制，特别是神经代理模型（neural surrogates）在解决多尺度问题时的固有缺陷。

Method: 采用理论分析结合两个简单示例来表征谱偏置、粗粒化和误差累积问题。通过分析中程天气预报在再分析数据（reanalysis data）上的表现，说明其处于有利的"甜点"（sweet spot）位置。

Result: 研究发现神经代理模型由于谱偏置而系统性地欠解析高频内容，粗粒化通过不可逆信息损失加剧了这一问题。许多多尺度问题中，任何架构或训练过程都无法完全恢复粗粒化表示所丢弃的信息。

Conclusion: 论文确定了神经代理模型具有真正价值的领域，建议进一步研究神经-经典混合方法（neural-classical hybrids），并呼吁建立更好的报告标准（reporting standards）。同时指出中程天气预报的有利情况无法推广到真正的混沌多尺度场景。

Abstract: Scientific machine learning is increasingly being spoken of as universal emulators for classical numerical solvers for multi-scale partial differential equations, but most apparent successes can be explained by facts that also define their limits. Many successful benchmarks live on low-dimensional solution manifolds where any competent reduced model will interpolate well. More fundamentally, neural surrogates systematically under-resolve high-frequency content due to spectral bias, and coarse-graining compounds this problem through irreversible information loss. In many multi-scale problems, no architecture or training procedure can fully recover what the coarse representation discards. Two simple examples are used to characterize spectral bias, coarse-graining and error accumulation. We discuss why medium-range weather prediction on reanalysis data sits in a favorable sweet spot and why this will not generalize to genuinely chaotic multi-scale scenarios. We identify domains where neural surrogates offer genuine value, propose further research on neural-classical hybrids, and call for better reporting standards.

</details>


### [2] [Quantitative Direct Sampling for Initial Acoustic Sources](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20187)
*Xiaodong Liu,Xianchao Wang*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出基于时空积分和辅助函数的新型指示函数，用于从时变波测量中定量重建初始声源，并通过数值实验验证了方法的鲁棒性、准确性和计算效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在解决从时变波测量中定量重建初始声源（initial acoustic sources）的挑战性问题，这对于实际声学成像应用具有重要意义。

Method: 通过声学数据的时空积分和精心设计的辅助函数（auxiliary functions）定义新型指示函数（indicator functions），这些指示函数为证明源重建的唯一性和开发定量直接采样方案（quantitative direct sampling scheme）提供了理论基础。

Result: 综合数值实验表明，所提出的方法具有鲁棒性（robustness）、准确性（accuracy）和计算效率（computational efficiency），突显了其在实践应用中的潜力。

Conclusion: 新型指示函数不仅为声源重建的唯一性证明提供了理论基础，而且开发出的定量直接采样方案在实际声学成像应用中展现出良好的性能。

Abstract: This paper addresses the challenge of quantitatively reconstructing initial acoustic sources from time-dependent wave measurements. We introduce novel indicator functions defined through spacetime integrals of acoustic data and carefully designed auxiliary functions. These indicators are foundational for both proving the uniqueness of source reconstruction and developing a quantitative direct sampling scheme. Our comprehensive numerical experiments demonstrate the robustness, accuracy, and computational efficiency of these methods, highlighting their potential for practical acoustic imaging applications.

</details>


### [3] [Direct construction of scalar quantum fields by L{é}vy fields -- nontrivial exact Wightman fields in a wider field with a relaxed Gårding-Wightman Axioms-](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20359)
*Sergio Albeverio,Suji Kawasaki,Yumi Yahagi,Minoru W. Yoshida*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文在当前研究背景下，介绍了关于构建精确相对论量子场模型的阶段性成果。利用Lévy随机场的随机分析工具，在放宽的Gårding-Wightman公理框架下构造了Hermitian标量量子场，并通过选取适当的子空间最终构建了满足完整公理要求的非平凡Wightman量子场。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在构建精确的相对论量子场模型，特别是针对高维时空（包括d≥4的情况）。研究动机源于在放宽的Gårding-Wightman公理框架下，利用随机分析工具构造量子场理论模型。

Method: 采用基于平稳加性随机场（即Lévy随机场）的随机分析论证方法。首先在放宽的Gårding-Wightman公理框架下构造Hermitian标量量子场<ℋ, U, ψ, D>，其中场算符ψ(f)是对称算子而非自伴算子。随后通过选取ℋ的适当子空间，构建满足完整公理要求的量子场。

Result: 成功构造了满足放宽Gårding-Wightman公理框架的Hermitian标量量子场，其中场算符ψ(f)为对称算子。进一步通过选取适当的Hilbert空间子空间，实际构建了满足所有Gårding-Wightman公理要求的非平凡精确Wightman量子场。

Conclusion: 研究展示了利用Lévy随机场和随机分析工具，能够在放宽的公理框架下构造量子场模型，并通过适当的技术处理最终获得满足完整公理要求的精确相对论量子场理论。这为高维时空量子场理论的构建提供了新的方法途径。

Abstract: This paper introduces partial results, in the current situation, of ongoing considerations corresponding to the above title. A construction on exact relativistic quantum field model with the space time dimension $d \in {\mathbb N}$, including the case where $d \geq 4$, is going to be discussed. Firstly, Hermitian scalar quantum fields $<{\cal H}, U, ψ, D>$, within a relaxed framework of the Gårding-Wightman Axioms, is constructed by making use of the stochastic calculus arguments with respect to the {\it{stationary additive random fields }} on ${\mathbb R}^d$, i.e., the {\it{L{é}vy random fields}} on ${\mathbb R}^d$. The first constructed $<{\cal H}, U, ψ, D>$, here, satisfy all the requirements of the the Gårding-Wightman Axioms, except that the field operators $ψ(f)$ with $f \in {\cal S}({\mathbb R}^d \to {\mathbb R})$ are symmetric operators on the physical Hilbert space ${\cal H}$, which situation is denoted here as {\it{a relaxed framework}} of the Gårding-Wightman Axioms. Secondly, by taking the adequate subspaces of ${\cal H}$, non trivial exact Wightman quantum fields, which satisfy all the requirements of the Gårding-Wightman Axioms, are constructed actually.
  keywords: Axiomatic quantum field theory, Gårding-Wightman axioms, Bochner-Minlos theorem, L{é}vy fields on ${\mathbb R}^d$.

</details>


### [4] [Generalised Langevin Dynamics: Significance and Limitations of the Projection Operator Formalism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20453)
*Christoph Widder,Tanja Schilling*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文讨论了Mori-Zwanzig投影算子形式主义的数学基础，重点分析了广义朗之万方程（generalized Langevin equation）的推导及其在粗粒化建模中的应用，并揭示了记忆项（memory term）作为耦合项的本质而非必然与记忆相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在探讨Mori-Zwanzig投影算子形式主义的数学基础，特别是针对Mori投影和Zwanzig投影在严格数学处理上的差异。研究关注该形式主义中广义朗之万方程的推导及其数学严谨性。

Method: 采用半群理论（semigroup theory）推导Mori投影的投影算子形式主义，并分析Dyson-Duhamel恒等式在时间演化算子有界扰动（如Mori投影）和无界扰动（如Zwanzig投影）情况下的不同数学处理。通过引入与斜伴随算子（skew-adjoint operators）谱分解相关的"快"和"慢"变量子空间投影来阐明记忆项的本质。

Result: 研究发现：对于有界扰动（Mori投影），Dyson-Duhamel恒等式与常数变易公式（variation of constants formula）一致；对于无界扰动（Zwanzig投影），Dyson-Duhamel恒等式应视为正交动力学的方程，其唯一解的存在性尚未确立。Mori广义朗之万方程的所有性质可直接从Volterra方程（Volterra equations）的适定性得出。特别地，当投影到与斜伴随算子谱分解相关的"快"和"慢"变量子空间时，记忆项会消失。

Conclusion: 论文阐明了Mori-Zwanzig形式主义中数学严谨性的关键差异，揭示了记忆项本质上是耦合项而非必然与记忆相关。这一认识对理解粗粒化模型（coarse-grained model）中记忆项的物理意义具有重要启示。

Abstract: We discuss some mathematical aspects of the Mori-Zwanzig projection operator formalism. The core of the Mori-Zwanzig formalism is the generalised Langevin equation, which is typically derived from the Dyson-Duhamel identity. We derive the projection operator formalism for Mori's projection by means of semigroup theory, and we illustrate where rigorous methods fail for the case of Zwanzig's projection. For bounded perturbations of the time-evolution operator (e.g. for Mori's projection), the Dyson-Duhamel identity coincides with the variation of constants formula. For unbounded perturbations (e.g. for Zwanzigs's projection), the Dyson-Duhamel identity should be considered an equation for the orthogonal dynamics, for which the existence of unique solutions has yet to be established. Then we recall that all properties of Mori's generalised Langevin equation follow directly from the well-posedness of Volterra equations, irrespective of the projection operator formalism. Further, we discuss the use of Mori's generalised Langevin equation as a coarse-grained model. Finally, we illustrate that the memory term is a coupling term that is not necessarily related to memory. To this end, we introduce projections onto subspaces of 'fast' and 'slow' variables that are associated with the spectral decomposition of skew-adjoint operators. For these projections, the memory term vanishes.

</details>


### [5] [Superintegrable 2D systems in magnetic fields with a parabolic type integral](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20465)
*Tatiana Ekelchik,Antonella Marchesiello*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该研究证明了在二维欧几里得空间中，存在磁场时具有二次多项式动量积分的二维超可积系统仅存在于恒定磁场和恒定静电势的情况。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机是探讨二维欧几里得空间中存在磁场时，具有二次多项式动量积分的超可积系统（superintegrable systems）的存在性问题。该问题在先前研究中已针对笛卡尔型或极坐标型积分进行了分析。

Method: 研究方法假设系统存在两个运动积分（除了哈密顿量外），且这些积分是动量的二次多项式。特别地，假设其中一个积分是抛物线型（parabolic type），第二个积分是椭圆型或"非标准"抛物线型，以此扩展先前研究。

Result: 研究结果表明，在欧几里得平面上，具有二次积分的唯一二维超可积系统是那些具有恒定磁场和恒定静电势的系统。这一结论通过分析抛物线型积分与椭圆型或非标准抛物线型积分的组合得到确认。

Conclusion: 结论确认了在二维欧几里得空间中，当存在磁场且运动积分为二次多项式时，超可积系统仅存在于恒定磁场和恒定静电势的特殊情况，这完善了对该问题分类的完整理解。

Abstract: We consider the problem on the existence of two dimensional superintegrable systems in the presence of a magnetic field in the two dimensional Euclidean space. We assume the existence of two integrals of motion, besides the Hamiltonian, that are quadratic polynomials in the momenta. This problem was already studied in the cases where one integral is of Cartesian or polar type [J. Bérubé, and P. Winternitz, J. Math. Phys., 45(5): 1959-1973, 2004]. We continue the investigation by assuming that one of the integrals is of parabolic type and the second integral is of elliptic or (''non-standard'') parabolic type, confirming so far that, on the Euclidean plane, the only two dimensional superintegrable system with quadratic integrals is the one with constant magnetic field and constant electrostatic potential.

</details>


### [6] [A semiclassical approach to spectral estimates for random Landau Schrodinger operators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20525)
*D. Borthwick,S. Eswarathasan,P. D. Hislop*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明了随机朗道薛定谔算子的谱性质，利用半经典伪微分演算和Grushin方法，在朗道能级附近的谱带中建立了半经典Wegner和Minami估计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究随机朗道薛定谔算子（random Landau Schrödinger operators）在二维空间中的谱性质，特别关注有界随机势在磁场作用下的影响。该工作旨在理解磁场中随机系统的谱统计特性。

Method: 采用半经典伪微分演算（semiclassical pseudodifferential calculus），其中半经典参数h为磁场强度B的倒数。通过Grushin方法将问题简化为分析L²(ℝ)上的有效哈密顿量（effective Hamiltonian），其主要项由紧自伴伪微分算子和组成。

Result: 证明了随机朗道薛定谔算子在每个朗道能级（Landau level）附近谱带中的半经典Wegner和Minami估计。这些估计描述了特征值统计的局部性质，是随机算子谱理论中的重要结果。

Conclusion: 通过半经典分析和Grushin方法，成功建立了随机朗道薛定谔算子的谱统计估计，为理解磁场中随机系统的谱性质提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We prove spectral properties for random Landau Schrödinger operators on $L^2(\mathbb{R}^2)$ with bounded, random potentials supported in a square $Λ_L \subset \mathbb{R}^2$ of side length $L>0$, using semiclassical pseudodifferential calculus. The semiclassical parameter $h$ is the inverse of the magnetic field strength $B > 0$. By means of the Grushin method, we are led to the analysis of an effective Hamiltonian on $L^2 (\mathbb{R})$, the principal term of which is a sum of certain compact, self-adjoint pseudodifferential operators. By analyzing these operators, we prove semiclassical Wegner and Minami estimates for the random Landau Schrodinger operator in energy intervals in the spectral bands around each Landau level.

</details>


### [7] [The Tentacles Landscape](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20541)
*Pablo Groisman*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文对Zhang和Strogatz提出的Kuramoto环中吸引盆（basins of attraction）的章鱼状（octopus-like）几何结构进行了严格数学证明，证实了该结构在高维系统中的普遍性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Zhang和Strogatz通过高维模拟提出Kuramoto环中的吸引盆具有章鱼状几何结构，但高维模拟的可靠性存在疑问。本文旨在对这些特征进行严格数学证明。

Method: 采用严格的数学证明方法，针对由任意光滑奇函数（smooth odd function）耦合的相同振子（identical oscillators）环系统，证明吸引盆的几何特性。

Result: 严格证明了章鱼状图像（octopus picture）的所有特征：吸引盆体积按$e^{-kq^2}$在卷绕数（winding number）$q$上缩放，且几乎全部体积集中在丝状触手（filamentary tentacles）而非吸引子附近。

Conclusion: 本文为Kuramoto环中吸引盆的章鱼状几何结构提供了严格的数学证明，证实了Zhang和Strogatz的猜想，并解决了高维模拟的可靠性问题。

Abstract: Zhang and Strogatz [Phys. Rev. Lett. 127, 194101 (2021)] used high-dimensional simulations to argue that basins of attraction in the Kuramoto ring are octopus-like: their volume scales as $e^{-kq^2}$ in the winding number $q$, nearly all of it concentrated in filamentary tentacles rather than near the attractor. They conjecture this geometry to be common in high dimensions but note that high-dimensional simulations are unreliable. We prove every feature of the octopus picture rigorously for identical oscillators on a ring coupled by any smooth odd function strictly increasing on $(-π,π)$.

</details>


### [8] [Variational Principles for Shock Dynamics in Compressible Euler Flows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20635)
*François Gay-Balmaz,Cheng Yang*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文建立了一个变分框架，将哈密顿原理（Hamilton's principle）推广到可压缩流体动力学中的激波（shock）解，通过引入局部于间断处的附加项，使兰金-雨贡纽（Rankine-Hugoniot）条件直接从无约束变分中自然导出。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 哈密顿原理在流体力学中作为推导控制方程、分析守恒定律和设计保结构数值格式的基本工具具有核心作用。然而，其经典表述仅限于光滑解，无法直接处理激波间断（shock discontinuities）。在变分框架内解决这一限制长期以来是一个具有挑战性的问题。

Method: 对于正压欧拉方程（barotropic Euler equations），引入了一个修正的作用量原理（modified action principle），该原理包含了局部于间断处的附加贡献项。随后将方法扩展到完全可压缩欧拉方程（full compressible Euler equations），结合非平衡热力学（nonequilibrium thermodynamics）的变分表述以及适当的变分约束和唯象约束（phenomenological constraints）。

Result: 该框架允许质量、动量和能量的兰金-雨贡纽关系（Rankine-Hugoniot relations）直接从无约束变分中产生，而无需在激波处施加连续性条件。附加项可自然地解释为耗散势（dissipation potential），将变分结构与激波处的能量损失联系起来。

Conclusion: 这为可压缩流体中的激波动力学提供了一个统一的变分描述，并突显了正压模型与完全可压缩模型在处理间断处的能量和熵（entropy）时的根本区别。

Abstract: Hamilton's principle plays a central role in fluid mechanics as a fundamental tool for deriving governing equations, analyzing conservation laws, and designing structure-preserving numerical schemes. However, its classical formulation is restricted to smooth solutions and does not directly accommodate shock discontinuities. Addressing this limitation within a variational framework has long been a challenging issue. In this paper, we develop a variational framework that extends Hamilton's principle to shock solutions in compressible fluid dynamics. For the barotropic Euler equations, we introduce a modified action principle that incorporates additional contributions localized at discontinuities. This allows the Rankine--Hugoniot conditions for mass and momentum to emerge directly from unrestricted variations, without imposing continuity across shocks. The additional term admits a natural interpretation as a dissipation potential, linking the variational structure to energy loss at shocks. We then extend the approach to the full compressible Euler equations. Using a variational formulation of nonequilibrium thermodynamics together with suitable variational and phenomenological constraints, we recover the Rankine--Hugoniot relations for mass, momentum, and energy. This yields a unified variational description of shock dynamics in compressible fluids and highlights a fundamental distinction between barotropic and full compressible models in the treatment of energy and entropy at discontinuities.

</details>


### [9] [Absence of Ballistic Transport in Quantum Walks with Asymptotically Reflecting Sites](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20654)
*Houssam Abdul-Rahman,Thomas A. Jackson,Yousef Salah*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明了一维位置依赖量子行走（position dependent quantum walks）中速度为零的充分条件，从而确立了无弹道输运（ballistic transport）的存在性。研究基于稀疏双无穷位点序列的先验速度上界估计，提出了仅依赖于选定子序列上硬币参数行为的确定性判据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于建立一维位置依赖量子行走中速度为零的充分条件，从而确定弹道输运的缺失。这有助于理解量子行走的输运性质与局部硬币参数之间的基本关系。

Method: 方法基于一个先验速度上界估计，该估计通过稀疏双无穷位点序列（sparse bi-infinite sequences of sites）、其间隙结构（gap structure）以及相应的局部硬币参数（local coin parameters）来表述。由此推导出仅依赖于选定子序列上硬币参数行为的确定性判据。

Result: 研究结果包括多个速度为零的确定性判据，这些判据仅依赖于适当硬币参数沿选定子序列的行为，而与硬币在其他位置的值无关。同时讨论了随机情况作为一般方法的应用，所有结果在CMV（CMV setting）框架下保持有效。

Conclusion: 结论表明，通过基于稀疏序列和局部硬币参数的先验速度上界估计，可以建立量子行走速度为零的充分条件。这些判据具有确定性特征，且结果在更广泛的CMV框架下保持普适性。

Abstract: We prove general sufficient conditions for zero velocity in position dependent one-dimensional quantum walks, and hence for the absence of ballistic transport. Our starting point is a general a priori upper bound on the velocity, formulated in terms of sparse bi-infinite sequences of sites, their gap structure, and the corresponding local coin parameters. This estimate yields several deterministic criteria for zero velocity that depend only on the behavior of suitable coin entries along selected subsequences and are independent of the values of the coins elsewhere. We also discuss the random case as an application of the general approach. All of our results remain valid in the CMV setting.

</details>

### [10] [multisphere: a Python implementation of the Multi Sphere Shape generator (MSS) for DEM simulations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20002)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: multisphere采用多球体表示法（multi-sphere representation），将复杂颗粒重建为相交球体集，支持从三角表面网格（triangulated surface meshes）和体素化体积（voxelized volumes）两种输入格式进行转换。

Result: 开发了一个功能完整的开源Python包，实现了复杂颗粒到多球体表示的转换，并提供了评估转换质量、可视化结果和导出数据格式的工具集。

Conclusion: multisphere为DEM模拟提供了一种有效的复杂颗粒几何表示解决方案，通过开源实现促进了该方法在颗粒系统研究中的应用和推广。

Abstract: multisphere is an open-source Python package for generating multi-sphere representations of complex particles for use in DEM simulations. It reconstructs triangulated surface meshes and voxelized volumes as sets of intersecting spheres and provides tools for evaluation, visualization, and export.

### [11] [Unjamming in a 3D Granular System: The Micromechanical Role of Friction in Force Distributions and Rheological Properties](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20102)
*Vicente Salinas,Héctor Alarcón,Eduardo Rojas,Pablo Gutiérrez,Gustavo Castillo*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在探究三维摩擦球体颗粒系统中unjamming转变的微观机制，特别关注随机颗粒移除这一不同于传统压缩/膨胀驱动方式的unjamming机制，以及摩擦系数对系统行为的影响。

Method: 采用离散元方法（Discrete Element Method, DEM）模拟三维摩擦球体颗粒系统，通过随机颗粒移除（random particle extractions）系统性地降低堆积分数（packing fraction），分析微观力学量如颗粒间作用力（interparticle forces）、配位数（coordination number）和整体堆积密度随摩擦系数的演化规律。

Result: 研究结果揭示了摩擦系数对结构特性和力学观测量的依赖关系，这些趋势与致密颗粒系统中观察到的现象在定性上一致，尽管本研究采用的驱动机制（随机颗粒移除）与传统的压缩/膨胀机制存在显著差异。

Conclusion: 即使在随机颗粒移除这一不同驱动机制下，三维摩擦球体颗粒系统的unjamming转变仍表现出与摩擦系数相关的结构-力学关系，这些发现为理解颗粒材料的unjamming行为提供了新的视角。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate the unjamming transition in a three-dimensional granular system composed of frictional spheres, in which the packing fraction is systematically reduced by random particle extractions. Using Discrete Element Method (DEM) simulations, we analyze the evolution of key micro-mechanical quantities, such as the interparticle forces, the coordination number and the overall packing density as a function of the interparticle friction coefficient. Our results reveal friction-dependent relationships on structural as well as mechanical observables, and exhibit trends that are qualitatively consistent with observations reported in dense granular systems. These trends persist despite the very different driving mechanism considered here.
  This paper is part of the thematic issue \emph{``Sand, silos and asteroids: clustering challenges in granular materials research''}.

### [12] [Polymeric Solvents Control Swelling-Induced Surface Creasing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20299)
*Zechao Jiang,Zhaoyu Ding,Shaohua Yang,Ye Xu,Dongshi Guan,Abdelhamid Maali,Joshua D Mcgraw,Thomas Salez,Zaicheng Zhang,Xingkun Man*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了聚合物溶剂聚合度$N_{\rm s}$可作为调控溶胀凝胶表面褶皱的独立控制参数，通过耦合溶胀热力学与力学稳定性理论，阐明了聚合物溶剂通过改变混合熵和渗透压来调节表面稳定性的机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上，溶胀聚合物凝胶的表面褶皱通常归因于压缩应变或层间失配，但其普适性控制机制尚不明确。本研究旨在探索聚合物溶剂聚合度对表面褶皱形成的影响，以揭示更精细的调控参数。

Method: 研究采用表面结合的聚二甲基硅氧烷（polydimethylsiloxane）凝胶，使用不同聚合度的硅油（silicone oils）作为溶剂进行溶胀实验。通过耦合溶胀热力学和力学稳定性的理论框架，分析聚合物溶剂聚合度$N_{\rm s}$对混合熵和渗透压的调节作用。

Result: 实验观察到随着溶剂聚合度$N_{\rm s}$的增加，表面从褶皱状态转变为稳定状态，尽管溶胀动力学和厚度方向的溶剂浓度分布几乎相同。理论分析表明，聚合物溶剂通过降低混合熵来改变渗透压，使$N_{\rm s}$能够独立调节平衡溶胀和褶皱阈值。

Conclusion: 该研究确立了聚合物溶剂作为溶胀诱导表面褶皱的主动热力学-力学调节因子，提出的理论框架能够准确捕捉溶剂聚合度与网络弹性之间的稳定性边界，为表面形貌控制提供了新的调控维度。

Abstract: Surface creasing in swelling polymer gels is commonly attributed to compressive strain or interlayer mismatch, yet its general control remains unclear. Here we show that solvent polymerization degree $N_{\rm s}$ provides an independent control parameter for crease onset in surface-bound polydimethylsiloxane gels swollen by silicone oils. Despite nearly identical swelling kinetics and through-thickness solvent concentration profiles, we observe a transition from creased to stable surfaces with increasing $N_{\rm s}$. A theory coupling swelling thermodynamics and mechanical stability reveals that polymeric solvents reduce the mixing entropy and thereby modify the osmotic pressure, allowing $N_{\rm s}$ to tune separately the equilibrium swelling and the crease threshold. This framework captures the stability boundary across solvent polymerization degree and network elasticity. These results identify polymeric solvents as active thermodynamic-mechanical regulators of swelling-induced surface.

</details>


### [13] [Controlling microgel morphology and swelling behavior by copolymerization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20404)
*Domenico Truzzolillo,Thomas Hellweg,Julian Oberdisse*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 微凝胶颗粒在溶剂中的热敏行为（即其温度依赖性溶胀特性）在过去四十年间持续引发工业界和学术界的兴趣。本文旨在综述近五年化学合成领域的研究，重点关注通过共聚策略调控此类聚合物体积相变温度（VPTT）的方法。

Method: 主要方法是通过将主单体（通常来自PNIPAM家族）与不同疏水性单体或带有可电离基团的单体进行共聚。在某些情况下，疏水性可通过光作为外部切换参数进行调控，而离子强度或pH值可影响含带电基团微凝胶的热敏性。

Result: 由于反应性差异或特定合成路径，可生成特定的微凝胶形态，如分子梯度、核壳、互穿网络或斑块（多叶状）结构。这些结构可能导致颗粒内热敏性的空间调制。

Conclusion: 本综述表明，现今已普遍实现对体积相变温度（VPTT）和形态的多重外部控制。这些进展为微凝胶的热敏行为调控提供了多样化的策略。

Abstract: The thermosensitive behavior of microgel particles suspended in solvents, i.e. their temperature-dependent swelling properties, has triggered ongoing interest in industry and academia over the past forty years. The most-studied polymer is poly(N-isopropylacrylamide) - PNIPAM -, where the volume phase transition temperature is well known to depend on the detailed molecular architecture of the monomers. In this article, we focus on publications mostly of the past five years in chemical synthesis, aiming at shifting or controlling the volume phase transition temperature (VPTT) of such polymers by copolymerization of a main monomer - often from the PNIPAM family - with either monomers of different hydrophobicity, or with ones bearing ionizable groups. In some cases, hydrophobicity may be modulated by light as external switching parameter, whereas ionic strength or pH may act on the thermosensitivity of the microgels containing charged groups. Due to either differences in reactivity, or specific synthesis routes, particular microgel morphologies, such as molecular gradient, core-shell, interpenetrated, or patchy (multi-lobular) structures may be generated. They may give rise to spatial modulations of thermosensitivity within particles and are highlighted in this review. Our short overview shows that multiple external control of VPTT and morphology is commonly achieved nowadays.

### [14] [Programming strain-stiffening in soft composites via structural memory near jamming](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20437)
*Yiqiu Zhao,Deng Pan,Yiming Pang,Jonathan Barés,Chang Xu,Che Liu,Haitao Hu,Yuliang Jin,Qin Xu*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 通过施加接近剪切堵塞（shear-jamming）相边界的机械训练协议，软复合材料中的无序接触网络能够编码结构记忆，实现从类颗粒到类生物聚合物的应变硬化（strain-stiffening）转变，为可编程软材料设计提供新策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前控制软复合材料非线性力学（如应变硬化）的策略主要依赖聚合物基质的非线性弹性，而离散夹杂物之间无序接触网络的非平衡和历史依赖性在复合材料力学中的作用尚未被探索。

Method: 通过在剪切堵塞（shear-jamming）相边界附近施加机械训练协议，并采用粗粒度（coarse-grained）复合材料模型进行模拟，研究接触网络的结构记忆效应。

Result: 接触网络中编码的结构记忆驱动了从类颗粒到类生物聚合物的应变硬化（strain-stiffening）转变，这种类生物聚合物的力学响应源于接近堵塞状态的接触网络的增强非仿射（non-affine）重构。

Conclusion: 无需依赖基质非线性，利用颗粒系统固有的非平衡记忆效应，建立了实现软复合材料高度可编程应变硬化（strain-stiffening）的设计策略。

Abstract: Soft composite solids, comprising discrete inclusions embedded within a compliant matrix, are emerging candidates for engineering synthetic tissues and soft robotic materials. Current strategies for controlling their nonlinear mechanics, such as strain-stiffening, have primarily relied on the nonlinear elasticity of polymer matrices. Although direct contacts between inclusions may enhance stiffening responses at high densities, the role of the non-equilibrium and history-dependent nature of disordered contact networks in composite mechanics remains unexplored. In this work, by applying a mechanical training protocol near a shear-jamming phase boundary, we demonstrate that the structural memory encoded in contact networks drives a crossover from granular-like to biopolymer-like strain stiffening. Simulations of a coarse-grained composite model reveal that this biopolymer-like mechanical response emerges from enhanced non-affine reconfigurations of nearly-jammed contact networks. Without relying on matrix nonlinearity, we establish a design strategy that leverages non-equilibrium memory effects intrinsic to granular systems to achieve highly programmable strain-stiffening in soft composites.

### [15] [Laddering of a knitted fabric: a topology-induced failure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20580)
*Antoine Faulconnier,Laura Michel,Mokhtar Adda-Bedia,Jérôme Crassous,Audrey Steinberger*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过实验和离散元杆模拟，探究了预拉伸针织面料中"梯状脱散（laddering）"现象的力学机制，揭示了张力阈值对脱散起始与停止的控制作用，以及脱散速度与面料张力的线性关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 梯状脱散是针织面料中因断线或脱针导致的结构缺陷传播现象，日常生活中如连裤袜损坏虽属小问题，但在工业规模生产中可能造成严重损失。研究此现象可为限制和减轻结构化材料损伤提供新思路。

Method: 采用实验和离散元杆（Discrete Element Rod）模拟相结合的方法，研究预拉伸模型针织物的梯状脱散过程。主要控制参数为施加在面料上的初始张力。

Result: 研究发现了由线圈自然曲率决定的力阈值，该阈值控制着脱散的起始和停止，因为脱散增长释放的纱线长度会松弛张力，使得在中等张力下可预测损伤。此外，脱散速度与弯曲波速度同量级，且与面料张力呈意外的线性比例关系，这源于弹性和摩擦力的复杂组合。

Conclusion: 研究结果从损伤控制和减轻的角度讨论了其意义，为理解针织材料中缺陷传播机制提供了新见解，可能启发限制结构化材料损伤的新解决方案。

Abstract: Laddering is the propagation of a topological defect in an everyday-life material: weft knitted fabrics, following a broken thread or a dropped stitch. What is a minor frustration when damaging a pair of tights is a more serious issue for industrial-scale production, but might inspire new solutions to limit and mitigate damage to architected materials. In this work, laddering is investigated in a pre-stressed model knit through experiments and Discrete Element Rod simulations. The control parameter is the initial tension applied on the fabric. A force threshold due to the stitch's natural curvature is evidenced. It controls both the propagation onset and arrest, as tension is relaxed by the thread length freed by ladder growth, and enables damage prediction at moderate tension. Furthermore, we uncovered that the laddering velocity is of the order of the velocity of bending waves and exhibits an unexpected linear scaling with the fabric tension, that arises from a complex combination of elastic and friction forces. Finally, we discuss the implications of our results from the perspective of damage control and mitigation.

</details>


### [16] [Flow-history-dependent orientational relaxation in dilute polydisperse colloidal rod suspensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20678)
*Yuto Yokoyama,Vincenzo Calabrese,Fabian Hillebrand,Henry J. London,Simon J. Haward,Amy Q. Shen*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了多分散棒状胶体悬浮液中，预剪切速率如何通过改变不同长度颗粒的取向分布来调控取向弛豫动力学，表明取向弛豫时间不再是材料常数，而是由流动条件和多分散性共同决定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多分散悬浮液中不同长度颗粒具有不同的旋转扩散时间尺度，但多分散性如何影响流动停止后的取向弛豫动力学尚不明确，特别是预剪切速率如何决定后续取向弛豫动力学缺乏深入理解。

Method: 在窄间隙泰勒-库埃特（Taylor-Couette）池中对稀纤维素纳米晶体（CNC）悬浮液进行简单剪切，使用高速偏振成像测量流动停止后的双折射弛豫；建立参数化为测量长度分布的多分散福克-普朗克（Fokker-Planck）模型来解释实验结果。

Result: 平均取向弛豫时间随预剪切速率增加而系统性减小；当基于加权平均棒长度的旋转扩散系数组织佩克莱数（Péclet number）时，数据在宽剪切速率范围内与理论吻合良好；这种趋势源于随着预剪切速率增加，对取向贡献最大的棒子亚群从较长棒向较短棒转移。

Conclusion: 在多分散系统中，取向弛豫时间不再是材料特定常数，而是由流动条件和多分散性共同决定；该研究为理解多分散棒悬浮液的取向动力学和解释流变光学测量提供了定量框架。

Abstract: Orientation and relaxation dynamics of rod-like colloids under flow govern the optical and mechanical properties of many emerging soft materials. In polydisperse suspensions, particles of different lengths exhibit distinct rotational diffusion timescales, yet how this polydispersity influences relaxation following flow cessation remains unclear. In particular, it is not well understood how the pre-shear rate determines the subsequent orientation relaxation dynamics. To address this question, we performed simple shear on dilute cellulose nanocrystal (CNC) suspensions in a narrow-gap Taylor-Couette cell and measured birefringence relaxation after flow cessation using high-speed polarization imaging. To interpret the experiments, we formulated a polydisperse Fokker-Planck model parameterized by the measured length distribution. As a result, the average orientation relaxation time systematically decreases with increasing pre-shear rate. Moreover, when organized by the Péclet number based on the rotational diffusion coefficient of the weighted average rod length, the data agree well with the theory over a wide range of shear rates. This trend arises because the rod sub-population contributing most strongly to the orientation shifts from longer rods to shorter rods as the pre-shear rate increases, showing that the flow history governs the orientation relaxation dynamics. In polydisperse systems, the orientation relaxation time is no longer a material-specific constant but is determined by both the flow conditions and the polydispersity. This study provides a quantitative framework for understanding orientation dynamics in polydisperse rod suspensions and for interpreting rheo-optical measurements.

</details>

### [17] [Purely Quadratic Non-Gaussianity from Tachyonic Instability: Primordial Black Holes and Scalar-Induced Gravitational Waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20063)
*He-Xu Zhang,Mei Huang*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了在多组分暴胀模型中由快子不稳定性产生的纯二次非高斯曲率扰动下的原初黑洞形成。研究发现原初黑洞丰度对扰动振幅和相关系数ρ均呈指数敏感，且谱宽在避免原初黑洞过度产生中起决定性作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索多组分暴胀模型中由快子不稳定性（tachyonic instability）产生的纯二次非高斯性（purely quadratic non-Gaussianity）对原初黑洞（primordial black hole, PBH）形成的影响。特别关注如何避免原初黑洞过度产生，同时保持可观测的引力波信号。

Method: 采用基于致密函数（compaction function）的扩展Press-Schechter框架，推导了线性致密函数的概率分布及其渐近指数尾部。该方法特别关注平滑场与其径向梯度之间的相关系数ρ对原初黑洞丰度的影响。

Result: 研究发现原初黑洞丰度不仅对扰动振幅呈指数敏感，还对相关系数ρ呈指数敏感。对于A<0的情况，曲率功率谱的谱宽起决定性作用：宽谱产生轻度负ρ值，无法抑制原初黑洞形成；而足够窄的谱使ρ→-1，导致指数抑制同时保持显著的引力波信号。

Conclusion: 热暴胀（thermal inflation）作为基准情景可产生小行星质量的原初黑洞暗物质和高频标量诱导引力波，但其典型宽谱特性使其难以同时满足脉冲星计时阵列观测和原初黑洞约束。谱宽控制是协调原初黑洞形成与引力波信号的关键因素。

Abstract: We investigate primordial black hole (PBH) formation in a cosmological scenario where curvature perturbations follow purely quadratic non-Gaussianity, $ζ= A(φ^2-\langleφ^2\rangle)$, arising from tachyonic instability in multi-component inflationary models. Within an extended Press-Schechter framework based on the compaction function, we derive the probability distribution of the linear compaction function and its asymptotic exponential tail, demonstrating that PBH abundance is exponentially sensitive not only to the amplitude of perturbations but also to the correlation coefficient $ρ$ between the smoothed field and its radial gradient. We further find that, for $A<0$, the spectral width of the curvature power spectrum plays a decisive role in avoiding PBH overproduction: broad spectra yield mildly negative $ρ$ and fail to suppress PBH formation, while sufficiently narrow spectra drive $ρ\to -1$, resulting in an exponential suppression while maintaining a sizable gravitational-wave signal. Thermal inflation provides a useful benchmark scenario with asteroid-mass PBH dark matter and high-frequency scalar-induced gravitational waves potentially detectable by future space-based interferometers, but its typically broad spectra make it challenging to reconcile PTA observations with PBH constraints.

</details>

### [18] [Topological Edge States Emerging from Twisted Moiré Bands](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19929)
*Yasser Saleem,Paweł Potasz,Anna Dyrdał,Björn Trauzettel,Ewelina M. Hankiewicz*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种在连续介质框架中处理有限几何结构的方法，用于分析扭曲双层WSe₂的边界物理，克服了动量空间表述和万尼尔阻塞的限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在克服传统动量空间表述和万尼尔阻塞（Wannier obstructions）在处理扭曲双层WSe₂有限几何结构时的局限性，为拓扑莫尔材料的边界物理提供更有效的分析框架。

Method: 通过将限制势（confinement potential）投影到体莫尔本征态上，在连续介质框架内直接处理有限几何结构，实现了无需晶格模型（lattice models）的真实空间边界物理描述。

Result: 在纳米带（nanoribbons）中观察到与体陈数（bulk Chern numbers）一致的螺旋边缘模式（chiral edge modes），这些模式在魔角区域（magic-angle regime）表现出强局域化、层极化反向传播模式（layer-polarized counter-propagating modes）和电可调性。

Conclusion: 该方法为拓扑莫尔材料（topological moiré materials）的边界物理建立了一个通用框架，能够控制局域化、杂化和拓扑转变（topological transitions）。

Abstract: We study twisted bilayer WSe$_2$ within a continuum moiré model and introduce a method for treating finite geometries directly in the continuum framework, overcoming limitations associated with momentum-space formulations and Wannier obstructions. By projecting a confinement potential onto bulk moiré eigenstates, we obtain a real-space description of edge physics without lattice models. Applying this approach to nanoribbons, we demonstrate chiral edge modes consistent with bulk Chern numbers and reveal their moiré-scale character. In the magic-angle regime, these states are strongly localized, exhibit layer-polarized counter-propagating modes, and are electrically tunable via a displacement field, enabling control of localization, hybridization, and topological transitions. Our results establish a general framework for boundary physics in topological moiré materials.

### [19] [Probing bilayer topological order with layer-resolved transport](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19955)
*Hongquan Liu,J. I. A. Li,D. E. Feldman*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种通过层分辨或自旋分辨噪声（layer-resolved or spin-resolved noise）来探测多组分系统中带电与中性任意子（anyons）统计性质的新协议，克服了仅通过散粒噪声（shot noise）测量分数电荷对统计性质约束不足的局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 散粒噪声可用于测量任意子的分数电荷，但电荷值仅对分数统计施加约束而不能完全确定统计性质。这一问题在多组分系统中尤为重要，例如双层石墨烯中的中性任意子电荷为零，无法提供其统计性质的信息。

Method: 提出一种基于层分辨或自旋分辨噪声的协议，利用统计性质与任意子电荷在各组分间分布的关系来探测统计性质。该方法还可通过测量霍尔条（Hall bar）中窄收缩区的层分辨电流来提取统计信息，即使在存在长程相互作用和其他非普适效应时也适用。

Result: 该协议适用于多种系统：MoTe₂中的分数量子自旋霍尔效应（fractional quantum spin Hall effect）、多层石墨烯和双层GaAs中的拓扑态，以及双层石墨烯中新发现的分数激子（fractional excitons）。

Conclusion: 该方法提供了一种探测多组分系统中任意子统计性质的有效途径，特别是对于中性任意子，克服了传统散粒噪声测量的局限性，为理解复杂系统中的分数统计提供了新工具。

Abstract: Shot noise has been used to measure fractional charges of anyons. The value of the charge imposes constraints on fractional statistics but does not determine it. This issue is particularly important in multi-component systems. For example, the zero charge of neutral anyons in bilayer graphene gives no information about their statistics at all. We propose a protocol to probe the statistics of charged and neutral anyons in multi-component systems with layer-resolved or spin-resolved noise. The protocol applies to the fractional quantum spin Hall effect in MoTe$_2$, topological states in multi-layer graphene and bilayer GaAs, and to recently discovered fractional excitons in bilayer graphene. The approach relies on the relation between statistics and the distribution of the anyon charge over the components. Information about statistics can also be extracted from a simpler measurement of the layer-resolved electric current through a narrow constriction in a Hall bar even in the presence of long-range interactions and other non-universal effects.

</details>


### [20] [Transverse thermophotovoltaics from nonreciprocal plasmon drag in metal](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20068)
*Dingwei He,Gaomin Tang*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究为横向热光伏效应建立了微观理论框架，通过非互易表面等离子体激元驱动的近场热辐射，在二维金属片中产生横向电流，为纳米尺度热能转换提供了理论基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 横向热光伏（transverse thermophotovoltaics）作为一种区别于传统结型光伏的新范式，此前缺乏理论支撑。本研究旨在为该效应建立微观理论框架，阐明其物理机制。

Method: 建立了包含电子-光子相互作用的微观形式体系，整合了由能量-动量守恒决定的电子跃迁因子、编码非互易表面模式的通量因子及其定向耦合。该方法定量验证了等离子体拖曳（plasmon-drag）机制。

Result: 理论形式体系揭示了在二维金属片中，通过近场热辐射驱动的非互易表面等离子体激元（nonreciprocal surface plasmon polaritons）产生横向电流的机制，并阐明了杂质散射（impurity scattering）的作用。

Conclusion: 该工作为横向热光伏器件提供了严格的理论基础，为主动纳米尺度热能转换开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Transverse thermophotovoltaics has been conceptually proposed as a paradigm distinct from conventional junction-based photovoltaics, but has so far lacked a theoretical foundation. In this Letter, we establish a microscopic formalism of this effect in which a transverse electric current emerges in a two-dimensional metal sheet via nonreciprocal surface plasmon polaritons driven by near-field thermal radiation. This theoretical formalism incorporates the electron-photon interaction by integrating electronic transition factor governed by energy-momentum conservation, the photon flux factor encoding the nonreciprocal surface modes, and their directional coupling. Our approach quantitatively confirms the plasmon-drag mechanism and reveals the role of impurity scattering. This work provides a rigorous theoretical foundation for transverse thermophotovoltaic devices and opens avenues for active nanoscale thermal energy conversion.

</details>


### [21] [Light-Induced Topological Phase Transitions and Anomalous Thermal Transport in d-Wave Altermagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20164)
*Ayesha Maryam,Muzamil Shah,Kashif Sabeeh,Reza Asgari*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了二维d波交变磁拓扑绝缘体（two-dimensional d wave altermagnetic topological insulator）在光驱动下的本征热输运和Floquet工程拓扑性质，揭示了线性偏振光如何诱导自旋选择性拓扑相变，并建立了热输运作为探测交变磁序的敏感探针。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索超越传统磁系统的全光调控拓扑和热电子响应（caloritronic responses）路径，并建立热输运作为探测交变磁序（altermagnetic order）的敏感探针。关注线性偏振光在交变磁体中如何打破自旋扇区间的对称性连接。

Method: 通过分析计算高频有效哈密顿量（high-frequency effective Hamiltonian），推导了贝里曲率（Berry curvature）的闭式表达式。研究了反常霍尔、能斯特（Nernst）和热霍尔电导率及其自旋分辨等效量，重点关注线性偏振光对二维d波交变磁拓扑绝缘体的影响。

Result: 线性偏振光在交变磁体中诱导了一系列自旋选择性拓扑相变：从量子自旋霍尔态（quantum spin Hall state）到自旋极化陈绝缘体（spin-polarized Chern insulator），最终到平庸相。能斯特响应显示显著的热激活和对陈数区域能隙大小的敏感性，而电和热霍尔响应均量子化并满足反常维德曼-弗朗兹定律（anomalous Wiedemann Franz law）。所有反常输运系数均表现出独特的d波偏振角依赖性。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明了超越传统磁系统的全光调控拓扑和热电子响应的可行路径，并确立了热输运作为探测交变磁序的敏感探针。交变磁体中的反常输运系数具有独特的d波偏振角依赖性，在正交旋转下反转符号并在对称性恢复方向消失。

Abstract: We study intrinsic thermal transport and Floquet-engineered topology in a two-dimensional d wave altermagnetic topological insulator powered by linearly polarized light. We analyze the anomalous Hall, Nernst, and thermal Hall conductivities, as well as their spin-resolved equivalents, and develop closed-form formulas for the Berry curvature using an analytically calculated high-frequency effective Hamiltonian. We demonstrate that linearly polarized light, in contrast to conventional antiferromagnets, breaks the symmetry connecting spin sectors in altermagnets, allowing a series of spin-selective topological phase transitions from a quantum spin Hall state to a spin-polarized Chern insulator and finally to a trivial phase. The Nernst response shows substantial thermal activation and significant sensitivity to the gap size in the Chern domain, but both the electrical and thermal Hall responses become quantized and meet the anomalous Wiedemann Franz law. Every anomalous transport coefficient exhibits a distinctive d wave dependence on the polarization angle, reversing sign under orthogonal rotation and vanishing at symmetry-restoring directions. Our findings show a path to all-optical regulation of topological and caloritronic responses beyond traditional magnetic systems and establish thermal transport as a sensitive probe of altermagnetic order.

</details>


### [22] [N-fold topological mode replication in hierarchical honeycomb lattices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20198)
*Keita Funayama,Kenichi Yatsugi,Hideo Iizuka*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种通过频率域复制基本拓扑模式来设计可扩展多带拓扑态的一般原理，在微机电平台上实现了多通道拓扑波导器件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多带拓扑态（multi-band topological states）虽能在多种物理平台实现稳健的波操控，但传统方法依赖具有复杂空间分布的高频模式，这些模式的脆弱对称性和赝自旋杂化限制了稳健拓扑态的实现。

Method: 提出一种通用设计原理：通过引入分层谐振器作为内部自由度到量子自旋霍尔晶格中，在频率域复制稳健的基本拓扑模式（fundamental topological mode）。该方法使多个拓扑态按分层级别离散出现，同时保持宿主晶格基本模式的空间分布。

Result: 在多功能微机电平台（microelectromechanical platform）上实现该设计原理，实验证明基本拓扑模式和复制的拓扑模式可在单个波导中同时传播，同时抑制相互串扰（cross-talk）。

Conclusion: 拓扑复制（topology replication）被确立为设计多带拓扑系统的通用策略，为多通道拓扑波器件开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Multi-band topological states enable robust and versatile wave manipulation across a variety of physical platforms. However, the emergence of multi-band topological states has relied on higher-frequency modes with complex spatial profiles, which constrains the realization of robust topological states due to fragile symmetry and pseudospin hybridization in these modes. Here, we show a general design principle for scalable multi-band topological states by replicating a robust fundamental topological mode in the frequency domain. By introducing hierarchical resonators as an internal degree of freedom into a quantum spin Hall-based lattice, multiple topological states emerge discretely in correspondence with the hierarchical levels while preserving the spatial profile of the fundamental mode at the host lattice. Implementing this design principle in a versatile microelectromechanical platform, we experimentally demonstrate that the fundamental and replicated topological modes propagate simultaneously in a single waveguide while suppressing mutual cross-talk. Our results establish topology replication as a universal strategy for designing multi-band topological systems and open routes toward multi-channel topological wave devices.

</details>


### [23] [Distinguishing and Separating In-Plane Hall Responses](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20227)
*Soumya Sankar,Xingkai Cheng,Junwei Liu,Berthold Jäck*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种通用框架，通过区分不同物理机制对平面内磁场霍尔效应的贡献来解决测量信号解释的模糊性问题，并以铁磁外尔半金属Fe3Sn为例进行了验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 平面内磁场产生的电霍尔效应因其在拓扑电子态中的内在起源和磁场传感的潜在应用而受到关注。然而，实际测量的横向电压通常包含各向异性和贝里曲率效应等多种现象的贡献，导致测量信号解释存在模糊性。

Method: 本研究引入了一个通用框架，通过不同物理机制在磁场反转对称性和角度依赖性上的差异来区分它们的贡献。采用12端霍尔棒结构独立控制电场和平面内磁场方向，并以铁磁外尔半金属Fe3Sn在平面内几何结构中的横向电压测量为例验证该方法。

Result: 通过分析Fe3Sn的测量数据，成功区分了不同物理机制对平面内霍尔响应的贡献。该方法为理解复杂材料系统中的霍尔效应提供了标准化的分析工具。

Conclusion: 本研究提出的标准化方法将指导未来对磁性和拓扑材料中平面内霍尔响应的研究，为解决测量信号解释的模糊性问题提供了通用框架。

Abstract: Electric Hall effects generated by an in-plane magnetic field have recently gained attention owing to their intrinsic origin in topological electronic states and potential application in magnetic field sensing. In pratice, the measured transverse electric voltage typically combines contributions from multiple phenomena, such as anisotropy and Berry curvature effects, leading to interpretative ambiguities of the measurement signal. Here, we introduce a universal framework that disentangles these contributions via their distinct field-reversal symmetries and angular dependencies. Leveraging a 12-terminal Hall bar for independent control of the electric and in-plane magnetic field directions, we exemplify this method by analyzing the transverse electric voltage recorded on the the ferromagnetic Weyl semimetal Fe3Sn in an in-plane geometry. The standardized approach presented in this work will guide future studies of in-plane Hall responses in magnetic and topological materials.

</details>


### [24] [Intrinsic Magnetoelectric Hall Effect from Layer-Orbital Quantum Geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20249)
*Sunit Das,Amit Agarwal*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了层状材料中电场和磁场共同作用下产生的本征磁电霍尔效应（intrinsic magnetoelectric Hall effect），该效应源于场修饰布洛赫态中混合层-轨道量子几何（mixed layer-orbital quantum geometry）的贡献。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统本征霍尔效应（如反常霍尔效应）源于布洛赫态的轨道量子几何。然而，在层状材料中，面外电场和磁场的联合作用会耦合层极化和轨道矩，从而在场修饰的布洛赫态中产生新的混合层-轨道量子几何。研究旨在探索这种几何结构是否能产生新的输运效应。

Method: 研究通过理论分析，揭示了电场和磁场双线性耦合下，由层极化和轨道矩相关的带间相干性（interband coherence）所导致的霍尔响应。进行了对称性分析以识别能承载该效应的层状材料类别，并以菱面体五层石墨烯（rhombohedral pentalayer graphene）作为代表性体系进行具体计算演示。

Result: 该混合量子几何产生了一种本征磁电霍尔效应，其响应与散射时间无关，且可在无自旋轨道耦合的非磁性系统中出现。霍尔系数在栅极反转下呈奇对称性，并追踪层极化。在菱面体五层石墨烯中，电导率可达约 $0.05\,e^2/h$ 的量级。

Conclusion: 研究确立了混合层-轨道量子几何作为一种本征磁电霍尔输运的新机制，并证明该效应可作为布洛赫能带中层分辨量子几何（layer-resolved quantum geometry）的直接探针。

Abstract: Intrinsic Hall effects, such as the anomalous Hall effect, originate from the orbital quantum geometry of Bloch states. However, in layered materials, the combined action of out-of-plane electric and magnetic fields couples to layer polarization and orbital moment, generating a mixed layer-orbital quantum geometry in field-dressed Bloch states. We show that this geometry produces an intrinsic magnetoelectric Hall effect that is bilinear in the electric and magnetic fields. The response is scattering-time independent and can arise in nonmagnetic systems without spin-orbit coupling. Its origin lies in interband coherence involving layer polarization and orbital moment, leading to a finite, non-quantized Hall response that persists in the band gap. The Hall coefficient is odd under gate reversal and tracks layer polarization. A symmetry analysis identifies the classes of layered materials that host this effect. As a representative realization, we demonstrate the effect in rhombohedral pentalayer graphene, where the conductivity reaches values of order $0.05\,e^2/h$. These results establish mixed layer-orbital quantum geometry as a mechanism for intrinsic magnetoelectric Hall transport and a direct probe of layer-resolved quantum geometry in Bloch bands.

</details>


### [25] [Acoustic quantum skyrmion-valley Hall effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20271)
*Lei Liu,Xiujuan Zhang,Ming-Hui Lu,Yan-Feng Chen*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究在表面声子晶体中实验实现了声学量子斯格明子-谷霍尔效应，通过工程化的自旋-轨道-动量相互作用，使斯格明子作为谷锁定的拓扑边缘态沿设计域壁稳健传播。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 斯格明子（skyrmions）作为类粒子的拓扑纹理结构在低功耗电子学和波基功能方面具有巨大潜力，但其实际应用受到缺乏稳健且可控传输的限制。研究旨在探索如何利用能带拓扑来克服这一局限性。

Method: 通过工程化的自旋-轨道-动量相互作用（spin-orbit-momentum interaction），在表面声子晶体（surface phononic crystal）中实验实现了声学量子斯格明子-谷霍尔效应（acoustic quantum skyrmion-valley Hall effect）。斯格明子作为谷锁定的拓扑边缘态（valley-locked topological edge states）沿设计的域壁（domain walls）传播。

Result: 斯格明子传输表现出同时的轨道角动量-谷锁定（OAM-valley locking）和自旋-纹理锁定（spin-texture locking），通过选择性激发实现了可控传播。研究建立了实空间与动量空间拓扑之间的直接对应关系。

Conclusion: 该研究为稳健、可控的斯格明子传输提供了一种通用策略，通过能带拓扑实现了对斯格明子传输的有效控制，克服了传统传输方法的局限性。

Abstract: Skyrmions are particle-like topological textures that hold great promise for low-power electronics and wave-based functionalities. Yet their utility is hindered by the lack of robust and controllable transport. Here, we show that band topology can be harnessed to overcome this limitation. We experimentally realize an acoustic quantum skyrmion--valley Hall effect in a surface phononic crystal via engineered spin--orbit--momentum interaction. Skyrmions emerge as valley-locked topological edge states, robustly propagating along designed domain walls. Crucially, the skyrmion transport exhibits concurrent orbital angular momentum (OAM)--valley locking and spin--texture locking, enabling controllable propagation through selective excitation. Our results establish a direct correspondence between real-space and momentum-space topology, providing a general strategy for robust, controllable skyrmion transport.

</details>


### [26] [Symplectic connection third-order Hall effect in a room-temperature ferromagnet](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20356)
*Yu Cao,Xukun Feng,Yiming Guo,Huiying Liu,Qia Shen,Hongliang Chen,Wanxi Gong,Yu Yang,Dandan Guan,Yaoyi Li,Shiyong Wang,Hao Zheng,Canhua Liu,Xiaoxue Liu,Yumeng Yang,Xuepeng Qiu,Ruidan Zhong,Jinfeng Jia,Shengyuan A. Yang,Cong Xiao,Liang Liu*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究在室温范德华铁磁体Fe3GaTe2中发现了由二阶贝里联络极化率（second-order Berry connection polarizability）引发的新型三阶非线性霍尔效应（third-order nonlinear Hall effects），揭示了超越贝里曲率和量子度量的高阶量子几何特性——辛联络（symplectic connection）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 三阶非线性霍尔效应（THE）作为探索量子材料中量子几何性质的有力探针，近期引起了广泛实验关注。然而，现有研究主要关注量子度量的四极矩和贝里曲率，需要探索更高阶的量子几何特性表征方法。

Method: 研究采用实验观测与第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）相结合的方法。通过测量Fe3GaTe2的三阶横向响应，结合标度律分析（scaling law analysis）和理论计算，建立了辛联络诱导的非线性霍尔效应机制。

Result: 实验发现Fe3GaTe2中的三阶横向响应具有磁化奇对称性（odd to magnetization），在居里温度（Curie temperature）以上消失，且与驱动电流方向无关。标度律分析和第一性原理计算证实该响应为辛联络诱导的三阶非线性霍尔效应。

Conclusion: 该发现为通过非线性输运探测超越贝里曲率和量子度量的高阶量子几何性质开辟了新途径，揭示了在不破坏反演对称性的广泛磁体中探索非线性霍尔现象的潜力。室温可操控性为基于量子几何联络结构的器件应用提供了前景。

Abstract: Third-order nonlinear Hall effects (THE) have recently attracted considerable experimental interest as powerful probes for quantum geometric properties in emergent quantum materials, encompassing quadrupole moments of quantum metric and Berry curvature. Here, we report a fundamentally new THE in room-temperature van der Waals ferromagnet Fe3GaTe2 from second-order Berry connection polarizability, which manifests a higher-order characterization of band geometry called symplectic connection. Our observations show that the third-order transverse response in Fe3GaTe2 is odd to magnetization, vanishes above the Curie temperature and remains independent of driving current directions. Scaling law analysis combined with first-principles calculations establishes this response as the symplectic-connection-induced THE. This discovery opens the door to probing high-order quantum geometric properties beyond Berry curvature and quantum metric through nonlinear transport, unveiling the potential of exploring nonlinear Hall phenomena in broad classes of magnets without breaking inversion symmetry. Moreover, the room-temperature manipulation of THE holds promises for device applications based on harnessing the quantum-geometric connection structure.

</details>


### [27] [Quantum Optical Signatures of Band Topology in Solid-State High Harmonics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20388)
*Denis Ilin,Alexander S. Solntsev,Ivan Iorsh*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究建立了固态系统中高次谐波产生（HHG）的通用理论，揭示了能带拓扑与光子统计之间的直接联系，为拓扑敏感的量子光产生和固态系统光谱学开辟了新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有高次谐波产生理论通常基于薛定谔方程处理光-物质动力学，无法充分描述复杂固态能带结构的混合态特性。本研究旨在发展一种能够自然捕捉场和物质混合态特征的理论框架。

Method: 采用密度矩阵演化方法，基于光子和物质自由度的弱关联展开，构建固态系统高次谐波产生的通用理论。以单边光学腔中的Su-Schrieffer-Heeger（SSH）模型作为范例系统，考虑对偶机制进行分析。

Result: 研究发现发射场的性质由底层固体的量子统计和量子几何决定。在拓扑相中，系统表现出比平庸相更强的高次谐波响应和量子光特征。腔-物质相互作用产生压缩的高次谐波量子光，其性质直接由材料系统中的电流-电流涨落决定。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了能带拓扑与光子统计之间的直接联系，为拓扑敏感的量子光产生和基于光子统计的固态系统光谱学开辟了新途径。研究显示相关非经典效应由材料复极化率编码的电流-电流涨落主导，而非单独的Kerr机制。

Abstract: We develop a general theory of high-harmonic generation (HHG) in solid-state systems, based on a weak-correlation expansion of photonic and matter degrees of freedom. Unlike standard HHG theories, which treat light-matter dynamics through the Schrodinger equation, our approach employs density-matrix evolution, naturally capturing the mixed-state character of both the field and the matter - a critical aspect for describing complex solid-state band structures. We show explicitly that the properties of the emitted fields are governed by the quantum statistics and quantum geometry of the underlying solid. Taking the Su-Schrieffer-Heeger (SSH) model in a one-sided optical cavity as a paradigmatic example and considering the dual regime, we demonstrate that in the topological phase a system exhibits a stronger HHG response and stronger quantum-light signatures than in the trivial phase. Furthermore, we show that cavity-matter interaction gives rise to squeezed high-harmonic quantum light, whose properties are directly imprinted by the current-current fluctuations in the material system. Crucially, the observed squeezing does not rely on a separate quartic Kerr mechanism. In the mesoscopic regime, the genuine quantum Kerr term is higher order in light-matter coupling strength and negligible, while the relevant non-classical effect is governed by current-current fluctuations encoded in the complex susceptibility of the material. This work establishes a direct link between band topology and photon statistics, opening new avenues for topology-sensitive quantum light generation and photon statistics based spectroscopy of solid-state systems.

### [28] [Spin-wave hybridization in bismuth iron garnet Mie spheres induced by the inverse Faraday effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20479)
*Fedor Shuklin,Khristina Albitskaya,Alexander Chernov,Mihail Petrov*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究展示了利用逆法拉第效应（inverse Faraday effect）在铁磁铋铁石榴石（BIG）米氏球中调控偶极-交换自旋波谱，通过光学米氏共振产生空间结构化的有效磁场，实现具有相反宇称的磁振子模式在相同角动量分量内的杂化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索利用光学方法对磁振子（magnon）谱进行对称性选择性控制的新途径。通过结合铁磁石榴石材料的磁光特性与米氏共振（Mie resonances）的场增强效应，为自旋波谱工程提供可调控的平台。

Method: 采用耦合模理论（coupled-mode theory）推导了避免交叉谱（avoided-crossing spectrum）和能级分裂的解析表达式。对BIG球体进行数值计算，验证了预测的杂化现象，并分析了阻尼、线宽和热效应的影响。

Result: 研究显示，在圆偏振光与平衡磁化共线入射时，光学微扰保持轴向对称性但破坏镜像宇称，使相同角动量分量内具有相反宇称的磁振子模式发生杂化。能级分裂与泵浦强度呈线性关系，在光学米氏共振附近达到最大值。

Conclusion: BIG米氏谐振器被确认为实现自旋波谱对称性选择性光学控制的有前景平台。预测的MHz至数百MHz量级的能级分裂在实际条件下应可观测，为磁振子谱工程提供了新的光学调控机制。

Abstract: We show that the inverse Faraday effect can be used to engineer dipole--exchange spin-wave spectra in ferrimagnetic bismuth iron garnet (BIG) Mie spheres. Internal optical Mie resonances generate spatially structured effective magnetic fields whose symmetry is inherited from the optical near field and which act as controllable perturbations of the magnon Hamiltonian. For circularly polarized light incident collinearly with the equilibrium magnetization, the optical perturbation preserves axial symmetry while breaking mirror parity, thereby enabling hybridization of magnon modes with opposite parity within the same $\widehat{J}_z$ sector. Using coupled-mode theory, we derive the corresponding avoided-crossing spectrum and analytical expressions for the induced level splittings, which scale linearly with pump intensity. Numerical calculations for BIG spheres confirm the predicted hybridization and show that the splitting is maximized near optical Mie resonances, where field enhancement and magneto-optical response are strongest. We further discuss the roles of damping, linewidth, and heating, and show that the predicted MHz--hundreds-of-MHz splittings should be observable under realistic conditions. These results identify BIG Mie resonators as a promising platform for symmetry-selective optical control of spin-wave spectra.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统低能近似方法无法充分捕捉flopping-mode自旋量子比特中双阱约束的空间特性和电磁环境，需要开发更精确的建模框架来直接关联器件几何结构与量子比特性能参数。

Method: 提出半解析微观建模框架，通过直接映射器件几何结构到量子比特参数，模拟基于电偶极自旋共振的单量子比特控制，并评估不同参数区域下Rabi振荡的频率和谱纯度。

Result: 分析揭示了快速电驱动与干净单模Rabi振荡之间的基本权衡；通过考虑两个电容耦合的flopping-mode量子比特，推导了相应的交换相互作用，揭示了双阱约束空间分布、磁场梯度和库仑相互作用之间的相互影响。

Abstract: We present a semi-analytical microscopic modeling framework for flopping-mode spin qubits, with which we capture the spatial properties of their double-well confinement and electromagnetic environment beyond conventional low-energy approximations. Our framework enables a direct mapping from the device geometry to qubit parameters and metrics. By using this approach, we simulate electric dipole spin resonance-based single-qubit control and evaluate the frequency and spectral purity of the Rabi oscillations across different parameter regimes. Our analysis reveals a fundamental tradeoff between fast electrical driving and clean single-mode Rabi oscillations. We also investigate two-qubit control by considering two capacitively coupled flopping-mode qubits and derive the corresponding exchange interaction with an appropriately restricted configuration interaction treatment. Our approach reveals the interplay between the spatial profile of the double-well confinement, magnetic field gradient, and Coulomb interaction, which together govern the effective exchange coupling strength. Our microscopic modeling framework enables efficient exploration of large parameter spaces and provides design guidelines for optimizing flopping-mode spin qubits in realistic architectures. This framework can also be generalized in a straightforward manner to other electrically controlled spin qubit platforms.

### [30] [Memristive Switches in Rigid Conjugated Single-Molecule Junctions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20542)
*Riccardo Conte,Lucienne van der Geest,Minu Sheeja,Przemyslaw Gawel,Cina Foroutan-Nejad,Herre S. J. van der Zant*

TL;DR: 该研究通过机械可控断裂结技术，在缺乏明显内部开关路径的刚性OPE类衍生物分子结中观察到非易失性双稳态迟滞IV特性，并建立了定量分析流程来分类忆阻行为、聚类电导状态、提取开关特征和稳定性指标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 分子结中的电压驱动忆阻开关现象已被报道，但其微观起源通常难以确定。本研究旨在探究缺乏明显内部开关路径的刚性OPE类衍生物的忆阻行为，以揭示其微观机制。

Method: 采用机械可控断裂结技术，在低温条件下研究三种刚性OPE类衍生物分子结。引入定量分析流程，对忆阻IV曲线进行分类，聚类两种电导状态，并从固定位移下的重复测量中提取开关特征和稳定性指标。

Result: 所有分子均表现出忆阻行为，但稳定性和迟滞可重复性强烈依赖于锚定基团和连接方式：硫醇酯锚定的线性联苯骨架显示出最可重复、主要由场驱动的迟滞，而硫醚锚定的间位苯变体则主要由随机、电流驱动的事件主导。电导统计表明其起源是外部的、机械介导的，涉及接触重排、多分子输运、闪烁（开-闭）接触、注入点偏移和π-π堆积二聚化。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了分子结中观察到的忆阻行为的微观起源是外部的、机械介导的机制，而非分子内部开关路径。锚定基团和连接方式对忆阻行为的稳定性和可重复性有重要影响，硫醇酯锚定的线性联苯骨架表现出最可靠的场驱动迟滞特性。

Abstract: Voltage-driven memristive switching has been reported in molecular junctions, yet its microscopic origin often remains elusive. Here, we study three rigid OPE-like derivatives that lack an obvious internal switching pathway using mechanically controlled break junctions (MCBJs) and observe non-volatile, bistable hysteretic IV characteristics at cryogenic temperature. We introduce a quantitative analysis workflow that classifies memristive IVs, clusters the two conductance states, and extracts switching features and stability metrics from repeated measurements at fixed displacement. While all molecules exhibit memristive behavior, stability and hysteresis reproducibility depend strongly on anchoring and connectivity: the linear biphenyl backbone with thiolate (SAc) anchoring shows the most reproducible, predominantly field-driven hysteresis, whereas the meta-phenyl variant with thioether (SMe) anchoring is dominated by stochastic, current-driven events. The resulting conductance statistics point to an extrinsic, mechanically mediated origin involving contact rearrangements, multi-molecule transport, blinking (open-closed) contacts, injection-point shifts, and $π$-$π$-stacking dimerization.

### [31] [Disorder induced time-reversal-odd nonlinear spin and orbital Hall effects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20592)
*Ruda Guo,Yi Liu,Cong Xiao,Zhe Yuan*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究发展了二阶时间反演奇（$\mathcal{T}$-odd）角动量电流理论，揭示了其来源包括自旋和轨道贝里曲率偶极子以及多种无序诱导机制，并发现轨道分量可与自旋分量相当甚至更大。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前研究旨在建立二阶时间反演奇（$\mathcal{T}$-odd）角动量电流的完整理论框架，该框架需要同时包含自旋和轨道分量，并系统探究其微观起源。

Method: 研究发展了一个理论框架，将自旋和轨道分量统一纳入二阶时间反演奇角动量电流的描述，并推导了区分不同贡献的一般标度关系（scaling relation）。通过模型计算验证理论预测。

Result: 研究发现$\mathcal{T}$-odd非线性角动量电流不仅源于自旋和轨道贝里曲率偶极子（Berry curvature dipoles），还来自无序诱导机制，包括坐标位移（coordinate shift）、侧跳（side-jump）自旋和轨道电流、反常散射振幅（anomalous scattering amplitude）和斜散射（skew scattering）。模型计算表明轨道分量可与自旋分量相当甚至更大。

Conclusion: 该理论为$\mathcal{T}$-odd非线性自旋和轨道输运研究奠定了基础，提供了区分不同微观机制的实验指导，并强调了轨道分量在角动量输运中的重要性。

Abstract: We develop a theory for the second-order time-reversal-odd ($\mathcal{T}$-odd) angular-momentum current, incorporating both spin and orbital components. We reveal that besides spin and orbital Berry curvature dipoles, $\mathcal{T}$-odd nonlinear angular-momentum current can originate from disorder-induced mechanisms including coordinate shift, side-jump spin and orbital currents, anomalous scattering amplitude, and skew scattering. A general scaling relation is derived to help distinguish some of these contributions in experiments. Model calculations demonstrate that the orbital component can be comparable to and much larger than the spin component. Our theory lays the groundwork for $\mathcal{T}$-odd nonlinear spin and orbital transport.

</details>


### [32] [Topological Word for Non-Abelian Topological Insulators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20624)
*Zhenming Zhang,Tianyu Li,Wei Yi*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为"拓扑词（topological word）"的统一框架，用于描述多能隙非阿贝尔拓扑绝缘体中的完整非阿贝尔体边对应关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究往往忽视能带邻接信息（band-adjacency information），而这对跨多个能隙的边缘态模式至关重要。需要建立一个统一框架来同时捕捉全局非阿贝尔拓扑和能带邻接信息。

Method: 提出拓扑词框架，由有序字母序列组成，每个字母代表描述能隙分辨拓扑的非阿贝尔荷（non-Abelian charge）。该框架通过静态模型和周期驱动的Floquet系统进行验证。

Result: 拓扑词成功捕捉了对应同伦分类的全局非阿贝尔拓扑以及能带邻接信息。即使在宇称-时间对称性破缺导致全局非阿贝尔拓扑定义不明确的情况下，拓扑词仍能提供关于拓扑和边缘态的见解。

Conclusion: 拓扑词框架为多能隙非阿贝尔拓扑绝缘体提供了完整的体边对应描述，与现有描述（如相带奇点和编织表示）既有联系又有区别，即使在对称性破缺条件下仍保持有效性。

Abstract: We propose a unified framework, dubbed topological word, for the complete non-Abelian bulk-boundary correspondence in multigap non-Abelian topological insulators. Composed by an ordered sequence of letters, each a non-Abelian charge depicting the gap-resolved topology, the topological word captures both the global non-Abelian topology corresponding to the homotopy classification, and the band-adjacency information. The latter, though crucial for the edge-state pattern across multiple gaps, is often overlooked in previous studies. We confirm our framework using both static models and periodically driven Floquet systems, and discuss its connection and distinction with existing descriptions, such as the phase-band singularities and braiding representations. Intriguingly, topological word continues to provide insight regarding topology and edge states, even as the global non-Abelian topology becomes ill-defined under broken parity-time symmetry.

</details>

Abstract: This work focuses on the structure, wettability and corrosion behaviors of Ti-6Al-4V alloy after roughening treatments in different concentrations of NaOH aqueous solutions followed by low surface energy hexadecyltrimethoxysilane (HDTMS) coating. In this regard, scanning electron microscopy, contact angle measurements, potentiodynamic polarization and electrochemical impedance spectroscopy were used to characterize the samples. In contrast to hydrophilicity caused by the hydrothermal alkaline treatments, the subsequent HDTMS coating donated considerable hydrophobicity. Typically, the highest sessile water contact angle (about 147 deg) was obtained for the sample treated in 3 molar NaOH solution followed by the HDTMS coating. In addition, the alkaline treatment reduced the corrosion resistance of the surface in a NaCl aqueous solution; however, the HDTMS hydrophobization process improved it significantly. It is eventually concluded that the coupled use of alkaline treatment and HDTMS functionalization can be further considered for moisture-exposed applications of Ti-based alloys.

### [34] [Griffiths-like phase, spin-phonon coupling, and exchange-bias in the disordered double perovskite GdSrCoMnO$_{6}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19894)
*Gyanti Prakash Moharana,Diptikanta Swain,Hanuma Kumar Dara,Debendra Prasad Panda,S. N Sarangi*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究报道了无序双钙钛矿GdSrCoMnO₆的结构、磁性和拉曼研究，发现其存在铁磁转变、类Griffiths相、自旋-声子耦合、低温磁冻结和交换偏置效应，表明结构无序对磁相关性、自旋动力学和自旋-晶格响应具有重要影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究无序双钙钛矿GdSrCoMnO₆的磁性和结构性质，旨在理解混合价态Co和Mn离子的随机分布以及铁磁与反铁磁相互作用竞争所产生的磁不均匀性效应。

Method: 采用直流磁化率（DC magnetization）、交流磁化率（AC susceptibility）和拉曼光谱（Raman measurements）等多种实验技术，系统研究了材料的磁相变、自旋动力学和自旋-声子耦合现象。

Result: 观察到铁磁转变温度T_C≈153K，类Griffiths相（Griffiths-like regime）延伸至T_G≈172K；拉曼测量显示声子频率在磁有序区域偏离非谐背景，表明存在自旋-声子耦合（spin-phonon coupling）；交流磁化率揭示低于冻结温度T_f≈30K的慢磁动力学；低温下观测到交换偏置效应（exchange-bias effect），5K时交换偏置场|H_EB|=379Oe。

Conclusion: 结构无序（structural disorder）在GdSrCoMnO₆的磁相关性、自旋动力学和自旋-晶格响应中起着重要作用，这些性质源于混合价态Co和Mn离子的随机分布以及铁磁与反铁磁相互作用的竞争。

Abstract: We report structural, magnetic, and Raman studies of the disordered double perovskite GdSrCoMnO$_{6}$~(GSCM). DC magnetization shows a ferromagnetic transition at $T_{C} \approx 153$~K. The inverse susceptibility exhibits a downturn above $T_{C}$ and is consistent with a Griffiths-like regime extending up to $T_{G} \approx 172$~K. Raman measurements show a deviation of the phonon frequency from the anharmonic background near the magnetic-ordering region, consistent with spin-phonon coupling. AC susceptibility indicates slow magnetic dynamics below the freezing temperature $T_{f} \approx 30$~K. These results point to magnetic inhomogeneity generated by the random distribution of mixed-valence Co and Mn ions and by the resulting competition between ferromagnetic and antiferromagnetic interactions. In the low-temperature regime, an exchange-bias effect is observed up to 50~K, with an exchange-bias magnitude $|H_{EB}| = 379$~Oe at 5~K. Structural disorder therefore plays an important role in the magnetic correlations, spin dynamics, and spin-lattice response of GSCM.

Abstract: Mimicking the collective excitatory and inhibitory behaviors of biological neurons remains a critical challenge in the development of neuromorphic computing systems that rival the complexity and performance of the human brain. Volatile high-to-low resistance switching in insulator-to-metal transition (IMT) materials produces an abrupt increase in current flow, resembling neuronal excitation. This electrical excitation enables IMT materials to be driven into a neuron-like spiking self-oscillation regime using simple RC circuits. Here, we report a new type of self-oscillation dynamics that occurs in the opposite class of metal-to-insulator transition (MIT) materials. Electrical triggering of the MIT suppresses current flow, resembling neuronal inhibition. Method: 研究提出了一种通用机制，通过耦合磁子几何相位与铁电诱导的交换相互作用和Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya相互作用中的亚晶格不对称性。采用第一性原理计算和线性自旋波理论，在单层CuCr2Se4材料中严格验证了这一几何相位驱动机制。

Abstract: While antiferromagnetic magnons in two-dimensional (2D) materials hold immense promise for high-frequency spintronics, achieving their efficient active control remains a critical challenge. Here, we propose a universal mechanism for the nonvolatile ferroelectric (FE) switching of antiferromagnetic magnon transport in 2D multiferroic lattices. Our mechanism relies on coupling the magnon geometric phase to the FE-induced sublattice asymmetry in exchange and Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya interactions. This explicitly breaks the exact compensation of opposite-chirality magnons inherent to collinear antiferromagnets, lifting their spin degeneracy and inducing a highly tunable net Berry curvature. Crucially, reversing the FE polarization deterministically swaps these magnetic asymmetries, which completely inverts the net magnon Berry curvature and the resulting anomalous thermal Hall conductivity. Using first-principles and linear spin-wave theory, we rigorously validate this geometric-phase-driven mechanism in single-layer CuCr2Se4. Our findings establish a robust paradigm for coupling multiferroicity with the magnon geometric phase, paving the way for nonvolatile and electrically switchable antiferromagnetic magnonics.

Abstract: Field-driven phenomena, from flash sintering to electromigration, exhibit threshold fields spanning six orders of magnitude. We show their product with the onset activation coherence length is a universal critical activation voltage, Vc =0.1-2.7 V. Vc represents the threshold electrical work required to resonantly couple to the universal phonon damping peak where lattice softening is maximized. This invariant unifies macroscopic thermal instabilities with the nanoscale Blech limit, establishing a universal phenomenological law for field-lattice coupling across 17 crystal families

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 结合混合泛函第一性原理计算（hybrid-functional first-principles calculations）和线性自旋波理论（linear spin-wave theory），分析氟化铜（CuF₂）的电子结构和磁激发。

Result: 氟化铜（CuF₂）沿其d波反铁磁对称性（d-wave altermagnetic symmetry）决定的动量方向，表现出meV量级的相反手性磁振子模式劈裂。该劈裂源于异常强的长程超超交换通道（long-range super-superexchange channel）Cu-F···F-Cu，增强了控制手性模式劈裂的第七近邻交换差异（J₇b - J₇a）。

Conclusion: 钌钛矿氟化铜（rutile CuF₂）为验证钌钛矿反铁磁性提供了理想平台，并提出通过轨道能量描述（orbital-energy description）来设计绝缘反铁磁体中大的手性磁振子劈裂。

Abstract: Altermagnets host momentum-selective spin splitting and chiral-split magnonic excitations despite vanishing net magnetization, enabling spin transport without ferromagnetism. In rutile structures, establishing altermagnetism spectroscopically has been challenging, motivating the search for a rutile platform with a resolvable exchange-driven chiral magnon splitting. Here we combine hybrid-functional first-principles calculations with linear spin-wave theory to show that rutile CuF$_2$ exhibits a meV-scale splitting between magnon modes of opposite chirality along momentum directions dictated by its $d$-wave altermagnetic symmetry. The splitting originates from an anomalously strong long-range super-superexchange channel Cu--F$\cdots$F--Cu, which enhances the symmetry-allowed difference between seventh-neighbour exchanges, $J_{7b} - J_{7a}$, controlling the chiral-mode splitting. We identify an orbital-resonance mechanism: energetic alignment between Cu $3d_{z^2}$ and F $2p_z$ states strengthens virtual hopping along the Cu--F$\cdots$F--Cu path and amplifies the anisotropic long-range exchange. Rutile CuF$_2$ therefore provides an ideal platform to validate rutile altermagnetism and suggests an orbital-energy description for engineering large chiral magnon splittings in insulating altermagnets.

Abstract: As an emerging magnetic phase, altermagnets (AMs) with collinear compensated magnetism in real space and alternating spin splitting in the band structure have attracted widespread attention. Here, based on first-principles calculations, we demonstrate that the layer stacking imposes symmetry constraints on the spin and valley degrees of freedom (DOFs) in an AM bilayer composed of two tetragonal altermagnetic monolayers, thereby enabling the tuning of these DOFs through interlayer sliding as well as by an external electric field. Furthermore, owing to the tunable valley splitting induced by interlayer sliding, enhanced tunneling magnetoresistance (TMR) can be realized by AM bilayers. ### [41] [Crystal structure prediction with nuclear quantum and finite-temperature effects via deep free energy learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20230)
*Xiaoyang Wang,Yinan Wang,Wenbo Zhao,Hanyu Liu,Hao Xie,Lei Wang,Han Wang*

Method: 研究观察到自洽谐波近似（self-consistent harmonic approximation, SCHA）的自由能面作为核质心位置的函数，与势能面具有相同的数学结构，因此可以直接通过深度神经网络势能（deep neural network potential）学习。构建了深度自由能（deep free energy, DF）模型，采用两级并发学习工作流（two-level concurrent-learning workflow）。

Result: 应用于200 GPa和300 K条件下的La-Sc-H体系，基于DF的晶体结构预测成功重现了实验观测到的LaH10和LaSc2H24的稳定性，并发现了一个未报道的热力学稳定笼状氢化物：P4/mmm LaScH8。在LaH10体系上的基准测试显示，DF模型相对于DFT级别的SCHA实现了1.72×10^6倍的成本降低。

Conclusion: 深度自由能（DF）框架为将有限温度和核量子效应纳入高通量晶体结构预测提供了一条可扩展的途径，显著降低了计算成本，同时保持了预测的准确性。

Abstract: Accurate crystal structure prediction (CSP) requires accounting for finite-temperature and nuclear quantum effects, yet first-principles evaluation of the free energy surface (FES) remains prohibitive for high-throughput searches. We observe that the self-consistent harmonic approximation (SCHA) FES, as a function of nuclear centroid positions, shares the same mathematical structure as a potential-energy surface and can therefore be directly learned by a deep neural network potential. The resulting deep free energy (DF) model, constructed via a two-level concurrent-learning workflow, evaluates free energies, forces, and stresses in a single forward pass. Applied to the La-Sc-H system at 200 GPa and 300 K, DF-based CSP reproduces the stability of the experimentally observed LaH10 and LaSc2H24, and discovers an unreported thermodynamically stable clathrate hydride: P4/mmm LaScH8. Benchmarked on the LaH10 system, the DF model achieves a 1.72*10^6-fold cost reduction relative to DFT-level SSCHA. The DF framework provides a scalable route for incorporating finite-temperature and nuclear quantum effects into high-throughput crystal structure prediction.

### [42] [Domain-Wall-Mediated Ultralow-Barrier Sliding and Pinning in Ferroelectric Moiré Superlattices Revealed by Machine Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20277)
*Jia-Wen Li,Sheng Meng,Xinghua Shi,Jin Zhang,Wei-Hai Fang*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 通过机器学习分子动力学研究，揭示了滑动铁电体MoS₂莫尔超晶格中自发热驱动层间滑动的微观机制，发现滑动过程由畴壁介导的集体重构路径主导，而非刚性层平移。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 由堆叠非极性单层构建的滑动铁电体（sliding ferroelectrics）能够通过层间滑动实现面外极化和非常规切换，但其微观滑动动力学机制尚不清楚。

Method: 采用机器学习分子动力学（machine-learning molecular dynamics）方法，研究铁电MoS₂莫尔超晶格（moiré superlattices）中的层间滑动行为，并分析硫空位（sulfur vacancies）对滑动过程的影响。

Result: 在300K温度下观察到自发热驱动层间滑动，相对速度约为1 m/s；滑动表现为莫尔图案的全局漂移而非双层刚性平移；硫空位触发滑动-钉扎转变，约0.1%的硫空位即可将长程滑动转化为局域振荡。

Conclusion: 滑动过程由畴壁介导的集体重构路径（domain-wall-mediated collective reconstruction pathway）主导，具有超低能垒，这一机制普遍存在于扭曲诱导的多畴结构中，深化了对莫尔超晶格和滑动铁电体微观动力学的理解。

Abstract: Sliding ferroelectrics built from stacked nonpolar monolayers enable out-of-plane polarization and unconventional switching via interlayer sliding, yet the microscopic sliding dynamics remain unclear. Using machine-learning molecular dynamics, we reveal spontaneous thermally driven interlayer sliding in ferroelectric MoS2 moiré superlattices, with relative velocities on the order of 1 m/s at 300 K. Instead of rigid translation of the entire bilayer, the motion appears as a global drift of the moiré pattern. Such thermally driven sliding is inconsistent with the meV/atom-scale rigid-sliding barrier. In contrast, when constrained relaxation is allowed, the sliding proceeds along an almost barrierless pathway that directly reproduces the global drift of the moiré pattern. Furthermore, sulfur vacancies trigger a sliding-to-pinning transition, with about 0.1% S vacancies already sufficient to convert the long-range sliding into localized oscillations. Notably, these phenomena are not restricted to small twist angles, but arise generically in twisting-induced multidomain structures. These results reveal that the sliding process is governed by a domain-wall-mediated collective reconstruction pathway with an ultralow barrier, rather than rigid layer translation, deepening the understanding of microscopic dynamics in moiré superlattices and sliding ferroelectrics.

</details>


### [43] [LLM-guided phase diagram construction through high-throughput experimentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20304)

Abstract: Constructing phase diagrams for multicomponent alloys requires extensive experimental measurements and is a time-consuming task. Here we investigate whether large language models (LLMs) can guide experimental planning for phase diagram construction. In our framework, a general-purpose LLM serves as the experimental planner, suggesting compositions for measurement at each cycle in a closed loop with high-throughput synthesis and X-ray diffraction phase identification. Using this framework, we experimentally constructed the ternary phase diagram of the Co-Al-Ge system at 900 degree C through iterative synthesis and characterization. We compared two strategies that differ in how the initial compositions are selected: one uses predictions from a domain-specific LLM trained on phase diagram data (aLLoyM), while the other relies solely on the general-purpose LLM. The two strategies exhibited complementary strengths. aLLoyM directed the initial measurements toward compositionally complex regions in the interior of the ternary diagram, enabling the earliest discovery of all three novel phases that form only in the ternary system. In contrast, the general-purpose LLM adopted a textbook-like approach which efficiently identified a larger number of phases in fewer cycles. In addition, a simulated benchmark comparing the LLM against conventional machine learning confirmed that the LLM achieves more efficient exploration. The results demonstrate that LLMs have high potential as experimental planners for phase diagram construction.

Abstract: We introduce the use of a crossed pair of Multilayer Laue Lenses (MLLs) as an objective in Dark-Field X-ray Microscopy (DFXM). In a demonstration experiment at the ID03 beamline at ESRF, two flat Mo-Si MLLs were used, with a physical aperture of 50 x 50 $\mathrm{μm^2}$ and a focal length of 14.25 mm at 19 keV. Applying a 10 % criterion to the Modulation Transfer Functions (MTFs) acquired, a spatial resolution of 56 nm is obtained in bright-field mode -- more than three times better than with a compound refractive lens (CRL) objective. The dark-field resolution is similar. With an efficiency of 26.7 % the MLL objective expands the science domain of DFXM significantly, both for bulk and near-surface studies. Similar to the CRL case, the reciprocal space resolution is dominated by the numerical aperture (NA) of the objective, with the NA being three times larger in the MLL case. This enables faster orientation mapping and implies improved options for the use of tomographic reconstruction algorithms. Although the MLL objective pupil varies with energy and position, secondary peaks are suppressed, simplifying both interpretation and forward simulations. ### [45] [Fluctuation-driven multi-step charge density wave transition in monolayer TiSe$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20355)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用基于第一性原理训练的机器学习原子间势能（machine-learning interatomic potential），驱动大规模分子动力学（molecular dynamics）模拟，研究单层TiSe₂的有限温度结构动力学。

Result: CDW熔化偏离传统二阶相变，呈现两步熔化过程：在T*≈200K和T_CDW≈250K之间存在扩展的涨落区域，伴随拓扑缺陷（topological defects）和畴壁（domain walls）增殖，以及完全过阻尼的软光学声子（soft optical phonon）。各向异性长波长热涨落自发稳定了具有C2对称性的非对称3Q手性CDW序。

Abstract: The exact microscopic origin, symmetry, and thermal melting mechanism of the charge density wave (CDW) phase in TiSe$_{2}$ remain a subject of intense debate, particularly regarding the presence of chiral structural order and a multi-step phase transition. Here, we resolve the finite-temperature structural dynamics of the monolayer TiSe$_{2}$ using large-scale molecular dynamics simulations driven by an accurate, first-principles-trained machine-learning interatomic potential. We demonstrate that the CDW melting deviates from a conventional second-order phase transition, while it undergoes a two-step melting process characterised by an extended fluctuation regime between $T^{\ast}\approx200$ K and $T_{\mathrm{CDW}}\approx250$ K, with proliferation of topological defects and domain walls, and accompanied by a completely overdamped soft optical phonon. Furthermore, we reveal that anisotropic long-wavelength thermal fluctuations spontaneously stabilise an asymmetric $3Q$ chiral CDW order with $C2$ symmetry. These findings provide a unified microscopic framework for understanding complex fluctuation-driven phase transitions in 2D quantum materials, demonstrating that the intricate CDW physics of TiSe$_{2}$ can be largely captured without invoking excitonic correlations.

Abstract: The discovery of higher-order topological insulator (HOTI) has established a new paradigm for understanding symmetry-constrained boundary electronic states. Here, based on first-principles calculations, we demonstrate the emergence of HOTI phase in organic lattices of two-dimensional azulenoid-kekulene-type carbon allotropes, namely AKC-[3,3] and AKC-[6,0]. Enabled by the $C_6$ rotational symmetry, the nontrivial bulk topology is confirmed through the topological invariant and fractionally quantized corner charge, giving $\{[M^{(I)}_{2}],[K^{(3)}_{2}]\}$ = $\{0,2\}$ and $Q_{\mathrm{corner}} = e/3$, respectively, accompanied by the emergence of exotic corner states in nanoflakes.   <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 发现晶界处存在大热梯度，热导率变化源于电荷重新分布和主体材料键强度调制，而非现有锂振子力学理论（lithium rattler mechanics）。插层驱动的内部加热事件导致局部热梯度、有限速度热波干涉和内部热波动，进而产生机械应变和亚晶粒热击穿。
