Abstract: Thermal runaway in lithium-ion batteries is governed by the poorly-understood initiation phase, where localised heating introduces instability. Here we identify the three key components that trigger thermal runaway, decreases in local conductivity, heat capacity changes, and intercalation heating, which significantly increase temperature gradients that accelerate battery degradation. Using a multiscale framework that links atomistic phonon calculations with grain-resolved thermal modelling, we identify large thermal gradients across grain boundaries arising from external heating events and intercalation-dependent thermal properties of Li$_x$ZrS$_2$. The observed changes in thermal conductivity are due to charge redistribution and bond-strength modulation of the host, in contrast to the existing theory of lithium rattler mechanics. Internal heating events driven by intercalation gives rise to local thermal gradients, finite-speed thermal wave interference, and internal thermal fluctuations that generate mechanical strain and sub-grain thermal breakdown. These results show that the trigger for thermal runaway is controlled by internal grain architecture and composition, as well as the external environment. Our findings establish materials and electrode design rules for suppressing hotspot formation and improving battery safety during fast charging.

Abstract: We investigate the feasibility of the macrospin approximation to account for the actual shape of soft magnetic nanoparticles (MNPs) with realistic geometries. Specifically focusing on magnetite, we use the superellipsoidal parametrisation to account for a variety of shapes, with a continuous interpolation from spherical to cubic morphologies, as well as different elongations. Our procedure consists of the direct comparison between angular-dependent hysteresis loops obtained by full micromagnetic simulations, with those produced by an extended Stoner-Wohlfarth (SW) model that incorporates both the intrinsic cubic magnetocrystalline anisotropy, and an effective uniaxial contribution arising from the particle elongation. These results establish a direct connection between nanoparticle morphology and effective macrospin parameters, demonstrating the suitability of the generalized SW model for describing the magnetic response of realistically shaped MNPs.

### [50] [Bulk and surface electronic structure of MoAlB(010)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20540)
*Gianmarco Gatti,Amalie H. Svaneborg,Wu Bing,Gesa-R. Siemann,Anders S. Mortensen,Naina Kushwaha,Jennifer Rigden,Jakob K. Svaneborg,Matthew D. Watson,Timur K. Kim,Charlotte E. Sanders,Kristian S. Thygesen,Zdenek Sofer,Philip Hofmann*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究MoAlB(010)材料的体相和表面电子结构，特别关注表面态的存在、稳定性及其自旋轨道分裂特性，以理解表面态的元素和轨道特性对其性质的影响。

Method: 采用角分辨光电子能谱（angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy, ARPES）与密度泛函理论（density functional）计算相结合的方法，系统研究MoAlB(010)的电子结构。

Result: 观察到体相费米能级交叉与先前报道的体相费米面一致；在费米能级附近的宽投影体相带隙中发现了多个表面态；这些表面态在真空系统残余气体暴露下的稳定性和Rashba型自旋轨道分裂（Rashba-type spin-orbit splitting）幅度存在差异。

Conclusion: 表面态的性质差异源于其元素和轨道特性：Al悬挂键（Al dangling bonds）形成的表面态对表面污染敏感，而主要源自Mo的表面态表现出更强的自旋轨道分裂；表面态在表面布里渊区$\bar{\mathrm{S}}$点附近存在由p2mm壁纸群（p2mm wallpaper group）的镜面对称元素保护的对称性强制交叉。

Abstract: The bulk and surface electronic structure of MoAlB(010) is studied by a combination of angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy and density functional calculations. The observed bulk Fermi-level crossings agree with the previously reported bulk Fermi surface of the material. Additionally, we find several surface states in the wide projected bulk band gaps around the Fermi energy. The surface states differ in their stability under residual-gas exposure in the vacuum system and in the magnitude of their Rashba-type spin-orbit splitting. We explain this in terms of their elemental and orbital character. A surface state arising from Al dangling bonds is sensitive to surface contamination, whereas a mainly Mo-derived surface state exhibits the stronger spin-orbit splitting. The surface states show symmetry-enforced crossings near the $\bar{\mathrm{S}}$ point of the surface Brillouin zone. These are protected by the mirror-symmetry elements of the p2mm wallpaper group.

</details>


### [51] [A computational alloy design framework for the promotion of amorphous grain boundary complexions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20547)
*Prince Sharma,Jaime Marian,Jason R. Trelewicz,Timothy J. Rupert*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种计算框架，用于设计具有非晶晶界复合体（amorphous grain boundary complexions）的合金，通过密度泛函理论（density functional theory）计算筛选促进非晶晶界形成的掺杂元素，并以富钨（W-rich）合金为例验证了该框架的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非晶晶界复合体（amorphous grain boundary complexions）已被证明是耐辐射界面，并能减少晶界脆化，是理想的微观结构特征。然而，将这些特征融入新合金体系通常是一个基于试错的缓慢而艰难的过程。

Method: 提出了一个基于密度泛函理论（density functional theory）计算的计算框架，首先评估掺杂元素的晶界偏析（grain boundary segregation）倾向，然后计算非晶化（amorphization）的能量惩罚并进行目标界面能比较，最终识别最佳掺杂元素。以富钨（W-rich）二元和三元合金为例进行了演示。

Result: 对于钨基体，钇（Y）和一些过渡金属如钴（Co）和镍（Ni）被发现能显著降低这些能量壁垒。通过电子结构分析、局部晶格畸变（local lattice distortion）和电荷密度分布计算提供了这些掺杂选择的机理解释。该框架通过与钨合金和难熔复杂高熵合金（refractory complex concentrated alloy）的实验文献对比得到验证，显示出掺杂选择与低烧结起始温度之间的强相关性。

Conclusion: 这项工作建立了一个可迁移的流程（transferable pipeline），用于在不同合金体系中设计具有晶界复合体（grain-boundary complexions）的合金。

Abstract: Amorphous grain boundary complexions have been shown to be radiation tolerant interfaces that can also reduce grain boundary embrittlement, marking them as favorable microstructural features. However, the incorporation of these features into new alloy systems is often a slow and arduous process based on trial and error. Here, a computational framework for alloy design is presented which enables the selection of dopants that promote the formation of amorphous grain boundary complexions. This framework is primarily built on density functional theory calculations and is demonstrated for W-rich binary and ternary alloys, which represent a promising target for fusion energy materials. Our framework first evaluates the grain boundary segregation tendency of dopants and then the energy penalty for amorphization alongside targeted interfacial energy comparison, with the end goal of identifying the best dopants. For a W base, Y and some transition metals such as Co and Ni are found to significantly lower these energetic barriers. Electronic structure analysis, local lattice distortion, and charge density distributions are calculated and used to provide mechanistic explanations for these dopant selections. Finally, the framework is validated by comparing with experimental literature for W alloys and a refractory complex concentrated alloy, showing a strong correlation between our dopant selections and low sintering onset temperatures that have been attributed to activated sintering. As a whole, this work establishes a transferable pipeline for designing alloys with grain-boundary complexions across diverse alloy systems.

</details>


### [52] [Predicting co-segregation in multicomponent alloys with solute-solute interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20593)
*Zuoyong Zhang,Chuang Deng*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究开发了一个扩展的双溶质偏析框架，用于定量预测多组分合金中的共偏析行为，特别考虑了溶质-溶质相互作用的影响，并通过机器学习工作流程和模拟验证了该框架的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多组分合金中杂质的共偏析是调控材料性能的有效策略，但定量预测含多种溶质体系的共偏析行为仍是合金设计的重要挑战。

Method: 研究开发了扩展的双溶质偏析框架，首先建立机器学习工作流程预测成对偏析能，构建包含溶质-溶质相互作用的双溶质偏析能谱，然后利用谱信息确定各溶质偏析的上下界。

Result: 该框架在镁基多组分体系中成功验证，与混合分子动力学/蒙特卡洛模拟及现有文献实验结果一致；研究还提出了通过引入与现有溶质具有吸引相互作用的额外溶质来促进共偏析的设计策略。

Conclusion: 溶质-溶质相互作用在调控共偏析行为中起关键作用，该研究为多组分合金的设计与优化提供了预测性途径。

Abstract: The co-segregation of impurities in multicomponent alloys has been widely recognized as an effective strategy for tailoring material properties. However, quantitative predictions of co-segregation behavior remain a significant challenge for alloy design in systems containing multiple solute species. In this work, we develop an extended dual-solute (DS) segregation framework to quantitatively predict co-segregation behavior with solute-solute interactions, including both homoatomic and heteroatomic contributions. A machine-learning workflow is first established to predict the pairwise segregation energy to construct the DS segregation energy spectra that intrinsically include solute-solute interactions. The resulting spectral information is then utilized to determine the upper and lower bounds of segregation for individual solutes. When applied to magnesium-based multicomponent systems constructed by alloying Mg with any two of the 11 candidate solute species, the extended DS segregation framework is successfully validated by hybrid molecular dynamics/Monte Carlo simulations and experimental results available in existing literature. Furthermore, we introduce a design strategy to promote co-segregation by incorporating additional solute species that exhibit attractive interactions with existing solutes, thereby enabling enhanced segregation even in the presence of strong site competition. These results underscore the critical role of solute-solute interactions in governing co-segregation behavior and provide a predictive pathway for the design and optimization of multicomponent alloys.

### [53] [Load-dependent Hardness Prediction for Materials using Machine Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20636)
*Madhubanti Mukherjee,Rampi Ramprasad,Harikrishna Sahu*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究开发了基于机器学习（ML）的硬度预测模型，通过包含压痕载荷（indentation load）等关键参数，显著提升了超硬材料（superhard materials）硬度预测的准确性，超越了传统基于密度泛函理论（DFT）弹性模量的方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超硬材料在耐磨和高应力应用中至关重要。传统方法通过密度泛函理论（DFT）计算的弹性模量关联硬度，虽能快速筛选但忽略了硬度的强载荷依赖性（load dependence）。

Method: 本研究利用大量经过整理的载荷依赖性实验维氏硬度（Hv）测量数据集，开发了机器学习（ML）模型。比较了仅使用实验数据的单任务模型（single-task ML model）与结合实验和计算数据的多任务模型（multi-task models）。

Result: 实验硬度与基于DFT的硬度值之间仅存在中等相关性。仅基于实验数据训练的单任务ML模型性能优于结合实验和计算数据的多任务模型。单任务模型的优越性表明，明确包含压痕载荷（indentation load）以及成分、电子和结构描述符（descriptors）对于准确预测硬度至关重要且足够。

Conclusion: 这些结果强调了高质量实验数据以及明确包含测量条件（特别是载荷）在开发可靠硬度预测模型中的重要性。仅使用DFT可获取的体积模量和剪切模量（或与实验数据结合）无法达到同等预测精度。

Abstract: Superhard materials are critical for wear-resistant and high-stress applications. Conventional approaches correlating hardness with elastic moduli derived from DFT calculations enable rapid screening but overlook the strong load dependence of hardness. In this work, machine learning (ML) models were developed using a large, curated dataset of load-dependent experimental Vickers hardness (Hv) measurements. Moderate correlation was observed between experimental and DFT-based Hv values, whereas a single-task ML model trained solely on experimental data outperformed multi-task models that combined experimental and computed data. The superior performance of the single-task model highlights that explicit inclusion of indentation load, along with compositional, electronic, and structural descriptors, is essential and sufficient for accurate hardness prediction, beyond what can be achieved using DFT-accessible bulk and shear moduli alone (or in tandem with experimental data). These results emphasize the importance of high-quality experimental data and explicit inclusion of measurement conditions, particularly load, in the development of reliable hardness prediction models.

</details>


### [54] [Polaron transport and Verwey transition in magnetite](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20642)
*Nikita Fominykh,Vladimir Stegailov*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究通过结合第一性原理计算、动力学蒙特卡洛和分子动力学模拟，建立了磁铁矿（Fe₃O₄）中极化子输运的微观模型，揭示了Verwey相变中三聚子（trimeron）跳跃机制，而非传统小极化子模型所预测的能带结构显著变化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 磁铁矿（Fe₃O₄）中的Verwey相变之谜已持续近一个世纪未能解决，需要建立能够直接描述极化子与晶格振动耦合的微观输运模型。

Method: 采用基于第一性原理（ab initio）的模型，结合动力学蒙特卡洛（kinetic Monte Carlo）和分子动力学（molecular dynamics）计算，直接描述极化子与晶格振动的耦合。

Result: 研究发现，与Ihle-Lorentz小极化子（small-polaron）模型相反，Verwey相变前后能带结构无显著变化，但观测到三聚子（trimeron）跳跃现象；所提模型给出的直流电导率（dc-conductivity）与实验数据吻合。

Conclusion: 该研究建立的微观模型成功解释了磁铁矿Verwey相变的输运特性，揭示了三聚子跳跃机制的关键作用，为这一长期未解的物理问题提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: The enigmatic puzzle of the Verwey transition in magnetite Fe$_3$O$_4$ has been unresolved for almost a century. We present an ab initio-based model of the polaron transport combining kinetic Monte Carlo and molecular dynamics calculations to directly describe the coupling of polarons with lattice vibrations. Contrary to the Ihle-Lorentz small-polaron model, we find no significant change in the band structure across the Verwey transition, however, trimeron hopping is observed. The proposed model provides dc-conductivity in agreement with experimental data across the Verwey transition.

### [55] [Strain effects in [001] textured Co80Ir20 thin films with negative magnetocrystalline anisotropy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20645)
*L. Aviles Felix,M. Vasquez Mansilla,J. E. Gomez,M. Balod,J. Padilla,J. Santiso,Subhakanta Das,S. N. Piramanayagam,A. Butera*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究分析了Co80Ir20铁磁薄膜中磁弹性效应（magnetoelastic effects）对磁各向异性的影响，发现不同底层材料（Ta、Pt）诱导的应变差异显著影响薄膜的有效各向异性场。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Co80Ir20铁磁薄膜因其负磁晶各向异性（negative magnetocrystalline anisotropy）与形状各向异性（shape anisotropy）叠加而备受关注，但已有研究大多未充分考虑磁弹性效应（magnetoelastic effects）的作用。

Method: 研究在Si/SiO2衬底上沉积24 nm厚Co80Ir20薄膜，采用不同底层材料（Ta、Pt）和覆盖层诱导[001]织构生长和不同程度的应变，通过X射线衍射（x-ray diffraction）、室温磁化强度-磁场回线（magnetization vs field loops）、温度依赖直流磁化测量（temperature dependent dc magnetization）和铁磁共振（ferromagnetic resonance）进行表征。

Result: X射线衍射显示c轴晶格参数（c-axis lattice parameter）依赖于底层材料（Ta产生更大的负应变），但织构度和平均晶粒尺寸基本恒定；铁磁共振测量表明有效各向异性场（effective anisotropy field）也受底层影响，Ta底层各向异性接近形状各向异性预期值，而Pt底层诱导了约7-9 kOe的额外面内各向异性场（in-plane anisotropy field）。

Conclusion: 观测到的应变与各向异性之间的相关性，结合微观结构性质的相似性，强烈表明在分析磁性数据以估算磁晶贡献（magnetocrystalline contribution）时，应力效应（stress effects）不可忽略。

Abstract: Co80Ir20 ferromagnetic thin films have recently been the focus of intensive research because the negative magnetocrystalline anisotropy adds to the shape anisotropy and favors a strong alignment of the magnetization in the film plane for [001] textured or epitaxial thin films. However, the role of magnetoelastic effects has not been properly considered in most published research. In this work we have performed a detailed analysis of 24 nm Co80Ir20 thin films deposited on Si/SiO2 with different underlayers (Ta, Pt) and overlayers in order to induce [001]-textured growth and different degrees of strain. Using x-ray diffraction measurements we have found that the c-axis lattice parameter depends on the underlayer material (larger negative strain for Ta), but the degree of texture and the average grain size remain essentially constant, except for one of the multilayers. Differences in the magnetic behavior according to the underlayer were also found in room temperature magnetization vs field loops and temperature dependent dc magnetization measurements. Anisotropy was quantified using ferromagnetic resonance which showed that the effective anisotropy field is also dependent on the underlayer. Ta underlayers show an anisotropy close to that expected for shape, while Pt underlayer induces an additional in-plane anisotropy field of the order of 7-9 kOe. A simple model of stress induced anisotropy gives anisotropy field values similar to those observed experimentally. The correlation between observed strain and anisotropy together with the similarity in microstructural properties strongly suggests that stress effects cannot be disregarded when analyzing the magnetic data for the estimation of the magnetocrystalline contribution.

### [56] [Engineering Wake-Up-Free Ferroelectric Capacitors with Enhanced High-Temperature Reliability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20698)
*Nashrah Afroze,Salma Soliman,Yu-Hsin Kuo,Sanghyun Kang,Mengkun Tian,Priyankka Ravikumar,Andrea Padovani,Asif Khan*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究系统探索了铁电铪锆氧化物（HZO）异质结构在高温可靠运行的设计空间，发现等离子增强原子层沉积（PE-ALD）HZO与钨（W）底电极组合可实现无唤醒（wake-up-free）开关特性至125°C，并显著提升耐久性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在探索铁电铪锆氧化物（HZO）异质结构的设计空间，以实现可靠的高温运行。研究动机源于需要将铁电存储器集成到单片三维（monolithic 3D）系统中，并满足严格的热约束条件。

Method: 采用热原子层沉积（Th-ALD）和等离子增强原子层沉积（PE-ALD）技术在钨（W）和氮化钛（TiN）底电极上沉积HZO薄膜，同时保持相同的顶电极结构。通过解耦等离子沉积HZO薄膜和PE-ALD过程中固有形成的氧化底界面的贡献，分析各因素对性能的影响。

Result: PE-ALD HZO与W底电极组合在125°C下表现出无唤醒开关特性，并在85-125°C宽温度范围内显著改善耐久性。氧化钨界面层（WOx）是高温下耐久性增强和唤醒抑制的主要因素，而PE-ALD HZO薄膜在减少唤醒方面提供次要益处。相比之下，PE-ALD HZO/TiN器件在唤醒行为或耐久性方面无明显改善，反而表现出极化性能退化。

Conclusion: PE-ALD HZO薄膜仅在沉积于W底电极上时才能在高温下实现优异的铁电性能，而Th-ALD HZO薄膜在TiN底电极上仍是高温运行的可选方案。这些发现阐明了沉积技术、电极化学和界面氧化之间的相互作用，为在严格热约束下集成铁电存储器到单片三维系统提供了设计指导。

Abstract: We systematically explore the design space of ferroelectric hafnium-zirconium oxide (H0.5Z0.5O or HZO) heterostructures for reliable high temperature operation. HZO films are deposited using thermal and plasma-enhanced atomic layer deposition (Th-ALD and PE-ALD) on tungsten (W) and titanium nitride (TiN) bottom electrodes (BE), while maintaining identical top electrodes. We demonstrate that PE-ALD HZO capacitors integrated with W BE exhibit wake-up-free switching up to 125C, along with significantly improved endurance compared to Th-ALD HZO/W devices across a wide temperature range (85-125C). By decoupling the contributions of the plasma-deposited HZO film and the oxidized bottom interface inherently formed during PE-ALD, we identify the oxidized W interfacial layer (WOx) as the primary factor governing endurance enhancement and wake-up suppression at elevated temperatures, while the PE-ALD HZO film provides secondary benefits in reducing wake-up. In contrast, PE-ALD HZO capacitors fabricated on TiN BE show no substantial improvement in wake-up behavior or endurance relative to Th-ALD HZO/TiN devices, despite the formation of an unintentional TiOxNy interfacial layer, and instead exhibit degraded polarization. This difference arises from the significantly weaker endurance enhancement and no wake-up suppression provided by oxidized TiN compared to oxidized W under comparable oxidation conditions. Overall, PE-ALD HZO films enable superior ferroelectric performance at elevated temperatures only when deposited on W BE, while Th-ALD HZO films remain a viable option for high temperature operation on TiN BE. These findings clarify the interplay between deposition technique, electrode chemistry, and interfacial oxidation, and provide design guidelines for integrating ferroelectric memories into monolithic 3D systems under stringent thermal constraints.

### [57] [Anisotropic multiband magnetotransport in LaAg$_2$Ge$_2$ thin films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20709)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Here, we report the molecular-beam epitaxy growth of LaAg$_2$Ge$_2$ thin films on MgO(001) and their magnetotransport properties. The Hall effect and magnetoresistance are captured by an effective two-carrier description with a high-mobility electron band, yielding a positive magnetoresistance of 22.5% at 9 T. Angle-dependent magnetoresistance exhibits a dominant twofold anisotropy and additional reproducible dip/peak features at characteristic tilt angles that are nearly independent of field and temperature. These results extend our understanding of the anisotropic electronic transport in thin-film germanides within the ThCr$_2$Si$_2$ family.

### [58] [Determining metrics from the scattering map of the time-dependent Schrödinger equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20160)
*Qiuye Jia*

Main category: math.AP

Method: 分析含时薛定谔方程的散射映射，研究两个含时度量对应的薛定谔算子的散射映射之差，建立其与度量几何结构之间的联系。

Result: 对于特定类别的度量，两个含时度量对应的薛定谔算子的散射映射仅相差一个紧算子当且仅当这两个度量通过微分同胚的拉回相关联。

Abstract: For a time dependent Schrödinger equation, the scattering map is the map sending the asymptotic profile of solution as $t\to-\infty$ to its asymptotic profile as $t\to+\infty$. In this paper we show that, for certain class of metrics, the scattering maps associated to two Schrödinger operators with two time dependent metrics only differ by a compact operator if and only if these two metrics are related by a pull-back of a diffeomorphism.

### [59] [Mathematical analysis of transverse EM field concentration for adjacent obstacles with nonlocal boundary conditions in the quasistatic regime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20171)
*Yueguang Hu,Hongjie Li,Hongyu Liu*

TL;DR: 本文在准静态近似框架下，对两个相邻障碍物之间的横向电磁场集中现象进行了严格的数学分析。研究聚焦于三种简并电导率模型，其中两个包含非局部边界条件，揭示了梯度爆炸的尖锐条件及最优爆炸速率，并阐明了波频率对场集中严重性的缓解作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在将经典场增强理论扩展到包含非局部表面效应，为纳米光子器件的定量设计提供精确的渐近公式。研究动机源于理解非局部边界条件如何修正经典梯度估计，以及波频率在间隙距离趋近于零时如何缓解场集中现象。

Method: 采用准静态近似（quasi-static approximation）框架，分析三种简并电导率模型（degenerate conductivity models）。其中两个模型引入了非局部边界条件（nonlocal boundary conditions）来捕捉表面非局域性（surface nonlocality）和薄层相互作用（thin-layer interactions）等基本物理现象。

Result: 建立了梯度爆炸（gradient blowup）的尖锐条件，并推导了相应的最优爆炸速率（optimal blowup rates）。结果表明非局部边界条件显著改变了经典梯度估计，同时发现波频率即使在间隙距离趋近于零时也能缓解场集中的严重程度。

Conclusion: 本研究成功将经典场增强理论扩展到包含非局部表面效应，为等离子体（plasmonic）和超材料（metamaterial）系统提供了精确的渐近公式。这些结果对于纳米光子器件（nanophotonic devices）的定量设计至关重要，揭示了非局部边界条件在调控场集中现象中的关键作用。

Abstract: This paper presents a rigorous mathematical analysis of transverse electromagnetic (EM) field concentration between two adjacent obstacles within the framework of the quasi-static approximation. We investigate three degenerate conductivity models recently introduced in [22], two of these incorporating nonlocal boundary conditions to capture fundamental physical phenomena, such as surface nonlocality and thin-layer interactions. Our primary results establish sharp conditions for gradient blowup and derive the corresponding optimal blowup rates. These findings elucidate how nonlocal boundary conditions modify classical gradient estimates. Furthermore, we analyze the influence of wave frequency, demonstrating that it mitigates the severity of field concentration even in the limit of a vanishing gap distance. Consequently, this work extends the classical theory of field enhancement in plasmonic and metamaterial systems to incorporate nonlocal surface effects, yielding precise asymptotic formulas that are essential for the quantitative design of nanophotonic devices.

</details>

### [60] [Quantum $f$-divergences via Nussbaum-Szkoła Distributions in Semifinite von Neumann Algebras](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19853)
*Theodoros Anastasiadis,George Androulakis*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明了在半有限冯·诺依曼代数上，两个正规态之间的量子f-散度等于对应的经典态（称为Nussbaum-Szkoła分布）之间的经典f-散度，将先前在$\mathbb{B}(\mathscr{H})$上的结果推广到任意半有限冯·诺依曼代数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究的动机是扩展先前关于量子f-散度与经典f-散度等价性的结果。先前研究仅证明了在有界算子代数$\mathbb{B}(\mathscr{H})$上两个正规态之间的量子f-散度等于对应的Nussbaum-Szkoła分布之间的经典f-散度。

Method: 采用数学证明的方法，将先前在$\mathbb{B}(\mathscr{H})$上的结果推广到任意半有限冯·诺依曼代数（semifinite von Neumann algebra）。该方法不限于特定的希尔伯特空间有界算子代数。

Result: 证明了在半有限冯·诺依曼代数上，两个正规态（normal states）之间的量子f-散度（quantum f-divergence）等于对应的经典态（称为Nussbaum-Szkoła分布）之间的经典f-散度（classical f-divergence）。

Conclusion: 该研究成功地将量子f-散度与经典f-散度的等价性结果从$\mathbb{B}(\mathscr{H})$推广到任意半有限冯·诺依曼代数，扩展了该数学框架的适用范围。

Abstract: In this article, we prove that the quantum $f$-divergence between two normal states on a semifinite von~Neumann algebra is equal to the classical $f$-divergence between two corresponding classical states, which are called Nussbaum-Szkoła distributions. This result has been proved by the second named author and T.C.~John for normal states on the von~Neumann algebra $\mathbb{B}(\mathscr{H})$ of all bounded operators on a Hilbert space $\mathscr{H}$. We extend their result for normal states on any semifinite von~Neumann algebra, not only $\mathbb{B}(\mathscr{H})$.

### [61] [Native quantum games from interacting discrete-time quantum walks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20455)
*Rashid Ahmad*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于相互作用的量子博弈框架，其中战略互动源于受控量子动力学而非外部数学结构。研究表明，在弱相互作用下，非平凡纳什均衡（Nash equilibrium）可以通过相互作用诱导的干涉项自然涌现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索战略互动如何从受控量子动力学中自然涌现，而非作为外部数学结构强加于系统。作者旨在建立一种物理上明确的战略相互依赖实现方式，将博弈论行为与量子输运过程联系起来。

Method: 方法包括引入相互作用定义的量子博弈（interaction-defined quantum games），其中玩家由可区分的量子行走者（quantum walkers）表示，策略对应局部硬币操作（local coin operations），收益定义为物理可观测量（physical observables）的期望值。具体采用相互作用的离散时间量子行走（interacting discrete-time quantum walks）作为平台，并在弱相互作用区域推导了收益函数的解析微扰分解（analytic perturbative decomposition）。

Result: 数值模拟表明，当行走者耦合时，竞争性、合作性和非对称博弈都允许稳定的稳态策略配置（stable stationary strategy profiles），而在没有相互作用时不存在非平凡均衡。对于基于碰撞的相位相互作用（collision-based phase interaction），收益在相互作用强度的一阶项上变得不可分离，并通常允许满足纳什条件（Nash conditions）的驻点。

Conclusion: 结论指出，该研究为量子输运过程中的战略相互依赖提供了物理上明确的实现，并确立了相互作用的量子行走作为研究从幺正动力学（unitary dynamics）中涌现的博弈论行为的最小平台。战略耦合源于联合概率分布中相互作用诱导的干涉项（interaction-induced interference terms）。

Abstract: We study how strategic interaction can arise from controlled quantum dynamics rather than being imposed as an external mathematical structure. We introduce a class of interaction-defined quantum games in which players are represented by distinguishable quantum walkers, strategies correspond to local coin operations, and payoffs are defined as expectation values of physical observables. Using interacting discrete-time quantum walks as a concrete platform, we demonstrate numerically that competitive, cooperative, and asymmetric games admit stable stationary strategy profiles when the walkers are coupled, while no non-trivial equilibria exist in the absence of interaction. To clarify the game-theoretic structure, we derive an analytic perturbative decomposition of the payoff function in the weak-interaction regime, showing explicitly that strategic coupling originates from interaction-induced interference terms in the joint probability distribution. For a collision-based phase interaction, the payoff becomes non-separable at first order in the interaction strength and generically admits stationary points satisfying the Nash conditions. Our results provide a physically explicit realization of strategic interdependence in quantum transport processes and establish interacting quantum walks as a minimal platform for studying game-theoretic behavior emerging from unitary dynamics.

</details>


### [62] [Derivation of the Schrodinger equation from fundamental principles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27041)
*Wenzhuo Zhang,Anatoly Svidzinsky*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文通过概率幅解释和能量-频率、动量-波矢关系，从基本原理推导薛定谔方程，提供了比薛定谔原始启发式方法更形式化的推导路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 薛定谔（Schrodinger）推导量子力学波动方程的路径是启发式的，更多依赖物理直觉而非形式化演绎。本文旨在提供更严谨的推导框架。

Method: 假设粒子波函数具有概率幅（probability amplitude）的物理意义，即找到粒子在时间t、位置r的概率幅，并利用关系式E=ħω、p=ħk将粒子能量和动量与关联概率波的频率和波矢联系起来。

Result: 基于上述假设和关系，推导出了薛定谔方程（Schrodinger equation）的粒子波函数形式。

Conclusion: 通过将波函数解释为概率幅并利用量子力学基本关系，可以形式化地推导薛定谔方程，这比原始启发式方法更具理论基础。

Abstract: Schrodinger path to the quantum mechanical wave equation was heuristic and guided more by physical intuition than formal deduction. Here we derive the Schrodinger equation for the particle wave function, assuming that it has a meaning of the probability amplitude to find the particle at time t at point r and the relations E=hw, p=hk expressing particle energy and momentum in terms of the frequency and wave vector of the associated probability wave.

</details>


### [63] [Rank-2 Electromagnetic Backgrounds and Angular Momentum Barriers in Gravitomagnetic Spin-Quadrupole Searches](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20717)
*Leonardo A. Pachon*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文系统分析了在高度带电离子中探测引力磁自旋四极耦合（gravitomagnetic spin-quadrupole coupling）时面临的四个主要障碍，并提出了使用多同位素、多跃迁的广义金图（Generalized King Plot）来分离电磁背景与引力信号的代数条件，为钼同位素链提供了首个实验室可推导的界限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在系统分析探测引力磁自旋四极耦合（gravitomagnetic spin-quadrupole coupling）在高度带电离子（highly charged ions）中面临的角动量选择规则和电磁背景约束，为实验设计提供理论框架。

Method: 通过识别四个顺序障碍并推导代数条件，提出使用多同位素、多跃迁的广义金图（Generalized King Plot）来分离电磁背景与引力信号，最小实验拓扑要求三个跃迁和满足特定条件的奇数自旋同位素。

Result: 对于钼同位素链（molybdenum chain），获得了首个实验室可推导的陀螺引力比（gyrogravitational ratio）界限 |χ-1| ≲ 10⁸-10⁹，该界限受限于当前核四极矩和跃迁速率的测量精度。

Conclusion: 论文量化了改进该界限每个数量级所需的实验里程碑，为未来探测引力磁自旋四极耦合的实验提供了路线图，强调了核参数精度对分离电磁背景的关键作用。

Abstract: We present a complete analysis of the angular momentum selection rules and electromagnetic backgrounds that constrain any spectroscopic search for the gravitomagnetic spin-quadrupole coupling in highly charged ions. A sequence of four barriers is identified: (i)~the Wigner-Eckart theorem mandates $j \geq 3/2$ electronic states for sensitivity to the rank-2 gravitomagnetic operator, excluding the deformation-immune $j=1/2$ states; (ii)~the nuclear electric quadrupole hyperfine interaction (HFS-E2) generates an $\sim 18$-orders-of-magnitude electromagnetic background in the required $j=3/2$ channel; (iii)~second-order HFS mixing between fine-structure levels leaves a residual $\sim 10^{-6}$ eV even after centroid extraction; (iv)~tensor nuclear polarizability (TNP), scaling with $B(E2)$ rather than $Q_s$, introduces an independent rank-2 background of $\sim 10^{-12}$ eV. We derive the algebraic conditions under which a multi-isotope, multi-transition Generalized King Plot can separate these backgrounds from the gravitational signal, and show that the minimum experimental topology requires three transitions and $N_{\text{odd}} \geq N_{\text{bkg}} + 1$ odd-spin isotopes with linearly independent nuclear parameters. For the molybdenum chain, this yields a first laboratory-derivable bound $|χ- 1| \lesssim 10^{8} - 10^9$ on the gyrogravitational ratio, limited by current precision on nuclear quadrupole moments and transition rates. We quantify the experimental milestones needed to improve this bound by each order of magnitude, providing a roadmap for future searches.

</details>


### [64] [Path integral formulation of finite-dimensional quantum mechanics in discrete phase space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20776)
*Leonardo A. Pachon,Andres F. Gomez*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究为有限维希尔伯特空间量子系统动力学建立了离散相空间中的路径积分表示，推导出精确演化核和加权离散相空间作用的路径求和表达式，并应用于qutrit系统验证纠缠动力学。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于为有限维量子系统动力学建立离散相空间中的路径积分表示，为多体自旋系统的半经典模拟和非经典性表征提供理论框架。

Method: 方法基于定义在$\mathbb{Z}_d \times \mathbb{Z}_d$（$d$为奇素数）上的离散维格纳函数（discrete Wigner function）和广义位移算子构建的韦尔变换（Weyl transform），推导精确演化核并利用核的组合律和短时近似迭代获得路径求和表达式。

Result: 结果显示：对于相空间坐标线性的哈密顿量，涨落求和可因子化并在与晶格严格共度的时间（克利福德协变区域）坍缩为确定性位移，实现经典哈密顿流的离散类比。应用于单qutrit和两个相互作用qutrits时，完整纠缠动力学需要作用量所有涨落区域的相干贡献。

Conclusion: 该构造为多体自旋系统的半经典模拟和通过维格纳负性（Wigner negativity）表征非经典性提供了相关框架，$\tildeμ=0$区域在有限时间步长下非实且在连续极限中坍缩为平凡核，无法再现纠缠动力学。

Abstract: We develop a path integral representation for the dynamics of quantum systems with a finite-dimensional Hilbert space, formulated entirely within a discrete phase space. Starting from the discrete Wigner function defined on $\mathbb{Z}_d \times \mathbb{Z}_d$ (with $d$ an odd prime), and the associated Weyl transform built from generalized displacement operators, we derive an exact evolution kernel that propagates the discrete Wigner function in time. By exploiting the composition law of the kernel and iterating the short-time approximation, we obtain a sum-over-paths expression for the propagator weighted by a discrete phase-space action that is the natural finite-dimensional counterpart of Marinov's functional. For Hamiltonians linear in the phase-space coordinates, we show that the fluctuation sum factorizes and, at times strictly commensurate with the lattice (the Clifford-covariant regime), collapses to a deterministic shift realizing the discrete analog of classical Hamiltonian flow. The formulation is applied to a single qutrit ($d=3$) under a diagonal Hamiltonian, and to two interacting qutrits, where we show explicitly that the full entanglement dynamics -- captured by a closed-form expression for the linear entropy valid for all times -- requires the coherent contribution of all fluctuation sectors of the action. The $\tildeμ= 0$ sector alone is non-real at finite time step and collapses to a trivial (uniform) kernel in the continuum limit, failing to reproduce the entanglement dynamics in either regime. We discuss the relevance of this construction for semiclassical simulation of many-body spin systems and the characterization of non-classicality through Wigner negativity.

</details>


### [65] [Bootstrapping Open Quantum Many-body Systems with Absorbing Phase Transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19862)
*Minjae Cho,Colin Oscar Nancarrow,Petar Tadić,Yuan Xin*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于密度矩阵正定性和稳态条件的系统化自举方法（bootstrap method），用于研究无限格点上具有吸收相变（absorbing phase transitions）的开放量子多体系统，并以量子接触过程（quantum contact process）为例进行了应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究开放量子多体系统（open quantum many-body systems）的稳态性质，特别是那些由Lindblad主方程（Lindblad master equations）描述且具有吸收相变（absorbing phase transitions）的系统。传统方法在处理这类无限格点系统时面临挑战，需要发展新的理论工具。

Method: 结合密度矩阵的正定性（positivity of density matrices）与稳态条件（steady-state conditions），发展了一种系统化的自举方法（bootstrap method）。该方法适用于无限格点上的Lindblad主方程系统，并以量子接触过程（quantum contact process）作为具体应用实例。

Result: 获得了稳态期望值的自举界限（bootstrap bounds）、临界耦合（critical coupling）、超临界相（supercritical phase）中非平凡稳态期望值比值的界限，以及亚临界相（subcritical phase）中Liouvillian谱隙（Liouvillian spectral gap）的界限。

Conclusion: 该方法为研究具有吸收相变的开放量子多体系统提供了有效的理论框架，能够系统地获得各种物理量的界限，展示了自举方法在量子非平衡系统研究中的应用潜力。

Abstract: We demonstrate that combining the positivity of density matrices with steady-state conditions yields a systematic bootstrap method for studying open quantum many-body systems governed by Lindblad master equations on infinite lattices, which exhibit absorbing phase transitions. As a concrete example, we apply this method to the quantum contact process with an absorbing state. We obtain bootstrap bounds on steady-state expectation values, the critical coupling, certain ratios of expectation values in the nontrivial steady state in the supercritical phase, and the Liouvillian spectral gap in the subcritical phase.

### [66] [Optimal Work Extraction from Finite-Time Closed Quantum Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.20512)
*Shoki Sugimoto,Takahiro Sagawa,Ryusuke Hamazaki*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了量子系统中功率与功之间的基本权衡关系，并针对一类可解的多体量子系统，提出了有限时间最优功提取问题的精确求解方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从量子系统中提取有用功是量子热力学的基本问题。在需要快速协议的场景中，功率与效率之间的基本权衡关系尚未建立，这促使研究者探索有限时间最优功提取问题。

Method: 研究在控制哈密顿量（control Hamiltonian）幅度受限的条件下，分析封闭量子系统的有限时间最优功提取问题。关键假设是控制哈密顿量在未受控动力学所保持的李代数（Lie algebra）上进行优化，从而将问题精确简化为非线性自洽方程。

Result: 研究揭示了功率与功之间的权衡关系，表明这两个基本性能指标无法同时最大化。对于包括海森堡模型（Heisenberg model）和SU(n)-哈伯德模型（SU(n)-Hubbard model）在内的可解多体系统，最优协议在相互作用绘景（interaction picture）中简化为时间无关的控制哈密顿量。

Conclusion: 该研究强调了快速协议对于实现最大功率的必要性，并为多体量子系统中的有限时间最优功提取提供了精确求解路径。通过利用可控项的李代数结构，该方法可通过高效数值计算应用于量子多体系统。

Abstract: Extracting useful work from quantum systems is a fundamental problem in quantum thermodynamics. In scenarios where rapid protocols are desired -- whether due to practical constraints or deliberate design choices -- a fundamental trade-off between power and efficiency is yet to be established. Here, we investigate the problem of finite-time optimal work extraction from closed quantum systems, subject to a constraint on the magnitude of the control Hamiltonian. We first reveal the trade-off relation between power and work under a general setup, showing that these fundamental performance metrics cannot be maximized simultaneously. We then identify a solvable class of finite-time optimal work-extraction problems. This class includes nontrivial many-body models such as the Heisenberg model and the SU(n)-Hubbard model. The key assumption is that the control Hamiltonian is optimized over a Lie algebra preserved by the uncontrolled dynamics. Within this class, the optimal work-extraction problem admits an exact reduction to a nonlinear self-consistent equation, circumventing extensive search over time-dependent control paths. The resulting optimal protocol turns out to be particularly simple: it suffices to use a time-independent control Hamiltonian in the interaction picture, determined by that equation. By exploiting the Lie-algebraic structure of the controllable terms, our approach is applicable to quantum many-body systems through efficient numerical computation. Our results highlight the necessity of rapid protocols to achieve the maximum power and provide an exact route to finite-time optimal work extraction in many-body quantum systems.

</details>


### [67] [Measurement and feedback-driven adaptive dynamics in the classical and quantum kicked top](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19874)
*Mahaveer Prasad,Ahana Chakraborty,Thomas Iadecola,Manas Kulkarni,J. H. Pixley,Sriram Ganeshan,Justin H. Wilson*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究将经典动力系统中的随机反馈控制协议应用于量子混沌的典范模型——受踢陀螺（kicked top），展示了在经典、半经典和量子极限下均可实现控制，并分析了量子干涉对高矩观测量的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典动力系统中，随机反馈可以稳定原本不稳定的周期轨道，形成受控与未受控相。本研究旨在将这些控制协议应用于量子混沌的典范模型——受踢陀螺（kicked top），探索其在经典、半经典和量子极限下的控制效果。

Method: 采用受踢陀螺作为研究模型，该模型可描述为自旋-S（spin-S）物体的动力学，其中自旋大小S充当有效普朗克常数（effective Planck constant），自然地在不同极限间插值。通过比较完整量子动力学与截断维格纳近似（truncated Wigner approximation），后者捕捉量子噪声但忽略埃伦费斯特时间（Ehrenfest time）后的干涉效应。

Result: 研究表明受踢陀螺在经典、半经典和完全量子极限下均可通过随机反馈协议控制。低矩观测量主要由半经典描述解释，而高矩的剩余差异与干涉贡献一致，可能还包括探索紧致相空间（compact phase space）的稀有轨迹中的非线性效应。数值研究显示所有控制率下均出现快速纯化（rapid purification）。

Conclusion: 控制能够淬灭（quench）陀螺编码量子比特（qubit）量子信息的能力，即使在未受控相中也是如此。这表明随机反馈控制协议在量子混沌系统中具有广泛适用性，且量子干涉效应对高矩观测量有显著影响。

Abstract: In classical dynamical systems, stochastic feedback can stabilize otherwise unstable periodic orbits, giving rise to distinct controlled and uncontrolled phases as the rate of control application is varied. In this work, we apply these control protocols in classical, semiclassical, and quantum regimes to the kicked top, a paradigmatic model of quantum chaos. The quantum kicked top, modeled as the dynamics of a spin-S object, naturally interpolates between these regimes with the spin size S acting as an effective Planck constant. We show that the dynamics of the kicked top in classical, semiclassical, and fully quantum limits can all be controlled using stochastic feedback protocols. Comparing the full quantum dynamics to a truncated Wigner approximation that captures quantum noise but neglects interference beyond the Ehrenfest time, we find that low-moment observables are largely accounted for semiclassically, while the remaining discrepancy in higher moments is consistent with contributions from interference and possibly nonlinearities in rare trajectories that explore the compact phase space. We also find rapid purification in the numerics studied for all rates of control considered, suggesting that control quenches the top's ability to encode a qubit of quantum information even in the uncontrolled phase.

</details>


### [68] [Quantum-to-Classical Computability Transition via Negative Markov Chains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19889)
*Hugo Lóio,Jacopo De Nardis,Tony Jin*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究基于负马尔可夫链过程采样发展了一种量子动力学表示方法，通过引入粒子和反粒子将量子动力学映射到指数大的构型空间上的马尔可夫过程。研究发现，对于由局部或成对相互作用生成的幺正演化，存在至少一种噪声通道能有效经典化系统，使蒙特卡洛采样变得高效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在理解量子复杂性的起源及其在噪声环境下的行为。量子复杂性源于随机粒子的增殖，这导致经典模拟和采样在特定时间尺度后变得不可行。研究探索噪声如何影响量子系统的可模拟性。

Method: 采用基于负马尔可夫链过程采样的量子动力学表示方法，引入粒子和反粒子概念。该方法将一般量子动力学映射到指数大构型空间上的马尔可夫过程。通过分析噪声通道对粒子增长的影响来研究系统的经典化过程。

Result: 研究发现，对于由局部或成对相互作用生成的幺正演化，存在至少一种噪声通道能有效经典化系统，抑制粒子增长并使蒙特卡洛采样高效。作为推论，对于这类幺正演化，受去极化噪声影响的开量子自旋链动力学在噪声强度超过临界阈值时会经历精确的经典可模拟性转变。

Conclusion: 噪声可以显著改变量子系统的可模拟性特征，使原本因粒子增殖而难以经典模拟的量子动力学在足够强的噪声下变得可高效采样。该临界阈值对于任何模型都能有效确定，为理解噪声环境下的量子计算复杂性提供了新视角。

Abstract: We develop a recently introduced representation of quantum dynamics based on sampling negative Markov chain processes. By introducing particles and antiparticles, this formalism maps generic quantum dynamics onto a Markov process defined over an exponentially large configuration space. Within this framework, quantum complexity arises from the proliferation of stochastic particles, which ultimately renders classical simulation and sampling intractable beyond a certain timescale. In the presence of noise, we demonstrate that for any unitary evolution generated by a linear combination of local or pairwise interactions, there exists at least one noise channel that effectively classicalizes the system by suppressing particle growth and making Monte Carlo sampling efficient. As a corollary, we show that for this class of unitaries, the dynamics of an open quantum spin chain subject to depolarizing noise undergoes an exact transition to classical simulability once the noise strength exceeds a critical threshold which can be efficiently determined for any model.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 扩展了基于非对易哈密顿量吉布斯态精确KMS细致平衡（exact KMS-detailed balance）的构造方法，为稳态制备提供了通用判据，并特别关注微正则系综的近似制备。

Abstract: Stationary states of quantum many-body Hamiltonians are invariant under the Hamiltonian evolution. Besides ground and thermal states, this class includes microcanonical ensembles that are of fundamental importance in statistical physics. We consider the preparation of general stationary states by leveraging recent advances in the field of open-system dynamics. In particular, constructions based on exact KMS-detailed balance with respect to Gibbs states of noncommuting Hamiltonians have only recently been proposed as a tool for their efficient preparation and, by extension to small temperatures, for ground state preparation. We extend these constructions to the problem of stationary state preparation, providing general criteria that characterize when such states have efficient implementations, along with specific results on the approximation of microcanonical ensembles. An interesting application of our work are tests of conjectured ensemble equivalences for local observables between microcanonical and Gibbs ensembles.

### [70] [Valley-Aware Optimal Control of Spin Shuttling Using Cryogenic Integrated Electronics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20482)
*Pau Dietz Romero,Nermine Chaabani,Lammert Duipmans,Alessandro David,Felix Motzoi,Stefan van Waasen,Lotte Geck*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 论文提出了三个核心贡献：1）结合无序谷映射（disorder-informed valley maps）和晶体管级低温电路仿真的端到端协同仿真框架（co-simulation framework）；2）针对速度调制（velocity modulation）设计的全集成低温穿梭信号发生器，通过片上存储器存储离散电路设置实现周期波形整形；3）噪声感知优化程序（noise-aware optimization procedure），仅调整可实现的电路控制参数。

Result: 在协同仿真框架中，优化的速度调制波形显著提升了传输性能，在平均速度20 m/s、距离10 μm的条件下实现了99.99 ± 0.007%的平均穿梭保真度（shuttling fidelity），同时穿梭期间模拟功耗保持在数十微瓦级别。

Conclusion: 该研究验证了片上存储和回放优化控制设置作为缓解可扩展穿梭架构中谷无序（valley disorder）的实用策略，为低温环境下高保真度电子穿梭提供了有效的解决方案。

Abstract: Electron shuttling is emerging as a key mechanism for enabling long-range coupling in scalable spin-qubit architectures. Bringing shuttling waveform generation into the cryostat can improve scalability, but imposes strict area and power constraints on the control electronics. Concurrently, shuttling in Si/SiGe is further limited by a spatially varying valley splitting that induces spin--valley mixing and degrades coherence. Here, we make three contributions that address these limitations jointly: (i) an end-to-end co-simulation framework that combines disorder-informed valley maps with transistor-level cryogenic circuit simulations including electronic noise; (ii) a fully integrated cryogenic shuttling-signal generator tailored to velocity modulation, enabling period-wise waveform shaping through discrete circuit settings stored in on-chip memory; and (iii) a noise-aware optimization procedure that tunes only these implementable circuit controls, using one of four discrete resistor settings per period, to generate high-fidelity shuttling sequences. Across simulated valley and noise realizations in our co-simulation framework, the optimized velocity-modulation waveforms improve transport performance, achieving an average shuttling fidelity of $99.99 \pm 0.007\%$ at $v_{\mathrm{avg}} = 20~\mathrm{m\,s^{-1}}$ over a distance of $10~μ\mathrm{m}$, while maintaining active analog power consumption in the tens of $μ\mathrm{W}$ during shuttling. This validates on-chip storage and replay of optimized control settings as a practical strategy to mitigate valley disorder in scalable shuttling architectures.

### [71] [Reflections on Quantum Reflectometry: Quantum and Tunneling capacitances as well as Sisyphus and Hermes resistances](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20790)
*O. Yu. Kitsenko,S. N. Shevchenko,L. Peri,Franco Nori*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统反射测量法（reflectometry）通常在量子系统所有特征时间远小于谐振器周期时研究，此时仅探测稳态量子态。需要建立更严格的驱动耗散量子比特-谐振器系统描述，以处理子系统动力学相互依赖的情况。

Method: 提出量子比特（qudit）-谐振器系统的严格理论描述方法，明确引入量子电容（quantum capacitance）、隧穿电容（tunneling capacitance）以及Hermes和Sisyphus电阻。该方法适用于任何量子系统与经典谐振器的耦合。

Result: 展示了如何严格定义量子电容、隧穿电容以及Hermes和Sisyphus电阻，并分析这些参数在子系统动力学相互依赖时的变化。具体应用于库珀对盒（Cooper-pair box）、单库珀对晶体管（single-Cooper-pair transistor）、双量子点（double quantum dot）和单电子盒（single-electron box）等系统。

Conclusion: 该理论框架为量子系统与经典谐振器耦合提供了严格描述，能够处理子系统动力学相互依赖的情况，适用于广泛的量子电子器件反射测量分析。

Abstract: When a quantum electronic device is coupled to an electrical resonator, admittance changes of the quantum subsystem may be detected. The effective reactance may include capacitive and inductive terms that incorporate geometric, quantum, and tunneling components; while the effective resistance may be composed of Sisyphus and Hermes terms linked to relaxation and decoherence, respectively. Such reflectometry is usually studied when all characteristic times of the quantum system are much shorter than the resonator's period, in which case only stationary quantum states are probed. We present a rigorous description of a driven-dissipative qudit-resonator system. Our approach demonstrates how to strictly introduce quantum and tunneling capacitances as well as Hermes and Sisyphus resistances, and how these values are modified when the dynamics of the subsystems becomes mutually dependent. We present the cases of a Cooper-pair box, a single-Cooper-pair transistor, a double quantum dot, and a single-electron box. Our approach can be applied to describe any quantum system coupled to any classical resonator.

### [72] [Supersymmetry, Supergravity and Non--Perturbative Dynamics of Gauge Theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19817)
*Tetiana Obikhod*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文综述了超对称（supersymmetry）、超引力（supergravity）和规范理论（gauge theories）的非微扰动力学，从超对称代数（supersymmetry algebra）出发，最终探讨了弦理论（string theory）中的模稳定化（moduli stabilisation）和德西特真空（de Sitter vacua）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在系统回顾从超对称代数到弦理论中模稳定化和德西特真空的完整理论路径，涵盖超对称表示、超空间形式体系（superspace formalism）、非微扰规范理论动力学以及超引力构造等核心内容。

Method: 采用综述性分析方法，首先讨论超对称代数表示、超空间形式体系以及Wess-Zumino模型和N=1超对称杨-米尔斯理论（N=1 supersymmetric Yang-Mills theory）等基本模型。通过Seiberg-Witten解（Seiberg-Witten solution）分析N=2规范理论的非微扰动力学，包括曲线（curve）、预势（prepotential）、Picard-Fuchs系统（Picard-Fuchs system）、BPS谱（BPS spectrum）和通过单极子凝聚（monopole condensation）实现的禁闭（confinement）。

Result: 论文详细分析了KKLT模稳定化机制（KKLT moduli stabilisation mechanism），包括对Kähler势（Kähler potential）的α'^3修正。识别了标量势（scalar potential）的三个区域：经典KKLT、修正后具有移动AdS最小值的KKLT，以及失控区域（runaway regime）。确定了区分受控德西特真空与解紧致化（decompactification）的临界参数ξ̂_c，并讨论了与德西特沼泽地猜想（de Sitter swampland conjecture）的张力。

Conclusion: 该综述系统梳理了从超对称代数到弦理论中模稳定化和德西特真空的理论发展路径，展示了超对称、超引力和规范理论非微扰动力学之间的深刻联系，同时指出了当前理论框架与德西特沼泽地猜想之间的潜在冲突。

Abstract: We present a review of supersymmetry, supergravity, and the non-perturbative dynamics of gauge theories, tracing a path from the supersymmetry algebra to moduli stabilisation and de~Sitter vacua in string theory. Representations of the supersymmetry algebra, the superspace formalism, and basic models including the Wess--Zumino model and $\mathcal{N}=1$ supersymmetric Yang--Mills theory are discussed. The non-perturbative dynamics of $\mathcal{N}=2$ gauge theories is analysed through the Seiberg--Witten solution: the curve, prepotential, Picard--Fuchs system, BPS spectrum, and confinement via monopole condensation. The transition to $\mathcal{N}=1$ supergravity is carried out in three steps, showing how the Kähler potential $K$ and superpotential $W$ determine all five Lagrangian sectors and how the scalar potential acquires its exponential prefactor and gravitationally induced negative contribution. String theory applications include D-brane gauge theories, the AdS/CFT correspondence, geometric engineering of the Seiberg--Witten solution, and reduction of $\mathcal{N}=4$ to $\mathcal{N}=1$ supersymmetry. The KKLT moduli stabilisation mechanism is analysed in detail, including $α'^3$ corrections to the Kähler potential. Three regimes of the scalar potential are identified -- classical KKLT, corrected KKLT with a shifted AdS minimum, and a runaway regime -- and the critical parameter $\hatξ_c$ separating controlled de~Sitter vacua from decompactification is determined. The tension with the de~Sitter swampland conjecture is discussed.

*Konstantinos N. Anagnostopoulos,Takehiro Azuma,Mitsuaki Hirasawa,Jun Nishimura,Stratos Papadoudis,Asato Tsuchiya*

TL;DR: 本文通过复朗之万方法模拟了洛伦兹型IIB矩阵模型，克服了符号问题，发现模型存在一个相，其中涌现出(3+1)维平滑、真实的膨胀时空。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 洛伦兹型IIB矩阵模型是超弦理论非微扰表述的有力候选者，其中N×N玻色子矩阵A_μ的本征值分布代表涌现时空，由大N极限下的模型动力学决定。然而，该模型存在符号问题（sign problem）需要克服。

Method: 采用复朗之万方法（complex Langevin method）进行数值模拟，矩阵尺寸N达到128。为避免因积分掉费米子矩阵后出现的Pfaffian导致的奇异漂移问题（singular drift problem），作者受超对称变形启发对模型进行变形，类似于欧几里得情形下定义"极化型IIB矩阵模型"（polarized type IIB matrix model）的方法。

Result: 研究发现变形后的模型存在一个相，其中涌现出(3+1)维膨胀时空（(3+1)-dimensional expanding spacetime），且空间和时间都是平滑且真实的。

Conclusion: 通过克服符号问题和奇异漂移问题，成功模拟了洛伦兹型IIB矩阵模型，并发现模型能够自然涌现出(3+1)维平滑真实的膨胀时空结构，为超弦理论的非微扰表述提供了重要支持。

Abstract: The Lorentzian type IIB matrix model is a promising candidate for a nonperturbative formulation of superstring theory. In this model, the eigenvalue distribution of the $N\times N$ bosonic matrices $A_μ$ $(μ= 0 , \ldots , 9)$ represents an emergent spacetime, which is determined by the dynamics of the model in the large-$N$ limit. Here we perform numerical simulations of the model overcoming the sign problem by the complex Langevin method with the matrix size $N$ up to $128$. In order to avoid the singular drift problem due to the Pfaffian, which appears after integrating out the fermionic matrices, we deform the model in a manner inspired by the supersymmetric deformation, which is used to define the ``polarized type IIB matrix model'' in the Euclidean case. We find that the deformed model exhibits a phase in which (3+1)-dimensional expanding spacetime emerges with both space and time being smooth and real.

### [74] [Mutual Information from Modular Flow in General CFTs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19860)
*César A. Agón,Pablo Bueno,Adem Deniz Piskin,Guido van der Velde*

Main category: hep-th

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 真空互信息（mutual information）作为子区域代数的普适量，为研究一般共形场论（conformal field theories）提供了通用窗口。然而，需要更精确的方法来近似计算任意分离距离下的互信息，特别是在缺乏现有结果的高维情况下。

Method: 利用球状区域关联的模流（modular flow）的几何性质，以及复制对称性中扭曲算符（twist operators）的算子乘积展开（operator product expansion）。通过复制理论中任意自旋原初算子的两点函数来约束扭曲算符，从而构建互信息的层次化近似。

Result: 获得了任意维度d中任意加速球状区域互信息的贡献表达式。当涉及最低标度维度的原初算子时，该结果提供了互信息长距离行为的最精确近似，超越了所有先前展开。基于此结果和短/长距离区间的普适性质，提出了适用于任意分离距离的新高精度解析近似。

Conclusion: 该方法的准确性通过d=2精确结果和d=3晶格结果得到验证，并成功应用于d=4麦克斯韦场的互信息表征，为该领域提供了首个可用结果。所提出的高精度解析近似为共形场论中互信息研究提供了强有力的新工具。

Abstract: The vacuum mutual information (MI) of subregion algebras provides a universal window into the data of general conformal field theories (CFTs). Exploiting the geometric nature of the modular flow associated to ball-shaped regions and the operator product expansion of twist operators implementing the replica symmetry in an $n$-fold version of a CFT, it is possible to construct a hierarchy of increasingly refined approximations to the full MI. In this letter, we use the two-point functions of primaries of arbitrary spin in the replicated theory to constrain the twist operators, and find their contribution to the MI of arbitrarily boosted balls in any $d$-dimensional CFT. When the two-point functions involve the primary with the lowest scaling dimension, our result provides the most precise approximation for the long-distance behavior of the MI, superseding all previous expansions. Building upon this result and certain universal properties of the short- and long-distance regimes, we put forward a new high-precision analytic approximation to the MI for arbitrary separations. The accuracy of our approach is validated against exact $d=2$ and lattice $d=3$ results. We further apply it to characterize the MI of a $d=4$ Maxwell field, a case for which no prior results are available.

</details>


### [75] [Excitability in quantum field theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19861)
*Jacqueline Caminiti,Federico Capeccia,Jonathan Sorce*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文建立了量子理论中局域可激发性（local excitability）的抽象代数判据，并在广义自由场论（generalized free field theory）中对零均值高斯态（zero-mean Gaussian states）进行了显式计算。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在量子场论（quantum field theory）中，仅使用局域算子（local operators）从一个态激发到另一个态并不总是可行的。本文旨在建立一般量子理论中局域可激发性的抽象代数判据。

Method: 论文建立了局域可激发性的抽象代数判据，并针对广义自由场论中的零均值高斯态进行了显式计算。证明中关键使用了信息论工具——正则纯化（canonical purification）。

Result: 研究发现，在高斯态（Gaussian states）的特殊性质下，单向可激发性（one-way excitability）总是意味着双向可激发性（two-way excitability）。这些结果推广了Powers、Stormer、van Daele、Araki和Yamagami的"拟等价定理"（quasiequivalence theorems）。

Conclusion: 论文为量子理论中的局域可激发性提供了系统的代数框架，特别阐明了高斯态在这一框架下的特殊性质。附录部分提供了广义自由场论代数表述的教学性介绍。

Abstract: In quantum field theory, it is not always possible to excite one state out of another using only local operators. This paper establishes abstract algebraic criteria for (local) excitability in general quantum theories, and computes these criteria explicitly for zero-mean Gaussian states in (generalized) free field theories. We find that in this context, due to the special nature of Gaussian states, one-way excitability always implies two-way excitability, and our results generalize the "quasiequivalence theorems" of Powers, Stormer, van Daele, Araki, and Yamagami. A key role in our proof is played by the information-theoretic tool of canonical purification. In appendices, we provide a pedagogical introduction to the algebraic formulation of (generalized) free field theory.

</details>


### [76] [Asymptotic charges as detectors and the memory effect in massive QED and perturbative quantum gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19866)
*Brett Oertel,Ian Moult,Sabrina Pasterski*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究通过探测器方法重新推导了量子引力和量子电动力学中的无穷渐近对称性，并将其推广到包含外部硬引力子的情况。研究修正了文献中的不一致之处，并证明了Faddeev-Kulish dressing正确编码了散射Fock空间中的记忆效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子引力和量子电动力学已被证明存在无穷渐近对称性（infinite asymptotic symmetries），这些对称性在某些情况下已扩展到dressed states。本研究旨在通过探测器方法澄清、确认并推广这些结果，特别是包含外部硬引力子（external hard gravitons）的情况。

Method: 采用探测器方法并包含Faddeev-Kulish dressing中的完整时间依赖性（full t dependence），以此重新推导相关陈述。该方法能够修正文献中的不一致之处，并对渐近对称性理论做出新的表述。

Result: 研究表明Faddeev-Kulish dressing正确编码了"in"和"out"散射Fock空间中的记忆效应（memory effect）。研究发现dressing在两种情况下都对记忆特征值（memory eigenvalues）产生了物理贡献。

Conclusion: 通过探测器方法，研究澄清并推广了量子引力和QED中的渐近对称性理论，修正了文献中的不一致，并证明了Faddeev-Kulish dressing在编码记忆效应方面的正确性及其对记忆特征值的物理贡献。

Abstract: It has been shown that there are an infinite set of asymptotic symmetries in quantum gravity and QED, and this has been extended to dressed states in some cases. Here we rederive these statements in terms of detectors in order to clarify, confirm, and generalize these results to include external hard gravitons. Using detectors and including the full t dependence in Faddeev-Kulish dressings allows us to correct discrepancies in the literature and make new statements. We show that Faddeev-Kulish dressings correctly encode the memory effect in the 'in' and 'out' scattering Fock spaces. We find a physical contribution to the memory eigenvalues arising from the dressings in both cases.

### [77] [Crosscap Defects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19868)
*Nadav Drukker,Shota Komatsu,Anders Wallberg*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文引入了一类新的共形场论（CFT）缺陷，称为"交叉帽缺陷（crosscap defects）"，这是通过时空的$\mathbb{Z}_2$自同构商构造的，提供了实射影空间上CFT的高余维推广。作者分析了这些缺陷的共形块分解，并在$O(N)$模型的高斯和Wilson-Fisher固定点中进行了具体研究。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究的动机是扩展共形场论（conformal field theory, CFT）中缺陷结构的理论框架。作者旨在构建一类新型缺陷，这些缺陷源于时空的$\mathbb{Z}_2$自同构商，为实射影空间（$\mathbb{RP}^{d}$）上的CFT提供高余维推广，从而丰富缺陷共形场论的理论体系。

Method: 方法是通过对时空进行$\mathbb{Z}_2$自同构商来构造交叉帽缺陷（crosscap defects），这些缺陷沿着$\mathbb{Z}_2$作用的$p$维固定轨迹延伸。作者分析了该设置下算符的两点函数，识别了三种算符乘积展开（operator product expansion, OPE）通道：体（bulk）、镜像（image）和缺陷（defect）通道，并推导了相应的交叉帽交叉方程（crosscap crossing equations）。

Result: 研究结果表明，交叉帽缺陷的共形块（conformal blocks）与缺陷CFT块相同，仅需重新定义交叉比（cross ratios）。在$O(N)$模型的高斯和Wilson-Fisher固定点中，作者显式计算了与$p$相关的CFT数据，发现与标准缺陷不同，对于一般的$p$，位移（displacement）和倾斜（tilt）算符不存在。这些缺陷提供了没有精确边际算符（exactly marginal operators）的缺陷共形流形（defect conformal manifolds）的实例。

Conclusion: 该论文成功引入并分析了交叉帽缺陷这一新型缺陷类别，扩展了共形场论中缺陷结构的理论框架。这些缺陷不仅提供了实射影空间上CFT的高余维推广，还展示了与标准缺陷不同的特性，特别是位移和倾斜算符的缺失，为缺陷共形流形的研究提供了新范例。

Abstract: We introduce a novel class of defects, termed {\it crosscap defects}, in conformal field theory (CFT) in general dimensions. These arise from quotienting the spacetime by a $\mathbb{Z}_2$ automorphism, and provide higher-codimension generalisations of CFT on real projective space ($\mathbb{RP}^{d}$). Crosscap defects extend along a $p$-dimensional fixed locus of the $\mathbb{Z}_2$ action and preserve an $SO(p+1,1)\times PO(d-p)$ subgroup of the conformal group. The two-point functions of operators in this setup exhibit three operator product expansion channels: bulk, image, and defect. These lead to several {\it crosscap crossing equations}, which we present. We analyse conformal block decompositions and show that the blocks are identical to defect CFT blocks up to a redefinition of cross ratios. As concrete examples, we study crosscap defects in the $O(N)$ model at the Gaussian and Wilson--Fisher fixed points in the $\varepsilon$-expansion. We compute explicitly the associated CFT data as a function of $p$ and find that, unlike standard defects, displacement and tilt operators are absent for generic $p$. They provide examples of defect conformal manifolds without exactly marginal operators.

At strong coupling, we employ the dual D5-brane solutions in Euclidean signature, where the defect is supported on an $S^2$ submanifold of the Euclidean $AdS_3\times S^1$ boundary. At weak coupling, we use the classical solutions of the ${\cal N}=4$ SYM equations of motion, previously conjectured to describe the defects dual to the D5-brane configurations. Notably, the coefficient $b$ is found to be negative in a finite region of parameter space. To our knowledge, this constitutes the first explicit example of an {\it interacting} unitary dCFT with $b<0$.
  We also compute the type-B Weyl anomaly coefficients associated with the extrinsic curvature of the defects, first at strong coupling and subsequently at weak coupling. In a certain limit, we find agreement between the weak- and strong-coupling results for both the type-A and type-B anomaly coefficients.

### [79] [On non-relativistic integrable models and 4d SCFTs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19885)

Method: 通过将S类理论的广义Schur指数用椭圆Jack函数（elliptic Jack functions）表达，例如在A1情况下指数自然地用Lamé方程的本征函数表示，并利用本征函数表达式验证Deligne-Cvitanović系列中不同理论间的映射关系。

Result: 研究发现不同理论的广义Schur指数可以相互映射，这暗示了与不同根系相关的非相对论椭圆Calogero-Moser模型本征函数的非平凡恒等式，并表明各种可积模型的非相对论极限自然地产生N=1 SCFTs类的广义Schur-like极限。

In particular we discuss explicitly how to express generalized Schur indices of theories of class $S$ in terms of elliptic Jack functions. For example, in the $A_1$ case the indices are given naturally in terms of eigenfunctions of the Lamé equation. We use the expression in terms of eigenfunctions to further check the recent observation that the generalized Schur indices of different theories in the Deligne-Cvitanović series can be mapped onto each other. This mapping implies non trivial identities on unrefined sums of eigenfunctions of non-relativistic elliptic Calogero-Moser models associated to different root systems. We claim then that the non-relativistic limits of various integrable models give rise naturally to generalized Schur-like limits of classes of $N=1$ SCFTs. As an example we discuss the relation of the Inozemtsev model, the non relativistic limit of the van Diejen model, and compactifications of the rank $Q$ E-string theory. We argue that in general the ``Schur index'' of $N=1$ $4d$ SCFTs can be understood as being related to the free fermionic limit of a non-relativistic integrable model.

### [80] [Black Hole Interiors as a Laboratory for Time-Dependent Classical Double Copy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19920)
*Damien A. Easson,Tucker Manton*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文证明了黑洞几何的俘获区域为时间依赖的经典双重拷贝（classical double copy）提供了精确场景，其中静态球对称情况下的每个俘获区间在相关的Kantowski-Sachs斑块上具有局部单拷贝描述，该描述本质上是时间依赖的，但可以从静态Kerr-Schild数据推导得出。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典双重拷贝在引力和规范理论之间建立了重要桥梁，但其最明确的实现仍局限于稳态或高度对称的设置。本研究旨在探索时间依赖的经典双重拷贝的精确实现场景。

Method: 通过分析黑洞几何的俘获区域（trapped regions），证明在静态球对称情况下，每个俘获区间在相关的Kantowski-Sachs斑块上具有局部单拷贝描述。该方法基于Kerr-Schild数据，无需外部黑洞完成的知识。

Result: 研究发现此类俘获区域由Kantowski-Sachs尺度因子之间的特殊关系（等价于纵向关系p∥=-ρ）表征，且Kerr-Schild标量和单拷贝场可以从内部宇宙学数据唯一重构。Schwarzschild解提供奇异基准，而规则的Bardeen解在整个俘获区域产生有限单拷贝场并平滑延伸到规则静态核心。

Conclusion: 俘获的Kerr-Schild内部区域为时间依赖的经典双重拷贝提供了精确的局部实验室，Bardeen解的视界相结构编码在单拷贝标量中，这扩展了经典双重拷贝的应用范围。

Abstract: The classical double copy provides a powerful bridge between gravity and gauge theory, but its most explicit realizations remain concentrated in stationary or highly symmetric settings. We show that trapped regions of black-hole geometries furnish an exact setting for time-dependent classical double copy. In the static, spherically symmetric case, each trapped interval admits a local single-copy description on the associated Kantowski--Sachs patch that is intrinsically time dependent, although it can be derived from static Kerr--Schild data and does not require knowledge of any exterior black-hole completion. We prove that this class is characterized intrinsically by a distinguished relation between the Kantowski--Sachs scale factors, equivalently by the longitudinal relation \(p_{\parallel}=-ρ\), and that the Kerr--Schild scalar and single-copy field are uniquely reconstructible from interior cosmological data. Schwarzschild provides the singular benchmark, for which the single-copy electric field diverges along the interior evolution, while the regular Bardeen solution yields a finite single-copy field throughout the trapped region and a smooth extension into a regular static core. The Bardeen core violates the strong energy condition in a compact region, whereas the corresponding single-copy Maxwell field remains regular and satisfies the standard classical energy conditions. We further show that the Bardeen horizon phase structure is encoded in the single-copy scalar. These results identify trapped Kerr--Schild interiors as an exact local laboratory for time-dependent classical double copy.

### [81] [Geometric Amplitudes: A Covariant Functional Approach for Massless Scalar Theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20099)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过进一步修改无质量标量场理论中的关联函数，研究框架有效所需的条件，并探讨该构造的几何解释。该方法优先考虑可观测量在场重定义下的协变变换，而非度规张量（metric tensor）及其导数的作用。

Result: 成功实现了无质量标量场理论中关联函数的"离壳"协变性，并阐明了该框架有效所需的条件及其几何解释。然而，虽然类似修改可能存在于有质量理论，但本文开发的框架无法直接推广到该情况。

Conclusion: 功能几何框架可以扩展至实现无质量标量场理论中关联函数的"离壳"协变性，但该扩展具有局限性，无法直接应用于有质量理论。该构造强调可观测量协变变换的优先性，为量子场论中的几何理解提供了新视角。

Abstract: Functional geometry is a framework using concepts from geometry to understand the invariance of amplitudes in quantum field theory under a large class of field redefinitions, including those involving derivatives. It is inspired by recursion relations among correlation functions, where higher-point functions depend iteratively upon smaller correlators. Previous work has shown that, with suitable modifications, these correlation functions become covariant under field redefinitions, provided they are evaluated at the physical ``on-shell" point. In this paper, we show how to further modify correlation functions in massless scalar field theories to achieve ``off-shell" covariance. We investigate the conditions required for the framework to work and discuss the geometric interpretation of this construction -- which prioritizes the covariant transformation of observables under field redefinitions over the role of a metric tensor and its derivatives. While analogous modifications may exist for massive theories, we show that framework developed here does not extend straightforwardly to that case.

*Naman Kumar*

Main category: hep-th

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究在合理假设下分析通用紧凑岛（universal compact islands）的构造可行性，特别关注内部伙伴熵（interior partner entropy）在固定紧凑区域内的积累及其与半经典熵界（semiclassical entropy bounds）的兼容性。

Result: 通用性迫使内部伙伴熵在固定紧凑区域内积累，晚期会超过由其边界面积设定的贝肯斯坦-霍金界限（Bekenstein-Hawking bound）。然而，至少一个辐射区域的有效岛实现需要与半经典熵界兼容，这导致了矛盾。

Conclusion: 研究得出了通用紧凑岛（universal compact islands）的条件性不可行结果（conditional no-go result），表明岛框架中的内部重建（interior reconstruction）必须保持内在的区域依赖性（region-dependent）。

Abstract: Entanglement islands resolve the AMPS firewall paradox in a region-dependent manner by modifying the entanglement wedge of Hawking radiation. We investigate whether this resolution can be made universal, in the sense that a single compact island serves as a common interior support for all AMPS-relevant radiation regions. We show that such a construction is obstructed under reasonable assumptions. Universality forces an accumulation of interior partner entropy within a fixed compact region, which at late times exceeds the Bekenstein--Hawking bound set by its boundary area. However, a valid island realization for at least one radiation region requires compatibility with semiclassical entropy bounds. This leads to a contradiction, yielding a conditional no-go result for universal compact islands. Our result implies that interior reconstruction in the island framework must remain intrinsically region-dependent.

### [83] [Computational Cosmic Censorship](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20170)
*Fuat Berkin Altunkaynak*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究提出AdS/CFT对应中弱宇宙监督原理的计算表述，通过复杂度=作用量方案分析过荷Reissner-Nordström-AdS时空中的裸奇点，发现奇点处的Gibbons-Hawking-York项发散导致全息复杂度无限，表明裸奇点因局部奇点结构产生无限计算成本而被排除。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在建立AdS/CFT对应中弱宇宙监督原理（weak cosmic censorship）的计算表述，探讨裸类时奇点（naked timelike singularities）在引力-全息对应中的可接受性。

Method: 采用复杂度=作用量方案（complexity=action proposal），计算包含裸奇点的过荷Reissner-Nordström-AdS时空的Wheeler-DeWitt作用量，分析体项、零项、连接项和奇点处Gibbons-Hawking-York项的贡献。

Result: 发现体项、零项和连接项保持有限，而奇点处的Gibbons-Hawking-York项发散；对于满足$f(r)\sim a r^{-p}$且$p>D-3$的静态球对称几何，奇点项均发散，导致全息复杂度（holographic complexity）发散，相对于对数发散的极端荷电扇区形成无限复杂度间隙。

Conclusion: 裸奇点不仅因几何原因被排除，更因其局部近奇点结构产生无限计算成本而被操作性地禁止，这为弱宇宙监督原理提供了基于计算复杂度的新解释。

Abstract: We propose a computational formulation of weak cosmic censorship in AdS/CFT. Using the complexity=action proposal, we evaluate the Wheeler-DeWitt action for overcharged Reissner- Nordström-AdS spacetimes containing naked timelike singularities. We show that the bulk, null, and joint contributions remain finite, while the Gibbons-Hawking-York term at the singularity diverges. More generally, for any static and spherically symmetric geometry with near-origin scaling $f(r)\sim a r^{-p}$, the singularity term diverges whenever $p>D-3$. This implies divergent holographic complexity and, even relative to the logarithmically divergent extremal charged sector, leaves an infinite complexity gap. This suggests an operational form of censorship: naked singularities are excluded not by geometry alone, but by an infinite computational cost arising from their local near-singularity structure.

Abstract: In this letter, we focus on the application of the off-shell recursion method proposed in \cite{Tao:2025fch} in the Yang-Mills planar loop integrands, which starts with solving the classical equation of motion via the perturbiner method. This matrix formalism not only makes the off-shell structure of the Yang-Mills planar integrands clearer, but also has potential use in finding amplitude relations at higher-loop levels. Abstract: We study the drag force acting on a heavy quark in a holographic plasma with rotational anisotropy and finite density. The bulk dual is the CCLP black hole of five-dimensional minimal gauged supergravity, characterised by two independent rotation parameters and electric charge. In the neutral Kerr--AdS limit, we use the principal Killing string to obtain an exact drag force for arbitrary rotation parameters. Abstract: We present a non-Abelian model for magnetic monopoles in inhomogeneous media, based on a generalization of the standard 't~Hooft-Polyakov model. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在封闭量子系统中，Krylov复杂度（Krylov complexity）具有几何描述，但需要研究环境耦合如何改变这一图像。本文旨在探索开放系统中算子增长（operator growth）的动力学特性。

Method: 采用Schwinger-Keldysh公式描述Krylov位置的全计数统计（full counting statistics），推导出Lindblad动力学下算子增长的有效作用量（effective action）。即使是最简单的退相干（dephasing）情况，也分析了相空间动力学的变化。

Result: 环境耦合导致相空间动力学不再是哈密顿型，在Krylov深度的共轭变量中产生扩散（diffusion），将确定性轨迹转变为随机轨迹。支撑指数复杂度增长的hyperbolic机制被拓宽，并在参数控制尺度之外被破坏。

Conclusion: 耗散（dissipation）被识别为混沌Krylov不动点（chaotic Krylov fixed point）的相关扰动，揭示了开放系统中算子增长是涌现相空间（emergent phase space）中随机动力学的问题。

Abstract: In closed quantum systems, Krylov complexity admits a geometric description; operator growth is equivalent to Hamiltonian flow in an emergent phase space whose structure is fixed by the Lanczos coefficients. We show that this picture survives, albeit in a fundamentally altered form, once the system is coupled to an environment.Using a Schwinger-Keldysh formulation of the full counting statistics of the Krylov position, we derive an effective action for operator growth under Lindblad dynamics. Even for the minimal case of dephasing, the phase-space dynamics ceases to be Hamiltonian; environmental coupling generates diffusion in the variable conjugate to Krylov depth, converting deterministic trajectories in to stochastic ones. The hyperbolic mechanism underlying exponential complexity growth is therefore broadened and, beyond a parametrically controlled scale, destroyed.This identifies dissipation as a relevant perturbation of the chaotic Krylov fixed point and reveals operator growth in open systems as a problem of stochastic dynamics in an emergent phase space.

In AdS$_3$/CFT$_2$, however, this picture is incomplete because of additional degrees of freedom, called singletons, associated with boundary diffeomorphisms. We present a general procedure for extending the BPS spectrum of supergravitons by dressing them with singletons, thereby defining a generalized, gravity-sector Hilbert space that admits decomposition into affine multiplets of the full superconformal algebra. This extends the procedure previously proposed in arXiv:2505.14888 which was applicable only at low levels, by removing that limitation. We apply the new procedure to the D1-D5 CFT ${\rm Sym}^N(T^4)$ and explicitly construct affine multiplets in the gravity sector for the $N=2$ theory up to level $h=2$. We find that, at the free orbifold point, the gravity-sector spectrum agrees with the CFT up to $h=\frac12$. Upon turning on a deformation, however, states at $h=1$ lift and the agreement improves to $h=\frac32$. Interestingly, the lifting occurs between states in the gravity sector, involving mixtures of supergravitons and singletons, and stringy states. We conjecture that, upon deformation, the gravity-sector Hilbert space becomes the monotone Hilbert space while its complement becomes the fortuitous Hilbert space.

Abstract: We study the instanton counting in four dimensional $\mathcal{N}=2$ supersymmetric gauge theories on the blow-up of $\mathbb{C}^2$: we start by formulating the instanton moduli space as a quiver variety, which we regularise by introducing two stability parameters, thus endowing it with a structure of infinitely many chambers separated by walls. Within a given chamber, we formulate the instanton partition function as a contour integral, which can be evaluated using the Jeffrey-Kirwan residue prescription. We characterise the physically relevant contributions in terms of bipartite oriented graphs and show that they can more efficiently be classified in terms of combinatorial objects called super-partitions. Within a given chamber, only certain types of super-partitions contribute and we show that the corresponding selection criteria are equivalent to stability conditions that have previously been proposed in the literature. We use this formalism to compare how the instanton counting changes when moving across walls between neighbouring chambers and provide explicit expressions for the corresponding partition functions. In a limiting chamber and using our approach, we show how to reproduce the Nakajima-Yoshioka blow-up formula.

In this work, we consider two non-relativistic Bose-Einstein condensates (formed inside of harmonic trap potentials with identical trapping frequencies) separated by a distance. We take a linearized quantum gravity model and investigate the generation of entanglement while gravitons serve as the mediator of entanglement. The entanglement is generated between the phonon modes of the two condensates, and we observe that for very low separation distance, the entanglement generated is significantly higher than that observed for the quantum gravity induced entanglement of masses or QGEM protocol; however, the fall of entanglement is faster than the two-particle case for two separated Bose-Einstein condensates. We observe that when the number of particles in the condensate is increased, the degree of entanglement for a smaller separation distance becomes substantially higher compared to the case discussed in \href{https://doi.org/10.1103/PhysRevD.105.106028}{Phys. Rev. D 105 (2022) 106028}, which allows for a more robust experimental proposal using this quantum gravity induced entanglement of phonons or QGEP protocol.

Motivation: 研究动机是应用调和分析方法系统研究$T\bar{T}$-形变（$T\bar{T}$-deformation）下的环面配分函数（torus partition function），以清晰解析其作为形变参数$λ$的函数的解析结构。

Method: 方法首先将共形场论（CFT）配分函数用Maass波形（Maass waveforms）表示，包括Eisenstein级数和尖点形式（cusp forms）。这些基函数在$T\bar{T}$-形变下呈现简单形变行为，通过谱分解（spectral decomposition）提供数值稳定高效的计算框架。

Result: 结果显示形变配分函数表现出Hagedorn奇点（Hagedorn singularity）。基于调和分析方法，研究提出了超越Hagedorn奇点的自然解析延拓（analytic continuation），使得能够计算任意$λ$值下的完整配分函数。

Conclusion: 结论表明调和分析方法为研究$T\bar{T}$-形变配分函数提供了有效框架，不仅揭示了其解析结构中的Hagedorn奇点，还实现了超越奇点的解析延拓，为理解形变理论提供了新视角。

Abstract: We apply harmonic analysis to study the $T\bar{T}$-deformed torus partition function. We first express the CFT partition functions in terms of Maass waveforms, including the Eisenstein series and cusp forms. These basis functions turn out to deform in a very simple way under the $T\bar{T}$-deformation. The spectral decomposition provides a numerically stable and efficient method to compute the partition function at finite values of the deformation parameter $λ$, allowing us to clearly resolve the analytic structure of the partition function as a function of $λ$. The resulting deformed partition function exhibits a Hagedorn singularity. Building on harmonic analysis approach, we propose a natural analytic continuation beyond the Hagedorn singularity, which enables us to compute the full partition function for any value of $λ$.

</details>

# cs.AI [[Back]](#toc)

### [94] [From Data to Theory: Autonomous Large Language Model Agents for Materials Science](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19789)
*Samuel Onimpa Alfred,Veera Sundararaghavan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种自主大语言模型（LLM）代理，用于端到端的数据驱动材料理论开发。该代理能够自主选择方程形式、生成并运行代码、评估理论与数据的匹配度，无需人工干预。研究展示了该框架在已知材料关系（如Hall-Petch方程）中的成功应用，以及在更复杂关系中的表现，同时指出了自主代理在科学建模中的潜力与局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在开发一种自主大语言模型代理，用于实现端到端的数据驱动材料理论开发。该研究试图解决传统科学建模中需要大量人工干预的问题，探索人工智能辅助科学发现的新途径。

Method: 该方法结合了逐步推理（step-by-step reasoning）与专家提供的工具，构建了一个自主LLM代理框架。该代理能够自主选择方程形式、生成并运行代码、测试理论与数据的匹配度，同时保持决策过程的清晰记录。

Result: 对于已确立的材料关系如Hall-Petch方程和Paris定律，代理能够正确识别控制方程并在新数据集上做出可靠预测。对于更专门的关系如Kuhn方程（描述共轭分子HOMO-LUMO能隙随长度的变化），性能更依赖于底层模型，其中GPT-5表现出更好的方程恢复能力。代理还能够提出新的预测关系，如应变依赖的HOMO-LUMO能隙变化规律。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，自主LLM代理在AI辅助科学建模和发现方面具有潜力，但仍存在局限性。即使数值拟合效果良好，代理仍可能返回不正确、不完整或不一致的方程，因此仔细验证仍然至关重要。这些结果凸显了自主代理在科学发现中的前景与当前限制。

Abstract: We present an autonomous large language model (LLM) agent for end-to-end, data-driven materials theory development. The model can choose an equation form, generate and run its own code, and test how well the theory matches the data without human intervention. The framework combines step-by-step reasoning with expert-supplied tools, allowing the agent to adjust its approach as needed while keeping a clear record of its decisions. For well-established materials relationships such as the Hall-Petch equation and Paris law, the agent correctly identifies the governing equation and makes reliable predictions on new datasets. For more specialized relationships, such as Kuhn's equation for the HOMO-LUMO gap of conjugated molecules as a function of length, performance depends more strongly on the underlying model, with GPT-5 showing better recovery of the correct equation. Beyond known theories, the agent can also suggest new predictive relationships, illustrated here by a strain-dependent law for changes in the HOMO-LUMO gap. At the same time, the results show that careful validation remains essential, because the agent can still return incorrect, incomplete, or inconsistent equations even when the numerical fit appears strong. Overall, these results highlight both the promise and the current limitations of autonomous LLM agents for AI-assisted scientific modeling and discovery.

</details>

The search targets production in association with a hard photon and uses the feature that a light gauge-singlet can only decay into a small number of hadronic channels, yielding jets with anomalously low charged-track multiplicity and mass compared to QCD jets at the same transverse momentum. This search extends the reach to hadronically-coupled particles into a previously inaccessible regime.

Abstract: In this Letter we explore the modelling of hadron production in electromagnetic ion dissociation (EMD) processes in high-energy ultraperipheral collisions at LHC energies. Since EMD can accompany exclusive particle production in these interactions, we demonstrate that the resulting hadrons can break the exclusivity vetos typically imposed by experiments. As two representative examples, we calculate the impact on existing LHC measurements of exclusive muon pair production ($γγ\toμμ$) and exclusive coherent $J/ψ$ production. We demonstrate that accounting for this effect resolves long-standing tensions between theoretical predictions and experimental measurements.

### [97] [Ultra-High-Energy Tau Neutrinos as Probes of Lorentz Invariance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19880)
*Vedran Brdar,Samiur R. Mir*
