<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 中微子望远镜已探测到能量高达约100 PeV的天体物理中微子，而当前和计划中的实验旨在观测更高能量的中微子以探测宇宙学中微子。随着中微子能量的增加，检验洛伦兹不变性破坏（Lorentz invariance violation, LIV）变得尤为吸引人，因为高维LIV算符对中微子传播的影响随能量快速增长。

Method: 使用SimProp生成宇宙学中微子通量，并将其与存在LIV效应时中微子味转换概率的计算相结合。通过分析标准味转换概率的偏差如何表现为GRAND和POEMMA实验中预期的τ中微子事件率变化来探测LIV效应。

Result: 首先考虑单个非零LIV算符（不同维度）的情况，发现GRAND和POEMMA的预期灵敏度比现有低能探测器的限制高出数个数量级。随后探索多个非零LIV参数的情景，表明参数间的相互作用相比单参数情况能显著改变灵敏度。

Conclusion: 总体而言，即将开展的超高能τ中微子观测将对LIV施加最严格的约束之一，为检验基本物理对称性提供重要机遇。

Abstract: Neutrino telescopes have detected astrophysical neutrinos with energies up to ${O}(100)$ PeV. Several current and proposed experiments aim to observe neutrinos at even higher energies, with the goal of detecting cosmogenic neutrinos. This increase in neutrino energy makes tests of Lorentz invariance violation (LIV) particularly appealing, since the effects of higher-dimension LIV operators on neutrino propagation grow rapidly with energy. In this work, we investigate the potential of the upcoming experiments GRAND and POEMMA to probe LIV in the neutrino sector through the detection of ultra-high-energy tau neutrinos. We generate the cosmogenic neutrino flux using SimProp and interface it with a calculation of neutrino flavor transition probabilities in the presence of LIV effects. Deviations from standard flavor transition probabilities manifest as changes in the expected tau neutrino event rates at GRAND and POEMMA. We first consider the case with a single nonzero LIV operator of various dimensions, and find that the projected sensitivities exceed existing limits from lower-energy probes by orders of magnitude. We then explore scenarios with multiple nonzero LIV parameters and show that their interplay can significantly modify the sensitivities compared to the single-parameter case. Overall, we find that upcoming observations of ultra-high-energy tau neutrinos will place some of the most stringent constraints on LIV.

### [98] [Technically Natural Suppression of Fifth Force](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20292)
*Kensuke Homma,Taishi Katsuragawa,Shinya Matsuzaki*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于对称性的第五力抑制机制，通过Z2对称的镜像标准模型扩展和双共形引力构造，产生作为赝Nambu-Goldstone玻色子的轻标量子，其耦合强度与质量之间存在参数无关的关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 轻标量子通常介导与局部引力测试不相容的第五力，除非其耦合参数被抑制或引入屏蔽机制。研究旨在探索基于对称性而非非线性标量动力学的抑制机制。

Method: 提出在双共形引力构造中的Z2对称镜像标准模型扩展，其中标度不变性的自发破缺产生作为赝Nambu-Goldstone玻色子的轻标量子。该标量子耦合到标准模型和镜像扇区之间的迹反常差异。

Result: 发现第五力强度α与标量子质量mσ之间存在参数无关的关联，比例由QCD可观测量和电弱标度设定。标准模型预测在米尺度上α∼10⁻⁴，对应mσ∼10⁻⁷ eV，恰好位于下一代实验的目标窗口内。

Conclusion: 与基于环境屏蔽的机制不同，该抑制机制直接源于对称性而非非线性标量动力学，为第五力抑制提供了新的理论框架，其预测可直接通过下一代实验进行检验。

Abstract: Light scalars generically mediate a fifth force incompatible with local tests of gravity unless their couplings are parametrically suppressed or screening mechanisms are introduced. We demonstrate that such suppression can arise from symmetry. We propose a $Z_2$-symmetric mirror extension of the Standard Model within a bi-conformal gravity construction, where spontaneous breaking of scale invariance produces a light scalaron as a pseudo-Nambu-Goldstone boson. This scalaron couples to the difference of trace anomalies between the Standard Model and mirror sectors. We find a parameter-independent correlation between the fifth-force strength $α$ and the scalaron mass $m_σ$, with the proportionality set by QCD observables and the electroweak scale. The Standard Model predicts $α\sim 10^{-4}$ at meter scales for $m_σ\sim 10^{-7}$ eV, which is directly in the target window of next-generation experiments. In contrast to environmental screening mechanisms, this suppression mechanism follows directly from symmetry rather than nonlinear scalar dynamics.

### [99] [Baryon-Meson Sum Rule for $b \to s ν\barν$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20340)
*Teppei Kitahara,Manas Kumar Mohapatra,Kota Sasaki*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文推导了Λ_b→Λνν̄和B→K^(*)νν̄衰变分支比之间的稳健求和规则（sum rule），该关系在右手微中子解耦假设下成立，且与有效哈密顿量中的18个独立威尔逊系数无关。该重子-介子求和规则的系数与b→c半轻子衰变中的相应求和规则系数数值相同。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索重子与介子b→sνν̄跃迁过程之间的关联，为区分不同新物理（new-physics）场景提供理论工具。特别是在右手微中子（right-handed neutrinos）解耦的假设下，建立模型无关的预测关系。

Method: 方法基于有效场论框架，在右手微中子解耦的假设下，推导Λ_b→Λνν̄和B→K^(*)νν̄衰变分支比之间的精确求和规则。该推导考虑了有效哈密顿量中的18个独立威尔逊系数（Wilson coefficients），但最终关系与这些系数无关。

Result: 主要结果发现：1）重子-介子求和规则的系数与b→c半轻子衰变中Λ_b→Λ_cτν̄和B→D^(*)τν̄的求和规则系数数值相同；2）一旦测量B→K^*νν̄的衰变率，即可在仅涉及左手微中子相互作用的新物理场景下，以模型无关的方式确定Λ_b→Λνν̄的衰变率。

Conclusion: 结论表明，重子与介子的b→sνν̄跃迁可观测量将成为区分不同新物理场景的有力探针。该求和规则为检验超出标准模型（beyond Standard Model）的物理提供了新的理论约束和实验验证途径。

Abstract: We derive a robust sum rule among the branching fractions of $Λ_b \to Λν\barν$ and $B \to K^{(\ast)} ν\barν$, assuming that right-handed neutrinos are decoupled. Despite the presence of 18 independent Wilson coefficients in the effective Hamiltonian, this relation remains exact. Remarkably, it is found that the coefficients of this baryon-meson sum rule are numerically identical to those of the $b\to c$ semileptonic sum rule among the branching fractions of $Λ_b \to Λ_c τ\barν$ and $B \to D^{(\ast)}τ\barν$. Once the decay rate of $B \to K^{\ast} ν\barν$ is measured, the decay rate of $Λ_b \to Λν\barν$ can be determined in a model-independent manner for new-physics scenarios involving only left-handed neutrino interactions. This clearly demonstrates that observables in baryonic and mesonic $b \to s ν\barν$ transitions will serve as a powerful probe for discriminating among new-physics scenarios.

Abstract: Semi-visible jets (SVJs) provide a characteristic collider signature of strongly interacting dark sectors, in which the key model parameter $r_{\mathrm{inv}}$ controls the fraction of dark hadrons decaying to dark matter candidates. The performance is found to be robust against varying signal parameters and $r_{\mathrm{inv}}$ can be reconstructed at a much higher precision, compared to previously developed analytical method. It offers a new approach to conduct SVJ searches that can potentially unify both $s$-channel and $t$-channel productions, enhancing the sensitivities.

### [101] [Graph-theoretic determination of massless modes in latticized theory-space models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20138)

Main category: hep-ph

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于为格点化理论空间模型（包括维度解构产生的链模型）中的费米子质量谱提供系统分析方法。该方法旨在揭示无质量模式的数量和局域化特性如何仅由理论空间的拓扑结构决定，而不依赖于具体模型参数。

Method: 方法核心是将费米子质量项映射到二分图（bipartite graph），其中场作为顶点，非零质量项作为边。通过分析图的最大匹配（maximum matching）和Dulmage-Mendelsohn分解，确定无质量模式的数量和波函数支撑集。

Result: 结果表明，无质量模式的数量由关联图的最大匹配基数固定。这些模式的波函数支撑集被限制在可通过偶数长度最大匹配交替路径从暴露或未匹配顶点到达的场上，这一特性由Dulmage-Mendelsohn分解表征。

Conclusion: 结论指出该方法仅依赖于格点化理论空间的拓扑结构，与模型参数无关。它使得能够系统构建具有预定数量和无质量模式局域化特性的格点化模型，为理论设计提供了图论工具。

Abstract: A graph-theoretic method is introduced for analyzing fermion mass spectra in latticized theory-space models, including chain models arising from dimensional deconstruction. Fermion mass terms are mapped to bipartite graphs, with fields as vertices and nonvanishing mass terms as edges. The number of massless modes is shown to be fixed by the cardinality of a maximum matching of the associated graph. Moreover, the wave-function support of these modes is restricted to fields reachable from exposed or unmatched vertices by even-length maximum-matching-alternating paths, as characterized by the Dulmage-Mendelsohn decomposition. These results depend only on the topology of latticized theory space and are independent of model parameters. The method enables a systematic construction of latticized models with prescribed numbers and localization properties of massless modes.

</details>


### [102] [Search for Axion Like Particles produced via the Primakoff process at COMPASS](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20734)
*Mehran Dehpour*

Main category: hep-ph

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 轴子样粒子（Axion-Like Particles, ALPs）是暗物质（dark matter）的有力候选者，并可能作为暗物质区（dark sector）的媒介粒子。本研究旨在通过重新解释COMPASS实验数据，探索ALPs与光子的耦合。

Method: 利用COMPASS实验2009年数据集，包括190 GeV的π⁻和μ⁻束流轰击固定镍靶，研究ALPs的Primakoff产生过程。由于高束流能量，MeV质量范围的ALPs产生显著洛伦兹增强（Lorentz boost），导致衰变光子高度准直，在电磁量能器中无法空间分辨，被重建为单个合并簇（merged cluster）。

Result: 通过量化标准模型Primakoff康普顿散射（Primakoff Compton scattering）样本中潜在的ALP污染，在质量范围0.2 ≲ m_a ≲ 600 MeV内推导出ALP-光子耦合g_{aγγ}的排除限。在95%置信水平下排除g_{aγγ} ≳ 10⁻¹ GeV⁻¹的耦合强度。

Conclusion: 研究结果为连接束流倾注实验（beam dump experiments）和高能对撞机的参数空间提供了独立约束。虽然当前对撞机限制更为严格，但本研究建立了新颖的重新解释框架，为未来在互补运动学区域（如Primakoff π⁰产生）研究分辨的双光子态提供了基准。

Abstract: Axion-Like Particles (ALPs) are well-motivated candidates for dark matter and potential mediators to the dark sector. We present a search for ALPs coupled to photons, based on a reinterpretation of COMPASS data. Using the 2009 dataset consisting of $190~\text{GeV}$ $π^-$ and $μ^-$ beams impinging on a fixed nickel target, we investigate the Primakoff production of ALPs. Due to the high beam energy, ALPs in the MeV mass range are produced with a significant Lorentz boost, leading to strongly collimated decay photons. Consequently, these photons are not spatially resolved by the electromagnetic calorimeter and are instead reconstructed as a single merged cluster. This signature mimics the single-photon signal of Standard Model Primakoff Compton scattering, which was the primary focus of the original COMPASS analysis. By quantifying this potential ALP contamination in the Compton scattering sample, we derive exclusion limits on the ALP-photon coupling $g_{aγγ}$ in the mass range $0.2 \lesssim m_a \lesssim 600~\text{MeV}$. Our results exclude couplings $g_{aγγ} \gtrsim 10^{-1}~\text{GeV}^{-1}$ at 95% C.L., providing independent constraints on the parameter space that bridges beam dump experiments and high energy colliders. While current collider-based limits remain more stringent, this work establishes a novel reinterpretation framework and provides a baseline for future studies of resolved diphoton states in complementary kinematic regimes, such as Primakoff $π^0$ production.

</details>


### [103] [Probing QCD instantons using jet correlation observables in proton-proton collisions at the LHC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20780)
*Sayak Guin,Swagatam Tah,Nihar Ranjan Sahoo,Sayantan Sharma*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种在LHC能级的pp对撞中区分瞬子（instanton）诱导过程与微扰硬散射事件的喷注关联观测量，并为未来电子-离子对撞机（EIC）的测量提供了直接应用方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在加速器中探测瞬子（instanton）将为QCD真空的拓扑性质提供实验证据。当前需要能够明确区分瞬子诱导过程与微扰硬散射事件的观测方法。

Method: 研究提出了喷注关联观测量（jet correlation observables），并计算了在具有物理夸克质量的2+1味QCD中瞬子的大小及其间距，从而对瞬子诱导过程中产生的强子的质心能量提供约束。

Result: 该方法能够在LHC能级的pp对撞中明确区分瞬子诱导过程与微扰硬散射事件。研究结果为未来电子-离子对撞机（Electron-Ion Collider, EIC）的ep测量提供了直接应用方案，EIC环境更有利于探测瞬子诱导过程。

Conclusion: 提出的喷注关联观测量为在加速器实验中探测QCD瞬子提供了有效工具，特别是在未来电子-离子对撞机（EIC）的清洁环境中具有重要应用前景。

Abstract: Discovery of instantons in colliders will provide experimental evidence for the topological properties of the QCD vacuum. In this work, we propose jet correlation observables that can unambiguously discriminate between instanton-induced processes and perturbative hard scattering events in pp collisions at LHC energies. By calculating the instanton sizes and their separations in 2+1 flavor QCD with physical quark masses, we provide constraints on the center-of-mass energies of the produced hadrons in an instanton-induced process. Our proposal is directly applicable for future ep measurements at the Electron-Ion Collider, offering a cleaner environment to probe instanton-induced processes.

</details>


### [104] [Self-Interaction and Galactic Magnetic Field Bounds on Millicharged Magnetic Monopole Dark Matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19873)
*Michael L. Graesser,R. Andrew Gustafson*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文研究了一个由暗U(1)对称性的磁单极子（magnetic monopoles）组成的暗物质模型，该模型与标准模型光子存在微小动力学混合（kinetic mixing），具有丰富的现象学特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该模型在理论上具有研究价值，其暗物质扇区由暗U(1)对称性的磁单极子组成，并与标准模型光子存在微小动力学混合，展现出丰富而有趣的现象学特征。

Method: 基于暗扇区温度和该U(1)对称性自发破缺（spontaneous symmetry breaking）的尺度，讨论了该暗物质模型的三种现象学上不同的情况。在所有情况下，将暗物质自相互作用的约束转化为对模型参数的约束。

Result: 由于磁单极子获得微小的可见磁荷，星系磁场的存活（称为帕克效应，Parker effect）对暗扇区和可见扇区之间的混合施加了进一步的约束。

Conclusion: 该暗物质模型具有理论价值和丰富的现象学特征，通过分析暗物质自相互作用约束和帕克效应，可以对该模型的参数空间施加重要限制。

Abstract: A dark matter sector composed of magnetic monopoles of a dark U(1) symmetry having a small kinetic mixing with the Standard Model photon has a rich and interesting phenomenology. The model in itself is also of theoretical interest. Based on the temperature of the dark sector and scale of spontaneous symmetry breaking for this U(1), three phenomenologically distinct cases for this model of dark matter are discussed. In all cases, constraints on dark matter self-interactions are translated into constraints on the model parameters. As the magnetic monopoles acquire a small visible magnetic charge, the survival of galactic magnetic fields, known as the Parker effect, places further constraints on the mixing between the dark and visible sectors.

### [105] [Chiral first order phase transition at finite baryon density and zero temperature from self-consistent pole masses in the linear sigma model with quarks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20196)
*Alejandro Ayala,Bruno El-Bennich,Ricardo L. S. Farias,Luis A. Hernández,Bruno S. Lopes,Luis C. Parra L.,Renato Zamora*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文使用含夸克的两味线性西格玛模型（Linear Sigma Model）作为QCD的有效描述，研究有限重子化学势和零温下的手征相变性质。研究发现相变为一级相变，发生在夸克化学势达到真空夸克质量时，手征凝聚、质量和耦合常数均呈现不连续行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在研究量子色动力学（QCD）在有限重子化学势和零温度条件下的手征相变（chiral phase transition）性质。通过使用两味线性西格玛模型作为QCD的有效描述，超越传统的环图近似（ring-diagram approximation），为任意化学势值提供有效描述。

Method: 采用含夸克的两味线性西格玛模型（Linear Sigma Model with quarks）作为QCD的有效理论框架。在一圈阶（one-loop order）建立并求解粒子极点质量（particle pole masses）的自洽耦合方程组，通过最小化一圈有效势（one-loop effective potential）获得化学势依赖的手征序参量值。

Result: 研究发现相变为一级相变（first order phase transition），当夸克化学势达到所选参数下的真空夸克质量时发生相变。手征凝聚（chiral condensate）、质量和耦合常数均呈现不连续行为。系统热力学分析显示声速平方（square of the speed of sound）在相变点出现不连续性，随后从下方平滑趋近共形极限（conformal limit）。

Conclusion: 该研究证实了在有限重子化学势和零温条件下，手征相变具有一级相变特征。超越传统环图近似的自洽处理方法为任意化学势值提供了有效描述框架，揭示了相变点处手征凝聚、质量和耦合常数的不连续行为以及热力学量的特征变化。

Abstract: We use the two-flavor Linear Sigma Model with quarks as an effective description of QCD to investigate the nature of the chiral phase transition at finite baryon chemical potential and zero temperature. We work at one-loop order to set up and solve the system of self-consistent coupled equations for the particle pole masses. The chemical potential-dependent value of the chiral order parameter is obtained by minimizing the one-loop effective potential. This treatment goes beyond the conventional ring-diagram approximation and provides a description valid for arbitrary values of the chemical potential. We find that the phase transition is of first order, and occurs when the quark chemical potential reaches the value of the vacuum quark mass for the chosen set of parameters. The first order nature of the transition is signaled by the discontinuous behavior of the chiral condensate, the masses and the couplings. The thermodynamics of the system is readily implemented and in particular, we find that the square of the speed of sound exhibits a discontinuity at the phase transition and then smoothly approaches the conformal limit from below.

</details>


### [106] [No planar degeneracy for the Landau gauge quark-gluon vertex](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20235)
*Georg Wieland,Reinhard Alkofer*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究通过Dyson-Schwinger方程系统计算了淬火QCD中夸克-胶子顶角的横向部分，发现其形状因子的角度依赖性较弱但不可忽略，并确认了动态手征对称性破缺的核心机制是胶子与夸克之间的动态张量耦合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在精确理解夸克-胶子顶点（quark-gluon vertex）在淬火QCD（quenched QCD）中的横向部分行为，特别是其角度依赖性和对动态手征对称性破缺（dynamical chiral symmetry breaking）的贡献。

Method: 基于合适的基系统（basis system）和精心选择的运动学变量（kinematical variables），采用Dyson-Schwinger方程（Dyson-Schwinger equations）系统求解Landau规范下夸克-胶子顶点的横向部分，并分析3PI Dyson-Schwinger方程的自洽耦合系统。

Result: 研究发现横向夸克-胶子顶点形状因子（form factors）的角度依赖性看似较弱，但即使这种温和依赖在追求精确结果时也不可忽略；确认动态手征对称性破缺的核心是胶子与夸克之间的动态张量耦合（dynamically generated tensor coupling），该耦合本身依赖于手征对称性破缺。

Conclusion: 研究提供了夸克-胶子顶点形状因子的高精度拟合，基于简单模型函数；发现夸克传播子（quark propagator）在脱耦解（decoupling solution）和标度解（scaling solution）下数值相同，且仅在类时半轴（real time-like half-axis）上存在极点。

Abstract: Based on a suitable basis system for the quark-gluon vertex' transverse tensor structures and on carefully chosen kinematical variables, the transverse part of the quark-gluon vertex in quenched QCD in the Landau gauge is obtained from a system of Dyson-Schwinger equations. We demonstrate by analysing this solution that the angular dependence of these transverse quark-gluon vertex form factors is seemingly weak. We nevertheless argue that this does not imply a planar degeneracy for this vertex because even this mild dependence cannot be neglected when aiming for reasonably precise results for derived quantities. Last but not least, for a self-consistently coupled systems of 3PI Dyson-Schwinger equations for the quark propagator and the quark-gluon vertex we confirm that the core ingredient to dynamical chiral symmetry breaking is the dynamically generated tensor coupling of glue to quarks which itself is only possible because of chiral symmetry breaking. Furthermore, we find (i) a relation in between the calculated chirality violating vertex form factors; (ii) that the quark propagator is identical within numerical errors when obtained either from a decoupling solution or the scaling solution for the Yang-Mills propagators and vertex functions; and (iii) that the resulting quark propagator is consistent with possessing poles only on the real time-like half-axis. Furthermore, we provide high-precision fits for the form factors based on sometimes astonishingly simple model functions.

</details>


### [107] [Primordial Magnetogenesis and Gravitational Waves from ALP-assisted Phase Transition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20768)
*Pankaj Borah,P. S. Bhupal Dev,Anish Ghoshal*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了早期宇宙中强一级相变（FOPT）如何同时产生可观测的随机引力波背景（SGWB）和大尺度原初磁场（PMF）。在最小轴子样粒子（ALP）框架下，通过ALP与标准模型（SM）的希格斯门户耦合，计算了PMF和SGWB的关联性，发现与γ射线耀变体观测一致的ALP参数区域可产生未来空间干涉仪可探测的SGWB。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 早期宇宙中的强一级相变（FOPT）可同时产生随机引力波背景（SGWB）和原初磁场（PMF）。近期Fermi-LAT数据显示的3.8σ非零星系际磁场（IGMF）证据进一步支持了磁场的宇宙学起源，促使研究者探索这两种宇宙信号在统一框架下的关联性。

Method: 研究采用最小轴子样粒子（ALP）框架，其中全局U(1)对称性通过辐射修正自发破缺，ALP扇区通过希格斯门户（Higgs-portal）与标准模型（SM）耦合。计算了当前PMF振幅和相干长度，考虑了逆级联效应，分析了最大螺旋和非螺旋构型。

Result: 对于最大螺旋构型，峰值磁场强度可达B₀ ∼ 10⁻⁹ G，相干长度λ₀ ∼ 10⁻³-10⁻¹ Mpc，与MAGIC、H.E.S.S.和Fermi-LAT从耀变体观测推断的IGMF下限一致。与γ射线耀变体数据一致的ALP参数区域（假设最大螺旋性）可在ALP衰变常数范围10³ GeV ≲ fₐ ≲ 10⁵ GeV内产生LISA等未来空间干涉仪可探测的SGWB。

Conclusion: 研究建立了宇宙学观测与实验室/天体物理ALP搜索之间的多信使互补性。综合约束倾向于相对较重的ALP（mₐ ≳ 0.1 GeV），这一参数区域可通过下一代强度和能量前沿实验进行探测，为ALP物理和早期宇宙相变提供了可检验的预测。

Abstract: Sufficiently strong first-order phase transitions (FOPTs) in the early Universe can simultaneously produce an observable stochastic gravitational wave background (SGWB) and a large-scale primordial magnetic field (PMF). The recent $3.8σ$ evidence for a non-zero intergalactic MF from anisotropic pair-halo searches using \textit{Fermi}-LAT data further motivates a cosmological origin of this MF. We investigate an FOPT-origin of both cosmic signatures, namely, PMF and SGWB, and the correlation between them, within a minimal axion-like particle (ALP) framework in which a global $U(1)$ symmetry is spontaneously broken through radiative corrections, with the ALP sector coupled to the Standard Model (SM) via Higgs-portal. We compute the present-day PMF amplitude and coherence length for both maximally helical and non-helical configurations, accounting for inverse cascade effects. For maximally helical configurations, we find peak field strengths up to $B_0 \sim 10^{-9}$ G at coherence length $λ_0 \sim 10^{-3}-10^{-1}$ Mpc, consistent with lower bounds on the IGMF inferred from blazar observations by MAGIC, H.E.S.S. and {\it Fermi}-LAT. We show that the ALP parameter region consistent with $γ$-ray blazar data (assuming maximal helicity) simultaneously produces SGWB detectable at future space-based interferometers, such as LISA, etc., over the ALP decay constant range $10^3~\text{GeV} \lesssim f_a \lesssim 10^5~\text{GeV}$. We directly map these onto effective ALP couplings to SM particles, e.g., photons, gluons, and fermions. This establishes a multi-messenger complementarity between cosmological observables and laboratory/astrophysical ALP searches, with the combined constraints preferring relatively heavy ALPs, $m_a \gtrsim 0.1~\text{GeV}$, in a regime accessible to next-generation intensity and energy-frontier experiments.

### [108] [Perfect spin nonreciprocity in gated superconducting altermagnetic heterostructures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20312)
*Pei-Hao Fu,Jun-Feng Liu,Luca Chirolli,Jorge Cayao*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索交变磁体（altermagnets）与超导异质结构中非互易自旋极化电流的产生机制，为开发电控非互易超导自旋电子器件提供理论基础。

Method: 通过在超导交变磁体与金属库之间引入有限正常区域并施加栅压，实现横向动量通道的选择性滤波，该滤波机制方向性地选择与动量依赖的自旋分裂超导交变磁态匹配的输运通道。

Result: 实现了局域和非局域自旋电流的完美非互易性，其极性可通过栅压高度调控，品质因子接近完美；局域和非局域电荷电流也表现出非互易行为，其品质因子同样可达完美值。

Conclusion: 该研究提出了一种基于交变磁体的电控非互易超导自旋电子器件实现途径，所有电流对交变磁场变化敏感，这一功能依赖性可用于识别交变磁体类型。

Abstract: We consider a superconducting altermagnet heterostructure and demonstrate that the interplay between altermagnetism and a selective filter of transverse momentum channels enables perfect nonreciprocal spin-polarized currents. We demonstrate that this nonreciprocity manifests in both local and nonlocal spin currents, signalling the emergence of directionally selective local and nonlocal spin behaviors. We show that the selective filter of transverse momentum channels is realized by gating a finite normal region between the superconducting altermagnet and the metallic reservoir, which then directionally selects transport channels that match the momentum-dependent spin-split superconducting altermagnetic states, allowing for nonreciprocal spin-polarized currents. We discover that the local and nonlocal spin nonreciprocity features a highly tunable polarity and nearly perfect quality factors, respectively, which is achieved by means of gate voltages and by varying the length of the finite region. Moreover, we find that local and nonlocal charge currents also develop a nonreciprocal behavior, whose quality factors can also reach perfect values. In all cases, the spin and charge currents are sensitive to variations of the altermagnetic field, a functional dependence that can be exploited to identify the type of altermagnetism. Our findings put forward an electrically controllable route towards nonreciprocal superconducting spintronic devices based on altermagnets.

### [109] [Discovery of parity-violating chiral polar-nematic charge density wave and superconductivity in kagome metals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20546)
*Xingwei Shi,Geng Li,Zhan Wang,Chuqi Zhang,Ke Zhu,Keyu Zeng,Zikun Tang,Li Huang,Zhen Zhao,Jianping Sun,Xiao Liu,Jin-Guang Cheng,Chengmin Shen,Shu Ping Lau,Kian Ping Loh,Haitao Yang,Xiao Lin,Ziqiang Wang,Hong-Jun Gao*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究通过扫描隧道显微镜等技术发现，非磁性kagome金属AV3Sb5在电荷密度波（CDW）态中自发破缺了反演对称性，形成了混合宇称的CDW态，包含铁电极化偶极和向列四极有序矩。这种多极耦合产生了电子手性，并可通过电场调控。在超导转变下观察到宇称破缺的配对密度调制。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用扫描隧道显微镜（scanning tunneling microscopy）结合原子力显微镜和光学二次谐波产生技术，直接探测kagome平面内的对称性破缺现象。通过电场调控实验研究多极耦合特性。

Result: 实验直接揭示了CDW态中kagome平面的反演对称性自发破缺。混合宇称CDW态表现出铁电极化偶极和向列四极有序矩，其共存与耦合导致非共线铁电极化和向列排列，破缺所有镜面对称性，在3Q CDW中产生稳健的电子手性。

Conclusion: 宇称破缺的电子手性多极有序为kagome金属及相关量子材料中的磁电效应、非互易输运、环流有序、配对密度波和非常规超导性提供了微观见解。多极与面内电场的耦合实现了手性极-向列CDW态及其手性的电场调控。

Abstract: Nonmagnetic kagome metals and superconductors AV3Sb5 (A = K, Rb, Cs) host unconventional charge density wave (CDW) and superconducting (SC) phases accompanied by multiple electronic symmetry breaking. Due to the centrosymmetric crystal structure, inversion symmetry has generally been assumed to hold. Here, using scanning tunneling microscopy complemented by atomic force microscopy and optical second-harmonic generation, we directly reveal that inversion symmetry in the kagome plane is spontaneously broken in the CDW state. The mixed-parity CDW state exhibits ferroelectric dipolar and nematic quadrupolar ordered moments. The coexistence and coupling between the dipole and quadrupole favor noncollinear ferro-polar and nematic alignment that breaks all mirror symmetries and gives rise to robust electronic chirality in the 3Q CDW. The multipolar coupling to in-plane electric field enables electric field control and manipulation of the chiral polar-nematic CDW state, including its chirality. Below the SC transition, we observe parity-violating pair density modulations at both the original and the CDW lattice wavevectors. Our findings of parity-violating electronic chiral multipolar order provide microscopic insights into the magnetoelectric and nonreciprocal transport, loop current order, pairing density waves, and unconventional superconductivity in kagome metals and related quantum materials.

### [110] [Superconductivity in bilayer La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$: A review focusing on the strong-coupling Hund's rule assisted pairing mechanism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20613)
*Zhiming Pan,Chen Lu,Fan Yang,Congjun Wu*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文综述了双层镍酸盐La₃Ni₂O₇中高Tc超导（high-Tc superconductivity）的理论机制，重点分析了由强耦合、洪德辅助（Hund-assisted）场景驱动的配对机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 双层镍酸盐La₃Ni₂O₇中高Tc超导的发现为探索非常规超导提供了新平台。实验证据表明其具有关联电子性质，这是驱动高临界温度（Tc）的关键因素。

Method: 研究采用理论分析框架，重点关注强耦合、洪德辅助场景下的配对机制。通过构建双层t-J-J⊥最小强耦合模型来描述3d_{x²-y²}能带的电子行为。

Result: 在强耦合区域，洪德规则耦合（Hund's rule coupling）使同一镍位点上两个E_g轨道的自旋对齐。强层间反铁磁交换（interlayer antiferromagnetic exchange）有效转移到巡游的3d_{x²-y²}轨道，产生有效耦合J⊥。在J⊥驱动下，3d_{x²-y²}电子形成层间库珀对（interlayer Cooper pairs），导致扩展s波配对超导（extended s-wave pairing SC）和高Tc。

Conclusion: 双层镍酸盐La₃Ni₂O₇的超导机制由强层间反铁磁交换和洪德耦合共同驱动。3d_{x²-y²}轨道参与超导凝聚态，而强局域的3d_{z²}电子形成层间梯子单重态（interlayer rung singlets），由于缺乏相位相干性，这些单重态不直接参与超导凝聚，而是导致赝隙相（pseudogap phase）的形成。

Abstract: Discovery of high-$T_c$ superconductivity (SC) in the bilayer nickelate series La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$ have attracted substantial interest, providing a new platform for exploring unconventional SC. Certain experimental evidence has pointed to a correlated electronic nature, which is the driving force responsible for its high critical temperature ($T_c$). This work reviews the SC in La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$, with a particular focus on theoretical understanding of its pairing mechanism driven by this strong-coupling, Hund-assisted scenario. The electronic landscape is governed by two $E_g$-orbitals within the bilayer structure of NiO$_2$ planes. The $3d_{z^2}$ orbital is nearly half-filled and exhibits a stronger localized character, while the $3d_{x^2-y^2}$ is approximately quarter-filled and remains highly itinerant. The localized $3d_{z^2}$ orbitals experience robust interlayer hybridization, mediated by the $2p_z$ orbitals of the inner apical oxygen atoms. This hybridization generates a strong interlayer antiferromagnetic (AFM) exchange. In the strong coupling regime, Hund's rule coupling aligns the spins of the two $E_g$ orbitals on the same nickel site. The strong interlayer AFM exchange is effectively transferred to the itinerant $3d_{x^2-y^2}$ orbital, generating an effective coupling $J_{\perp}$ within this orbital. This mechanism is captured by a minimal strong-coupling bilayer $t$-$J$-$J_{\perp}$ model for the $3d_{x^2-y^2}$ band. Driven by $J_{\perp}$, $3d_{x^2-y^2}$ electrons can form interlayer Cooper pairs, leading to an extended $s$-wave pairing SC with high $T_c$. Meanwhile, the strongly localized $3d_{z^2}$ electrons tend to form interlayer rung singlets. Due to a lack of phase coherence, these singlets do not directly participate in the SC condensate, but instead give rise to a pseudogap phase.

</details>


### [111] [Stabilization of a non-superconducting, orthorhombic phase by over-hydrogenating LaFeSiH](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20716)
*M. F. Hansen,C. Lepoittevin,J. -B. Vaney,P. Boullay,V. Nassif,A. Sulpice,H. Mayaffre,M. -H. Julien,S. Tencé,P. Toulemonde*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究通过高压热分解富氢前驱体实现了LaFeSi的过氢化，合成了四方超导相LaFeSiH和正交半导体相LaFeSiH₁₊ₓ，揭示了氢含量对铁基硅化物电子基态的可控调控。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 化学组成是调控铁基超导体（iron-based superconductors）电子基态的有效途径，但高度掺杂相的获取仍受限制。本研究旨在探索通过氢化实现LaFeSi体系的高掺杂，拓展铁基硅化物（Fe-based silicides）的研究空间。

Method: 采用高压热分解（high-pressure thermal decomposition）富氢前驱体（hydrogen-rich precursors）的方法：使用蒽（anthracene）合成四方相LaFeSiH，使用氨硼烷（ammonia borane）合成正交过氢化相LaFeSiH₁₊ₓ。通过化学分析和中子衍射（neutron diffraction）确定氢含量和占位。

Result: 成功合成了两种氢化相：四方超导相LaFeSiH（单氢位点）和正交半导体相LaFeSiH₁₊ₓ（x~0.6，含第二氢位点）。后者在100°C附近释放氢后转变为四方超导相LaFeSiH₁₊δ（δ<<0.6），实现了氢含量对电子性质的连续调控。

Conclusion: 该工作证实了层状LaFeSiX（X=H, O, F）家族的化学灵活性，提供了进入高氢掺杂区域（high hydrogen-doping regime）的途径，为研究铁基硅化物超导性创造了新机遇。

Abstract: Chemical composition provides a powerful route to tune the electronic ground state of iron-based superconductors and other quantum materials, yet access to highly doped phases remains limited. Here we demonstrate that high-pressure thermal decomposition of hydrogen-rich precursors enables over-hydrogenation of LaFeSi. Using anthracene, we synthesize tetragonal superconducting LaFeSiH, including a single hydrogen site, while ammonia borane yields a structurally distorted over-hydrogenated phase, LaFeSiH1+x, with an orthorhombic structure. Chemical analysis reveal excess hydrogen (x ~ 0.6), implying a second H site in LaFeSiH1.6 whose localization and occupancy are determined by neutron diffraction. In contrast to metallic LaFeSi and superconducting LaFeSiH, orthorhombic LaFeSiH1.6 exhibits semiconductor-like behavior. Upon hydrogen release near 100 °C, it transforms into tetragonal superconducting LaFeSiH1+δ (δ << 0.6). These results establish the chemical flexibility of the layered LaFeSiX (X = H, O, F) family and provide access to a high hydrogen-doping regime, creating new opportunities to investigate superconductivity in Fe-based silicides.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前研究构建了能够提取非高斯隐藏输入特征的最优LPC网络，但这些递归交互动力系统对外部输入的响应速度可能非常缓慢。本文旨在研究如何减少LPC系统的响应时间。

Method: 研究通过优化横向预测编码（lateral predictive coding, LPC）网络结构来最小化响应时间，同时保持预测误差（能量成本）和信息鲁棒性。特别探索了模块化结构组织，大幅减少横向交互数量。

Abstract: Lateral predictive coding (LPC) is a simple theoretical framework to appreciate feature detection in biological neural circuits. Recent theoretical work [Huang et al., Phys.Rev.E 112, 034304 (2025)] has successfully constructed optimal LPC networks capable of extracting non-Gaussian hidden input features by imposing the tradeoff between energetic cost and information robustness, but the resulting dynamical systems of recurrent interactions can be very slow in responding to external inputs. We investigate response-time reduction in the present paper. We find that the characteristic response time of the LPC system can be minimized to closely approaching the lower-bound value without compromising the mean predictive error (energetic cost) and the information robustness of signal transmission. We further demonstrate that optimal LPC networks taking a modular structural organization with extensively reduced number of lateral interactions are equally excellent as all-to-all completely connected networks, in terms of feature detection performance, response time, energetic cost and information robustness.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本文发展了新的短程-长程比较条件，证明当两个非齐次随机矩阵的方差轮廓马尔可夫链具有可比性时，它们会展现出相同的普适边缘统计特性，而无需考虑矩阵元素的精细细节。

Result: 通过马尔可夫链比较定理，推导了随机带矩阵、Wegner轨道模型和汉克尔轮廓随机矩阵等典型模型的谱边缘统计，揭示了由几何结构、尖峰模式和稳定吸引域塑造的丰富普适与非普适现象景观。

Conclusion: 马尔可夫链比较方法超越了经典随机矩阵理论的能力范围，揭示了边缘统计普适性根本上由方差轮廓马尔可夫链的可比性决定，为理解稀疏随机矩阵的普适现象提供了新框架。

Abstract: The first paper in this series introduced a \emph{short-to-long mixing} condition that captures mean-field GOE/GUE edge universality in the supercritical sparsity regime, for symmetric/Hermitian random matrices with independent entries and a Markov variance profile. This condition reduces the universality problem to the mixing properties of the underlying Markov chains.
  In this paper, we develop new \emph{short-to-long comparison} conditions that extend the analysis to the subcritical and critical sparsity regimes. Specifically, we prove that two inhomogeneous random matrices exhibit the same universal edge statistics whenever their variance-profile Markov chains are comparable, regardless of the fine details of the matrix entries. To illustrate the power of our Markov chain comparison theorem, we derive the spectral edge statistics for several prototypical models: random band matrices, the Wegner orbital model, and Hankel-profile random matrices. These comparisons uncover a rich landscape of both universal and non-universal phenomena -- shaped by geometric structure, spike patterns, and domains of stable attraction -- features that lie fundamentally beyond the reach of classical random matrix theory.

### [116] [Macroscopic loops in the random loop model on sparse random graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20514)
*Andreas Klippel*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 该研究在稀疏随机图上的随机环模型（random loop model）中证明了宏观环（macroscopic loops）的存在性，即访问正比例顶点的环。通过确定性漂移方法（deterministic drift method）建立了一般判据，并在多种随机图模型中验证了该判据，得到了边密度超过显式阈值时的宏观环概率下界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 主要目标是证明稀疏随机图上带有交叉（crosses）和横杠（bars）的随机环模型中宏观环的存在性。宏观环定义为访问正比例顶点的环，这在统计物理和随机图理论中具有重要意义。

Method: 开发了基于任意有限图的确定性漂移方法，包含三个关键要素：环数的局部分裂-合并-重连分析（local split--merge--rewire analysis）、配分函数（partition function）的精确微分恒等式，以及将相关同环插入体积（same-loop insertion volume）约化为小顶点集诱导边计数的切片估计（slice estimate）。该方法产生了一个基于底层图小集稀疏条件的一般判据。

Result: 在随机正则图（random regular graphs）、稀疏Erdős--Rényi图和简单有界度配置模型（simple bounded-degree configuration models）中验证了该判据。当边密度超过依赖于环权重θ和交叉参数u的显式阈值时，获得了宏观环概率的平均下界（averaged lower bounds）。对于整数值θ，配分函数的迹表示（trace representation）意味着对数凸性（log-convexity），从而将平均界升级为远离阈值时间的逐点时间结果（pointwise-in-time results）。

Conclusion: 该研究成功建立了稀疏随机图上随机环模型中宏观环存在性的一般理论框架，并在多种随机图模型中获得了具体的定量结果。方法的核心是通过小集稀疏条件将宏观环的存在性与图的结构性质联系起来。

Abstract: We study the random loop model with crosses and bars on sparse random graphs. Our main objective is to prove the existence of macroscopic loops, in the sense that a loop visits a positive proportion of the vertices. We develop a deterministic drift method on arbitrary finite graphs based on three ingredients: a local split--merge--rewire analysis for the loop number, an exact differential identity for the partition function, and a slice estimate reducing the relevant same-loop insertion volume to induced edge counts of small vertex sets. This yields a general criterion in terms of a small-set sparsity condition on the underlying graph. We then verify this condition for random regular graphs, sparse Erdős--Rényi graphs, and simple bounded-degree configuration models, obtaining averaged lower bounds on the probability of a macroscopic loop whenever the edge density exceeds an explicit threshold depending on the loop weight \(θ\) and the cross parameter \(u\). For integer values of \(θ\), a trace representation of the partition function implies log-convexity, which upgrades the averaged bounds to pointwise-in-time results away from the threshold time.

</details>


### [117] [The Ising Model on a Two-Community Stochastic Block Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20631)
*Alessandra Bianchi,Vanessa Jacquier,Matteo Sfragara*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 该研究分析了伊辛模型（Ising model）在双社区随机块模型上的相变行为，完整刻画了相图并证明了吉布斯测度（Gibbs measure）的唯一性/非唯一性相变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于理解伊辛模型在具有社区结构的随机图上的统计力学行为，特别是探究当自旋被分为两个相等社区时，系统在不同相互作用参数下的相变特性。

Method: 采用双社区随机块模型（two-community stochastic block model）作为图结构，将n个自旋分为两个相等组，并引入社区间相互作用参数α_n∈[0,1]来研究系统的相行为。

Result: 研究完整刻画了相图，证明了吉布斯测度的唯一性/非唯一性相变。在超临界区域，两个社区的磁化向量（magnetization vector）的分布收敛到狄拉克测度（Dirac measures）的混合，支持点数为2或4个。在唯一性区域，亚临界区证明了淬火中心极限定理（quenched central limit theorem），临界区则建立了n^{1/4}尺度上的非高斯涨落。

Conclusion: 该研究系统揭示了伊辛模型在社区结构图上的丰富相变行为，特别是发现了磁化向量分布对相互作用参数尺度α_n≫1/n或α_n≲1/n的依赖性，以及在临界点附近涨落行为的尺度变化。

Abstract: We study the Ising model on a two-community stochastic block model, where $n$ spins are split into two equal groups with inter-community interaction parameter $α_n\in[0,1]$. We provide a complete characterization of the phase diagram and show that, almost surely with respect to the graph realization, the model undergoes a uniqueness/non-uniqueness phase transition of the Gibbs measure. In particular, in the supercritical regime, the law of the magnetization vector of the two communities converges to a mixture of Dirac measures that, depending on whether $α_n\gg 1/n$ or $α_n\lesssim 1/n$, is supported on two or four points, with possibly different weights. In the uniqueness region, we further analyze the fluctuations of the magnetization vector: in the subcritical regime, we prove a quenched central limit theorem under the classical $\sqrt{n}$ scaling, while at criticality we establish non-Gaussian fluctuations on the smaller scale $n^{1/4}$.

</details>


### [118] [The Legendre structure of the TAP complexity for the Ising spin glass](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20660)
*Jeanne Boursier*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 该研究分析了伊辛自旋玻璃（Ising spin glass）的Thouless-Anderson-Palmer（TAP）自由能的复杂度（complexity），提出了三个关于临界点数量的猜想，并通过Kac-Rice计算和超对称假设（supersymmetric ansatz）验证了第一个猜想的下界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于理解自旋玻璃系统中TAP自由能临界点的统计特性，特别是复杂度（临界点数量）与巴黎西公式（Parisi formula）及配分函数大偏差率函数（large-deviation rate function）之间的精确联系。

Method: 采用Chen、Panchenko和Subag的广义TAP泛函（generalized TAP functional），结合Kac-Rice计算和超对称假设（supersymmetric ansatz）来推导复杂度下界，并扩展到条件设置中分析层次化"骨架"结构。

Result: 建立了退火复杂度（annealed complexity）下界，该下界与第一个猜想的预测相匹配；在条件设置中分析了层次化祖先骨架，为第二和第三个猜想提供了额外证据。

Conclusion: 研究提出了三个关于TAP状态复杂度的猜想，并通过数学分析验证了第一个猜想的下界，同时为TAP状态在非平衡自由能水平上的超度量层次结构（ultrametric hierarchy）组织提供了理论支持。

Abstract: We study the complexity of the Thouless-Anderson-Palmer (TAP) free energy for Ising spin glasses with a general mixed p-spin covariance, working with the generalized TAP functional of Chen, Panchenko, and Subag. We formulate three conjectures about the complexity (i.e. number of critical points). First, the annealed complexity is given by the Legendre transform of a variational functional constructed from the Parisi formula subject to a constraint on the overlap mass at zero, thereby establishing a precise link between the enumeration of TAP states and the large-deviation rate function of the partition function. Second, the quenched complexity is governed by the Legendre transform of a closely related functional in which the mass up to -- but not including -- the supremum of the support is constrained. Third, TAP states at any non-equilibrium free-energy level are organized into an ultrametric hierarchy, with ancestor states at other levels appearing only in subexponential number. Using a Kac-Rice computation combined with a supersymmetric ansatz, we establish a lower bound on the annealed complexity that matches the prediction of the first conjecture. We further extend the analysis to a conditional setting in which a hierarchical "skeleton" of ancestors is prescribed, providing additional evidence in support of the second and third conjectures.

</details>

### [119] [Neural posterior estimation of the neutrino direction in IceCube using transformer-encoded normalizing flows on the sphere](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19846)
*R. Abbasi,M. Ackermann,J. Adams,J. A. Aguilar,M. Ahlers,J. M. Alameddine,S. Ali,N. M. Amin,K. Andeen,C. Argüelles,Y. Ashida,S. Athanasiadou,S. N. Axani,R. Babu,X. Bai,A. Balagopal V.,S. W. Seen,M. Seikh,S. Seunarine,P. A. Sevle Myhr,R. Shah,S. Shah,S. Shefali,N. Shimizu,B. Skrzypek,R. Snihur,J. Soedingrekso,D. Soldin,P. Soldin,G. Sommani,C. Spannfellner,G. M. Spiczak,C. Spiering,J. Stachurska,M. Stamatikos,T. Stanev,T. Stezelberger,T. Stürwald,T. Stuttard,G. W. Sullivan,I. Taboada,S. Ter-Antonyan,A. Terliuk,A. Thakuri,M. Thiesmeyer,W. G. Thompson,J. Thwaites,S. Tilav,K. Tollefson,J. A. Torres,S. Toscano,D. Tosi,K. Upshaw,A. Vaidyanathan,N. Valtonen-Mattila,J. Valverde,J. Vandenbroucke,T. Van Eeden,N. van Eijndhoven,L. Van Rootselaar,J. van Santen,J. Vara,F. Varsi,M. Venugopal,M. Vereecken,S. Vergara Carrasco,S. Verpoest,D. Veske,A. Vijai,J. Villarreal,C. Walck,A. Wang,E. H. S. Warrick,C. Weaver,P. Weigel,A. Weindl,J. Weldert,A. Y. Wen,C. Wendt,J. Werthebach,M. Weyrauch,N. Whitehorn,C. H. Wiebusch,D. R. Williams,L. Witthaus,G. Wrede,X. W. Xu,J. P. Yanez,Y. Yao,E. Yildizci,S. Yoshida,R. Young,F. Yu,S. Yu,T. Yuan,S. Yun-Cárcamo,A. Zander Jurowitzki,A. Zegarelli,S. Zhang,Z. Zhang,P. Zhelnin,P. Zilberman*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于Transformer编码器和球面归一化流（normalizing flow）的IceCube中微子方向重建新方法，在计算速度和角分辨率方面均显著优于传统的B样条（B-spline）似然重建方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: IceCube作为立方公里级的中微子探测器，精确的方向重建对于关联天文源至关重要。传统B样条似然重建方法计算耗时，需要数小时完成全天扫描，限制了实时分析能力。

Method: 采用Transformer编码器映射到2-球面上的归一化流分布，结合C²-光滑有理二次样条（rational-quadratic splines）、尺度变换和旋转定义新型球面归一化流。改进了标准Transformer架构，包括双残差流（dual residual streams）、非线性QKV投影和独立类别标记（class token）的交叉注意力处理。

Result: 该方法在100 GeV至100 PeV能量范围内显著提升了径迹（tracks）和簇射（showers）的角分辨率。在100 TeV沉积能量下，通过径迹（throughgoing tracks）的中值角分辨率提升1.3倍，簇射提升1.7倍，起始径迹（starting tracks）提升2.5倍。全天扫描时间从数小时缩短至数秒，且计算时间与后验分布范围无关。

Conclusion: 该方法首次实现了机器学习（ML）方法在100 GeV以上能量范围内超越基于似然的μ子重建性能，为IceCube中微子天文学提供了快速且精确的方向重建工具。

Abstract: IceCube is a cubic-kilometer-scale neutrino detector located at the geographic South Pole. A precise directional reconstruction of IceCube neutrinos is vital for associations with astronomical objects. In this context, we discuss neural posterior estimation of the neutrino direction via a transformer encoder that maps to a normalizing flow on the 2-sphere. It achieves a new state-of-the-art angular resolution for the two main event morphologies in IceCube - tracks and showers - while being significantly faster than traditional B-spline-based likelihood reconstructions. All-sky scans can be performed within seconds rather than hours, and take constant computation time, regardless of whether the posterior extent is arc-minutes or spans the whole sky. We utilize a combination of $C^2$-smooth rational-quadratic splines, scale transformations and rotations to define a novel spherical normalizing-flow distribution whose parameters are predicted as a whole as the output of the transformer encoder. We test several structural choices diverting from the vanilla transformer architecture. In particular, we find dual residual streams, nonlinear QKV projection and a separate class token with its own cross-attention processing to boost test-time performance. The angular resolution for both showers and tracks improves substantially over the whole trained energy range from 100 GeV to 100 PeV. At 100 TeV deposited energy, for example, the median angular resolution improves by a factor of $1.3$ for throughgoing tracks, by a factor of $1.7$ for showers and by a factor of $2.5$ for starting tracks compared to state-of-the art likelihood reconstructions based on B-splines. While previous machine-learning (ML) efforts have managed to obtain competitive shower resolutions, this is the first time an ML-based method outperforms likelihood-based muon reconstructions above 100 GeV.

</details>


### [120] [Prospects for measuring exclusive diffractive $η,η'$ at the LHC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20037)
*Rainer Schicker*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 该论文研究了质子-质子对撞中的中心独占衍射产生过程，重点分析了在LHC能量下通过波密子-波密子融合产生赝标量介子η和η'的可行性，以确定波密子的自旋结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究质子-质子对撞中中心独占衍射产生过程的特征，特别关注通过波密子-波密子融合产生赝标量介子η和η'的可行性，旨在确定波密子的自旋结构。

Method: 采用雷吉理论（Regge approach）描述波密子，利用适当放置的探测器系统测量前向散射质子或其残余物，并结合覆盖中间快度范围的探测器来识别中心衍射事件。

Result: 在LHC能量下，质子-质子对撞中的中心衍射产生主要由波密子-波密子融合主导，研究证实了识别赝标量介子η和η'在波密子-波密子融合中的可行性。

Conclusion: 通过分析中心独占衍射产生过程，特别是研究赝标量介子η和η'在波密子-波密子融合中的产生，为确定波密子的自旋结构提供了有效方法。

Abstract: Central exclusive diffractive production in proton-proton collisions
  at hadron colliders is characterised by hadronic activity at or close to
  midrapidity, and by the two forward scattered protons, or their remnants.
  In such events, no particles are produced between the midrapidity system
  and the forward beam particles. These events can hence be identified with
  appropriately placed detectors for measuring the forward scattered protons,
  or their remnants, and a detector system covering the midrapidity range.
  At the energies of the LHC, central diffractive production in proton-proton
  collisions is dominated by pomeron-pomeron fusion. The description of the
  pomeron within the Regge approach is summarized, and the feasibility of
  identifying pseudoscalar mesons $η,η'$ in pomeron-pomeron fusion
  is studied for determining the spin structure of the pomeron.

</details>


### [121] [Using Graph Neural Networks for hadronic clustering and to reduce beam background in the Belle~II electromagnetic calorimeter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20518)
*Jonas Eppelt,Torben Ferber*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文提出使用图神经网络（Graph Neural Network）解决Belle~II电磁量能器中光子能量分辨率下降和假光子簇重建问题，通过识别并移除不需要的能量沉积来改善强子识别和定位精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Belle~II电磁量能器面临两个主要挑战：SuperKEKB加速器创纪录的亮度导致背景率增加，造成光子能量分辨率下降和更多假光子簇重建；强子在量能器中的相互作用产生不规则能量沉积，可能被误判为光子簇，影响中性强子的位置分辨率和识别准确性。

Method: 采用图神经网络方法，将具有能量测量的晶体表示为节点，利用图结构捕捉输入的稀疏性。通过消息传递层学习图边关系，以处理Belle~II电磁量能器的不对称传感器布局，并在探测器模拟中识别挑战性情况。

Result: 该方法能够有效识别和移除聚类前不需要的能量沉积，有望改善光子能量分辨率，减少假光子簇重建，并提高中性强子的位置分辨率和识别准确性。

Conclusion: 图神经网络为解决Belle~II电磁量能器在高亮度运行条件下的挑战提供了有前景的解决方案，通过改进聚类前的能量沉积处理，能够同时应对背景增加和强子相互作用带来的问题。

Abstract: The Belle~II electromagnetic calorimeter consists of 8376 CsI(Tl) scintillation crystals and is not only used for measuring electromagnetic particles but also for identifying and determining the position of hadrons, particularly neutral\textbf{} hadrons. Recent data-taking periods have presented challenges for the current clustering method: Firstly, the record-breaking luminosities achieved by the SuperKEKB accelerator have increased background rates, leading to a higher number of crystals with energy depositions, and an overall increase in the total energy measured in the calorimeter. This resulted in poorer photon energy resolution and the reconstruction of more fake photon clusters. Secondly, challenges arise from the nature of hadronic interactions. In contrast to $γ$ and $e^{\pm}$, hadrons interacting in the calorimeter result in irregular, sometimes even disconnected energy depositions. These clusters can be misinterpreted as photon clusters, thereby reducing the position resolution of neutral hadrons or causing a complete misidentification of the hadron. Graph neural networks offer a promising solution to both challenges. By representing only crystals with an energy measurement as nodes, graphs capture the sparsity of the input. Using message-passing layers that learn the graph edges also helps to address the asymmetric sensor layout of Belle~II's ECL. In these proceedings, we will present a novel approach to identify the challenges in the detector simulation. Using this information, we train a Graph Neural Network to identify and remove unwanted depositions abefore clustering.

</details>


### [122] [Review of experimental studies of charmed meson decays at BESIII](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20644)
*Yijia Zeng,Xiang Pan,Hailong Ma*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文综述了截至2026年4月15日BESIII实验对粲介子（D^0、D^+、D^+_s）及其激发态衰变的实验研究，报告了最精确的CKM矩阵元、衰变常数和强子形状因子的平均值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 粲介子衰变的实验测量为检验理论计算、测试CKM矩阵（Cabibbo-Kobayashi-Maskawa matrix）幺正性以及寻找超出标准模型（standard model, SM）的新物理效应提供了重要信息。

Method: 基于BESIII实验对粲介子衰变的大量实验测量，包括绝对分支比、衰变常数、强子形状因子、CKM矩阵元、轻子味普适性检验、强相位差测量、多体强子衰变振幅分析以及稀有衰变搜寻等。

Result: 获得了最精确的平均值：CKM矩阵元|V_{cs}|=0.9648±0.009±0.0036和|V_{cd}|=0.2259±0.0014±0.0013；衰变常数f_{D^+}=(213.1±2.0±1.5) MeV和f_{D^+_s}=(253.2±1.2±1.6) MeV；以及多个强子形状因子（form factors）的精确测量结果。

Conclusion: BESIII实验的粲介子衰变研究提供了高精度的实验数据，这些结果对于检验理论模型、测试标准模型基本参数以及探索新物理具有重要意义。

Abstract: Experimental measurements of different decays of charmed mesons have been extensively performed at BESIII. Precision measurements of absolute branching fractions of different decays, the decay constants of $D^+$ and $D^+_s$ mesons, hadronic form factors of $D$ transitions to light hadrons ($K$, $π$, $η$, $η^\prime$, $K^*(892)$, $ρ$, $ω$, $φ$, $K_1(1270)$, $f_0(980)$), $c\to s(d)$ Cabibbo-Kobayashi-Maskawa (CKM) matrix elements, tests of lepton flavor universality with various (semi)leptonic $D$ decays, precision measurements of strong phase difference between $D^0$ and $\bar D^0$ decays, amplitude analyses of multibody hadronic $D_{(s)}$ decays, search for rare $D$ decays have been reported. The reported results offer important information to test different theoretical calculations, to test the unitarity of the CKM matrix, and to search for new physics effects beyond the standard model (SM). This paper reviews experimental studies of different decays of $D^0$, $D^+$, and $D^+_s$ as well as their excitations at BESIII as of April 15, 2026. Based on existing results of (semi)leptonic $D$ decays from all experiments, we have presented the most precise averages for the CKM matrix elements $|V_{cs}|=0.9648\pm0.009\pm0.0036$ and $|V_{cd}|=0.2259\pm0.0014\pm0.0013$, the decay constants of $D^+$ and $D^+_s$ $f_{D^+}=(213.1\pm2.0\pm1.5)$ MeV and $f_{D^+_s}=(253.2\pm1.2\pm1.6)$ MeV, as well as the hadronic form factors $f^{D\to K}_+(0)=0.7342\pm0.0007\pm0.0008$, $f^{D\to π}_+(0)=0.6337\pm0.0053\pm0.0037$, $f^{D\to η}_+(0)=0.351\pm0.009\pm0.005$, $f^{D\to η^\prime}_+(0)=0.263\pm0.025\pm0.006$, $f^{D_s\to η}_+(0)=0.4653\pm0.0058\pm0.0069$, $f^{D_s\to η^\prime}_+(0)=0.535\pm0.020\pm0.011$, and $f^{D_s\to K^0}_+(0)=0.627\pm0.036\pm0.009$, where the first and second uncertainties are statistical and systematic, respectively.

</details>

### [123] [Predictive drift compensation of multi-frame STEM via live scan modification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20558)
*Matthew Mosse,Jonathan J. P. Peters,Eoin Moynihan,James A. Gott,Ana M. Sanchez,Michele Conroy,Lewys Jones*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种通过分析历史帧来预测未来帧采样网格点的方法，以减轻扫描透射电子显微镜（STEM）中的样品漂移问题，该方法适用于多种扫描模式和成像条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扫描透射电子显微镜（STEM）作为材料表征的常用工具，容易受到样品、样品台或电子束漂移的影响，导致图像畸变或多帧成像过程中的视场移动。虽然通常通过后处理图像配准来校正，但漂移会减少所有帧共有的可用区域。

Method: 该方法通过分析历史帧来预测即将采集的未来帧的采样网格点（sampling-grid points）。校正在两个时间尺度和两个长度尺度上进行：通过逐帧偏移扫描网格来消除长程漂移，通过逐像素偏移来最小化图像内部扭曲。

Result: 该方法在原子分辨率成像和低倍率原位视频捕获中均展示了应用实例。该框架适用于光栅扫描（raster）、蛇形扫描（serpentine）、交错扫描（interlaced）等多种扫描模式，以及顺序扫描或扫描旋转序列STEM。

Conclusion: 提出的方法能够有效减轻STEM成像中的样品漂移问题，通过预测性网格调整提高了多帧成像的稳定性和可用区域，为不同扫描模式和成像条件提供了通用的校正框架。

Abstract: Scanning transmission electron microscopy (STEM) is widely used tool for materials characterisation. However, being a scanned technique, STEM is susceptible to sample, stage or beam drift, manifesting as distortions within images or movement in the field-of-view during multi-frame imaging. Often this is corrected post-acquisition using image registration of multiple frames, but drift reduces the usable area common to all frames. Here we present a method to mitigate sample drift by analysing past frames to predict the sampling-grid points for the immediately future frame. We present this correction across two time-scales and two lengthscales. By offsetting the scan-grid framewise we remove long-range drift, and offsetting pixelwise we minimise intra-image warping. Examples are presented for both atomic-resolution imaging and lower-magnification in-situ video capture. The framework is general to raster, serpentine, interlaced and other scan patterns, as well as sequential or scan-rotation series STEM.

</details>

# math.AG [[Back]](#toc)

### [124] [From Finite-Node Conifold Geometry to BPS Structures II: Functorial Incidence and Quiver Assembly](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20110)
*Abdul Rahman*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 该论文从有限节点schober数据包出发，构造了相应的相互作用与关联层，建立了有限箭图理论数据包，并证明了其规范性质与不变性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前工作已提取了有限节点锥形退化（finite-node conifold degeneration）的固有有限代数状态数据。本文旨在构造相应的相互作用层（interaction layer）与关联层（incidence layer），为后续的分级相互作用、稳定性、BPS态及壁穿越结构提供基础。

Method: 从有限节点schober数据包$S_Σ$出发，定义了扩展顶点集$V_Σ^{\mathrm{ext}}$、由附着函子（attachment functors）决定的函子耦合关系，并构造了函子关联数据包$\mathfrak{I}_Σ$及其规范二元去范畴化$\mathcal I_Σ$。最终组装成有限箭图理论数据包$\mathfrak Q_Σ$。

Result: 证明了该数据包由有限节点schober数据规范确定，与修正的变态扩张（corrected perverse extension）及其混合霍奇模（mixed-Hodge-module）细化兼容，且在有限节点schober实现的等价变换下保持不变。

Conclusion: 成功构造了所需的相互作用与关联层，为后续研究中的分级相互作用、稳定性、BPS态及壁穿越结构（wall-crossing structures）奠定了基础。

Abstract: In previous work, we extracted the intrinsic finite algebraic state data of a finite-node conifold degeneration in the form $A_Σ:= (V_Σ,E_Σ,c_Σ)$, where $V_Σ$ is the finite node-indexed vertex set, $E_Σ$ is the nodewise coupling space, and $c_Σ$ is the coefficient vector of the corrected global extension class. The purpose of the present paper is to construct the corresponding interaction and incidence layer. Starting from the finite-node schober package $S_Σ:= (\mathcal C_{\mathrm{bulk}},\{\mathcal C_{p_k}\}_{k=1}^r,\{Φ_k,Ψ_k\}_{k=1}^r,Sh(S_Σ))$, we define the extended vertex set $V_Σ^{\mathrm{ext}} := V_Σ\sqcup \{v_{\mathrm{bulk}}\}$, the functorial coupling relation determined by the attachment functors, the resulting functorial incidence package $\mathfrak{I}_Σ:= (V_Σ^{\mathrm{ext}},\rightsquigarrow_Σ)$, and its canonical binary decategorification $\mathcal I_Σ:= (V_Σ^{\mathrm{ext}},I_Σ)$. From these data we assemble the finite quiver-theoretic package $\mathfrak Q_Σ:= (V_Σ,E_Σ,c_Σ,\mathcal F_Σ,I_Σ)$, where $\mathcal F_Σ:= \{(Φ_k,Ψ_k)\}_{k=1}^r$ is the functorial coupling datum. We prove that this package is canonically determined by the finite-node schober datum, compatible with the corrected perverse extension and its mixed-Hodge-module refinement, and invariant under equivalence of finite-node schober realizations. This yields the interaction and incidence layer required for later graded interaction, stability, BPS, and wall-crossing structures.

</details>


### [125] [Interacting Multi-Node Conifold Light Sectors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20637)
*Abdul Rahman*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 该论文研究卡拉比-丘（Calabi-Yau）三维流形有限节点锥形奇点（conifold degenerations）的相互作用轻扇区（interacting light sectors），建立了块约化结构定理（block-reduced structure theorem），分离出关系坍缩（relation collapse）和剩余相互作用（residual interaction）两个逻辑层次。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究有限节点锥形奇点从相互作用轻扇区的视角出发，尽管每个普通双重点（ordinary double point）贡献一个秩为一的局部消失扇区（local vanishing sector），但修正后的全局对象不一定能组装为节点片段的自由独立和（freely independent sum）。

Method: 使用修正的变态（perverse）和混合霍奇模（mixed-Hodge-module）退化包、修正扩展类（corrected extension classes）的全局胶合定律（global gluing law），以及F-丛（F-bundle）侧的刚柔原子分解（rigid-flexible atom decomposition），定义了相互作用多节点轻扇区包（interacting multi-node light-sector package）。

Result: 在块分离循环族（block-separated cycle family）中，有限节点包分离为两个逻辑层次：关系坍缩（由修正扩展、光滑化和分解侧的共同关系格（common relation lattice）控制）和幸存全局扇区间的剩余相互作用（由传输和原子侧的约化块相互作用矩阵（reduced block interaction matrix）控制）。

Conclusion: 该结果分离出了耦合锥形轻态（coupled conifold light states）的几何和霍奇理论前驱（Hodge-theoretic precursor），为后续多节点重述斯特罗明格锥形机制（Strominger's conifold mechanism）提供了数学输入。

Abstract: We study finite-node conifold degenerations of Calabi--Yau threefolds from the point of view of interacting light sectors. Although each ordinary double point contributes a rank-one local vanishing sector, the corrected global object need not assemble as a freely independent sum of nodewise pieces. Using the corrected perverse and mixed-Hodge-module degeneration package, the global gluing law for corrected extension classes, and the rigid-flexible atom decomposition on the \(F\)-bundle side, we define an interacting multi-node light-sector package and prove a block-reduced structure theorem. In the block-separated cycle family, the finite-node package separates into two logically distinct layers: relation collapse, controlled by a common relation lattice on the corrected-extension, smoothing, and resolution sides, and residual interaction among the surviving global sectors, controlled by a reduced block interaction matrix on the transport and atom sides. The result isolates the geometric and Hodge-theoretic precursor of coupled conifold light states and provides the mathematical input for a later multi-node reformulation of Strominger's conifold mechanism.

</details>

### [126] [Neuro-evolutionary stochastic architectures in gauge-covariant neural fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20373)
*Rodrigo Carmo Terin*

Main category: cs.NE

TL;DR: 该研究扩展了规范协变随机神经场框架，将架构级参数提升为函数空间中演化的慢随机变量，并引入与有效模型局部U(1)结构兼容的马尔可夫演化方案，通过最小实现验证了完全对称约束的Ginibre U(1)版本能够稳健地接近窄近边际区域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在扩展规范协变随机神经场（gauge-covariant stochastic neural-field）框架，通过将架构级参数提升为函数空间中演化的慢随机变量，构建一个能够提供对称约束诊断的有效理论，用于评估边际性和有限宽度效应。

Method: 方法包括：1）在经典对易场（classical commuting fields）中表述有效理论；2）引入与有效模型局部U(1)结构兼容的马尔可夫演化方案（Markovian evolutionary scheme）；3）采用最小实现，将基因型简化为权重方差参数σ_w²，适应度函数结合谱一致性、边际稳定性和对称约束临界锚。

Result: 比较三种演化模型发现，只有完全对称约束的Ginibre U(1)版本能够稳健地接近窄近边际区域（narrow near-marginal regime），并重现预测的低频有限宽度谱行为。该版本通过最大李雅普诺夫指数、放大因子和修饰谱核提供对称约束的边际性诊断。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，对称引导的有效稳定性诊断可作为受控环境中随机架构搜索的实用原则。完全对称约束的Ginibre U(1)演化模型在接近边际区域和重现有限宽度谱行为方面表现出优越性。

Abstract: We extend our gauge-covariant stochastic neural-field framework by promoting architecture-level parameters to slow stochastic variables evolving in function space. Our effective theory is formulated in terms of classical commuting fields and provides symmetry-constrained diagnostics of marginality and finite-width effects through the maximal Lyapunov exponent, the amplification factor, and dressed spectral kernels. On top of this dynamics, we introduce a Markovian evolutionary scheme compatible with the local $U(1)$ structure of the effective model. By using a minimal implementation, the genotype is reduced to the weight-variance parameter $σ_w^2$, and the fitness functional combines spectral agreement, marginal stability, and a symmetry-constrained critical anchor. Comparing three evolutionary models, we find that only the fully symmetry-constrained Ginibre $U(1)$ version robustly approaches a narrow near-marginal regime and reproduces the predicted low-frequency finite-width spectral behavior. These results support the use of symmetry-guided effective stability diagnostics as practical principles for stochastic architecture search in controlled settings.

</details>

### [127] [Exact analytical edge states in the extended Su-Schrieffer-Heeger model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20561)
*P. A. Grizzi,A. A. Aligia,P. Roura-Bas*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 本文研究了扩展Su-Schrieffer-Heeger（eSSH）模型不同相的拓扑性质，推导了半无限链边缘态的精确解析表达式，建立了体边对应关系，并给出了有限链低能边缘态的高精度近似解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究扩展Su-Schrieffer-Heeger（eSSH）模型的拓扑相，该模型包含了超越最近邻的平移不等价原子间的跃迁过程，旨在深入理解其拓扑性质。

Method: 推导了半无限eSSH链边缘态的精确解析表达式，其波函数以单位元胞衰减因子z从边界指数衰减；通过周期边界条件下体哈密顿量的绕数（winding number）确定拓扑相图。

Result: 建立了体边对应关系：绕数的变化与体能隙闭合以及边缘态解的条件|z|=1相一致；对于有限链，获得了低能边缘态的解析近似表达式，证明其具有高精度。

Conclusion: 扩展Su-Schrieffer-Heeger模型展现出清晰的拓扑相结构，体边对应关系得到严格验证，为理解超越最近邻相互作用的拓扑系统提供了理论框架。

Abstract: We investigate the topology of the different phases of the extended Su-Schrieffer-Heeger (eSSH) model, which includes hopping processes between translationally inequivalent atoms beyond nearest neighbors. Exact analytical expressions for the edge states of a semi-infinite eSSH chain are derived, with wave functions that decay exponentially from the boundary with a unit-cell decay factor z. From the winding number of the bulk Hamiltonian under periodic boundary conditions, we determine the topological phase diagram and establish the bulk-boundary correspondence: changes in the winding number coincide with bulk gap closings and with the condition |z|=1 for the edge-state solutions. For finite chains, we further obtain analytical, approximate expressions for the low-energy edge states, which are shown to be highly accurate.

</details>

### [128] [On Uniqueness of Mock Theta Functions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20034)
*Ovidiu Costin,Gerald V. Dunne,Ali Saraeb*

Main category: math.NT

TL;DR: 本文发展了一种重振（resurgent）方法来解决模拟θ函数（mock theta functions）跨越其自然边界（natural boundary）的唯一延拓问题。通过将Mordell-Appell积分表示为重振函数的拉普拉斯变换，并旋转积分路径到Stokes线，建立了模拟模关系（mock-modular relations），从而获得跨越自然边界的规范延拓。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在解决模拟θ函数跨越其自然边界的唯一延拓问题。模拟θ函数在模变换下表现出特殊行为，其跨越自然边界的延拓是数论和数学物理中的重要问题，需要发展新的解析方法来处理这类超越边界的问题。

Method: 方法基于重振理论（resurgent theory），将Mordell-Appell积分表示为重振函数的拉普拉斯变换。通过将拉普拉斯积分路径旋转π角度到Stokes线，建立了模拟θ函数与对应单变量级数之间的模拟模关系。该方法应用了经典关系持久性原则（principle of permanence of relations）的重振延拓。

Result: 证明了模拟模关系在q侧存在唯一解，其系数由对应的Mordell-Appell积分确定。这产生了跨越自然边界的规范延拓，并在每个群中挑选出了特定的模拟θ函数族。完成了对阶数为3和5情况（mf3和mf5）的完整分析。

Conclusion: 该方法为模拟θ函数跨越自然边界的唯一延拓问题提供了重振解决方案，建立了规范延拓并识别了特定函数族。该方法可自然推广到更高阶情况，一般理论将在后续论文中呈现。

Abstract: We develop a resurgent approach to the problem of unique continuation of mock theta functions across their natural boundary. The starting point is the representation of the associated Mordell-Appell integrals as Laplace transforms of resurgent functions, which serve as the primary analytic objects.
  By rotating the Laplace contour by $π$, i.e. onto the Stokes line, one obtains, in all known cases, the mock-modular relations between the Mordell-Appell integrals and the corresponding unary series in $\hat q=e^{-πi τ}$ and $\hat q_1=e^{-πi (-1/τ)}$.
  We then prove that these relations admit a unique solution on the $q$-side, expressed in terms of $q=e^{πi τ}$ and $q_1=e^{πi (-1/τ)}$, with coefficients determined by the corresponding Mordell-Appell integrals. This yields a canonical continuation across the natural boundary, given by a resurgent extension of the classical principle of permanence of relations, and singles out a distinguished family of mock theta functions in each group.
  We present a complete analysis for the order 3 and 5 cases (mf3 and mf5). The method extends naturally to higher orders; a general theory will appear in a separate paper.

</details>

### [129] [Scaling at Chiral Clock Criticality via Entanglement Renormalization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19876)
*Shiyong Guo,Brian Swingle*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究利用多尺度纠缠重整化拟设（MERA）张量网络研究Z3手性钟模型的连续量子相变临界线，发现有效标度数据从Potts固定点平滑变化，支持慢速重整化群流假设。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机是探究Z3手性钟模型的连续量子相变临界线，该临界线被认为由从3态Potts固定点到具有时空各向异性标度的另一固定点的慢速重整化群流描述。

Method: 采用多尺度纠缠重整化拟设（Multiscale Entanglement Renormalization Ansatz, MERA）张量网络，通过变分原理构建模型基态的MERA表示，从中获取基态能量、标度算子及其标度维度。

Result: 发现随着手性参数增加，有效标度数据从Potts数据开始平滑变化。在方法框架内，若重整化群流足够慢，这一结果仍可与双固定点假设保持一致。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明MERA能有效捕捉手性钟模型的复杂低能物理，并为各向异性连续场论提取场论数据，验证了该方法在研究此类系统中的应用价值。

Abstract: We employ the Multiscale Entanglement Renormalization Ansatz (MERA) tensor network to investigate a critical line of continuous quantum phase transitions of the $\mathbb{Z}_3$ chiral clock model. This critical line is believed to be described by a slow renormalization group flow from the 3-state Potts fixed point to another fixed point that features anisotropic scaling of space and time. We use the variational principle to construct a MERA representation of the model's ground state, from which we obtain the ground state energy and the set of scaling operators and their scaling dimensions. These scaling dimensions determine the critical exponents of the model, and we study these critical exponents and other scaling data as a function of the model's chiral parameter. We find a set of effective scaling data that smoothly varies starting from the Potts data as the chiral parameter is increased. Within the context of our approach, we discuss how this result may nevertheless be consistent with the two fixed point hypothesis provided the renormalization group flow is sufficiently slow. Our findings demonstrate MERA's effectiveness in capturing the complex low-energy physics of the chiral clock model and in extracting field theory data for an anisotropic continuum theory.

</details>


### [130] [Nudged Elastic Membranes for Constructing Reduced Two-Dimensional Potential Energy Surfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19964)
*Uday Sankar Manoj,Nicole Drew,Ismaila Dabo,Lukas Muechler*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出了"推弹膜方法（nudged elastic membrane method）"，用于构建势能面（PES）的二维简化表示，能够捕捉化学反应中固有的多维特征，而无需昂贵的Hessian矩阵信息。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的路径优化方法虽然广泛用于化学反应分析，但可能无法捕捉势能面（potential energy surfaces, PES）中固有的多维特征。需要一种能够揭示PES多维地形的方法，而不依赖计算成本高的Hessian信息。

Method: 作者引入了推弹膜方法（nudged elastic membrane method），该框架仅使用能量和力（forces）而不需要更昂贵的Hessian信息，在PES的化学相关区域构建二维简化势能面。

Result: 该方法在三维原型模型和三重态甲醛分子系统中得到验证。生成的膜不仅捕捉了一维反应路径特征，还揭示了真正的二维结构，如三重态甲醛PES中先前未报道的二阶鞍点（second-order saddle point）。

Conclusion: 推弹膜方法为探索超越单一路径图景的多维PES地形提供了实用途径，并能提供可直接用于后续精修的结构起点。

Abstract: Path optimization methods have been widely used and highly successful for the analysis of chemical reactions. Yet, they can fail to capture intrinsically multidimensional features of potential energy surfaces (PES). We introduce the nudged elastic membrane method, a framework for constructing two-dimensional reduced potential-energy surfaces in chemically relevant regions of a PES using only energies and forces without requiring more costly Hessian information. The method is demonstrated for a three-dimensional prototype model and for the triplet formaldehyde molecular system. In both cases, the resulting membrane captures one-dimensional reaction-path features as well as genuinely two-dimensional structures such as a yet unreported reported second-order saddle point in the PES of triplet formaldehyde. The method further provides direct access to structures that can serve as starting points for subsequent refinement. Our results show that the method offers a practical route to exploring multidimensional PES topography beyond the single-path picture.

</details>


### [131] [Mesoscopic theory of flocking with alignment and anti-alignment copying](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20251)
*Chunming Zheng*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究分析了具有成对对齐（aligning）与反对齐（anti-aligning）复制交互的集体运动随机模型，推导了从微观到介观的精确描述，发现竞争性交互在热力学极限下抑制长程极性序，而有限系统则展现出由交互组成控制的涨落诱导结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于分析集体运动中个体通过成对对齐或反对齐复制交互更新方向的随机模型，探索竞争性对齐规则如何影响群体动力学和有序性。

Method: 方法包括分析退火动力学（annealed dynamics）和淬火动力学（quenched dynamics），从圆上的微观主方程出发，通过傅里叶模式展开和系统的大N展开，推导出精确的介观描述，获得封闭的福克-普朗克方程（Fokker-Planck equations）和极化的有效随机微分方程。

Result: 结果显示，竞争性的对齐与反对齐交互在热力学极限下抑制了长程极性序（long-range polar order），而有限系统展现出由交互组成控制的非平凡涨落诱导结构（fluctuation-induced structure），结果通过吉莱斯皮模拟（Gillespie simulations）验证。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了一个解析可处理的框架，用于分析以竞争性复制规则和内在噪声为特征的集体动力学，为理解交互组成如何调控群体有序性提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We study a stochastic model of collective motion in which individuals update their orientation through pairwise aligning or anti-aligning copying interactions. We analyze both annealed dynamics, where interaction types are chosen probabilistically at each update, and quenched dynamics, where individuals are permanently assigned to aligning or anti-aligning subpopulations. Starting from the microscopic master equation on the circle, we derive an exact mesoscopic description via a Fourier-mode expansion and a systematic large $N$ expansion, obtaining closed Fokker-Planck equations and effective stochastic differential equations for the polarization. We show that competing alignment and anti-alignment suppress long-range polar order in the thermodynamic limit in both cases, while finite systems display nontrivial fluctuation-induced structure controlled by the interaction composition. Our results, validated by Gillespie simulations, establish an analytically tractable framework for collective dynamics characterized by competing copying rules and intrinsic noise.

</details>


### [132] [Spectral Fluctuation-Dissipation-Response Inequalities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20362)
*Jie Gu*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究为有限状态马尔可夫跳跃过程推导了谱涨落-耗散-响应不等式，通过比较因果磁化率与其被动平衡参考，建立了频率分辨和频率积分的界限，这些界限由稳态熵产生率、探针方差、短时扰动扩散和可逆弛豫时间尺度界定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在为有限状态马尔可夫跳跃过程（finite-state Markov jump processes）建立热力学限制，特别是在非平衡稳态下涨落-耗散定理（fluctuation-dissipation theorem, FDT）的破坏情况。通过比较因果磁化率（causal susceptibility）与被动平衡参考，为实验可测量的热力学行为提供理论框架。

Method: 通过推导谱涨落-耗散-响应不等式（spectral fluctuation-dissipation-response inequalities），建立频率分辨（frequency-resolved）和频率积分（frequency-integrated）的不等式。这些不等式将因果磁化率与其平衡参考之间的失配，与稳态熵产生率（steady-state entropy production rate）、探针方差（probe variance）、短时扰动扩散（short-time perturbation diffusion）和可逆弛豫时间尺度（reversible relaxation timescales）联系起来。

Result: 研究获得了精确恢复平衡态标准涨落-耗散定理的界限，并直接适用于可测量的因果磁化率。这些界限为驱动稳态（driven steady states）中FDT破坏提供了实验可测试的热力学限制，将非平衡响应与热力学耗散量联系起来。

Conclusion: 该研究为有限状态马尔可夫跳跃过程建立了严格的谱涨落-耗散-响应不等式，这些不等式在平衡态精确恢复标准FDT，并为非平衡稳态中的响应行为提供了由热力学量界定的实验可测试限制，从而量化了驱动系统中FDT破坏的程度。

Abstract: We derive spectral fluctuation--dissipation--response inequalities for finite-state Markov jump processes. By comparing the causal susceptibility to its passive equilibrium reference, we establish frequency-resolved and frequency-integrated inequalities that bound their mismatch in terms of the steady-state entropy production rate, probe variance, short-time perturbation diffusion, and reversible relaxation timescales. Our bounds exactly recover the standard fluctuation--dissipation theorem at equilibrium and apply directly to measurable causal susceptibilities, providing experimentally testable thermodynamic limits on FDT breakdown in driven steady states.

</details>


### [133] [Quantum many-body scars leading to time-translation symmetry breaking in kicked interacting spin models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20419)
*Ángel L. Corps,Armando Relaño,Angelo Russomanno*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究分析了具有长程相互作用的伊辛模型在周期性驱动下的动力学行为，观察到初始态与展示时间平移对称性破缺的Floquet态之间存在显著重叠，导致持续的二倍周期倍增现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解周期性驱动的长程相互作用伊辛模型中时间平移对称性破缺的机制，特别是探索初始态与Floquet态之间的重叠如何导致二倍周期倍增（period doubling）现象。

Method: 采用具有长程相互作用的伊辛模型，施加时间周期性驱动（time-periodic kicking），分析不同初始态（包括畴壁和倾斜自旋态）的动力学演化，通过Floquet理论考察π-谱配对（π-spectral pairing）和长程序（long-range order）。

Result: 研究发现初始态与展示时间平移对称性破缺的Floquet态存在显著重叠，这些态以双重态形式组织，显示π-谱配对和长程序；对于倾斜自旋初始态，有限尺寸标度分析表明二倍周期倍增振荡随系统尺寸增大而持续，且持续时间随系统尺寸指数增长。

Conclusion: 尽管展示时间平移对称性破缺的Floquet态是少数，但其数量随系统尺寸指数增长，这解释了为何多种不同初始态都能观察到二倍周期倍增现象，呈现出类似量子疤痕系统的弱遍历性破缺特征。

Abstract: We study an Ising model with long-range interactions undergoing a time-periodic kicking. For different initial states we observe persistent period doubling. When there is period doubling we find that the initial state has relevant overlap with Floquet states showing time-translation symmetry breaking, organized in doublets displaying $π$-spectral pairing (as highlighted by the $π$-spectral gap) and long-range order (as shown by the eigenvalues of the magnetization in the doublet). We observe period doubling for initial states with domain walls and tilted spins, and for the latter ones a finite-size scaling of the relevant $π$-shifted gap and magnetization eigenvalues suggests period-doubling oscillations persisting for larger system sizes and lasting a time exponential in the system size. We find that just a minority of Floquet states displays time-translation symmetry breaking while the rest is thermal, a weak-ergodicity breaking situation typical of systems with quantum scars. Although the time-translation symmetry breaking eigenstates are the minority, their number is exponential in the system size and this motivates the period doubling observed for many different initial states.

### [134] [Encounter times of random walkers with simultaneous resetting on networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20770)
*Cristian D. Suarez-Jimenez,Alejandro P. Riascos,Denis Boyer*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究了网络中多个随机游走者在同步重置协议下的动力学行为，推导了平均首次相遇时间的精确解析表达式，并建立了确定重置概率何时能减少相遇时间的一般判据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索网络中多个随机游走者在同步重置协议下的集体动力学行为，特别关注重置如何影响游走者之间的相遇过程。这为网络上的集体搜索和相遇问题提供了统一的理论框架。

Method: 方法包括为这一集体马尔可夫过程推导平均首次相遇时间的精确解析表达式，这些结果用无重置动态的转移矩阵的特征值和特征向量表示。理论预测通过规则网络和异质网络的数值结果进行验证，涵盖两个或多个游走者的相遇情况以及局部与非局部动态的组合。

Result: 研究发现同步重置能显著减少特定目标节点和初始条件下的相遇时间，但对于高度探索性动态或远距离目标则效果有限。与独立重置相比，同步重置在均匀网络中更高效，而独立重置在异质结构中可能表现更优，揭示了同步与探索之间的权衡关系。

Conclusion: 结论表明同步重置为网络上的集体搜索和相遇问题提供了统一方法，其效果取决于网络结构、目标节点和动态特性。研究建立了确定重置概率何时能优化相遇时间的一般判据，为网络搜索策略设计提供了理论指导。

Abstract: In this work, we study the dynamics of multiple random walkers on networks subject to a simultaneous resetting protocol, whereby all walkers are synchronously returned to their respective initial nodes. For this collective Markovian process, we derive exact analytical expressions for the mean first-encounter time, defined as the average time required for all walkers to meet for the first time at a given node. These results are formulated in terms of the eigenvalues and eigenvectors of the transition matrices governing the dynamics without resetting, providing a clear spectral interpretation of the impact of resetting on encounter processes. We further establish a general criterion for finite networks that determines when the introduction of a nonzero resetting probability reduces the mean first-encounter time and leads to an optimal resetting strategy. The theoretical predictions are illustrated through numerical results on regular and heterogeneous networks, for encounters involving two or more walkers, and for combinations of local and nonlocal dynamics. Our findings demonstrate that simultaneous resetting can significantly reduce encounter times for specific target nodes and initial conditions, while becoming ineffective for highly exploratory dynamics or distant targets. A comparison with independent resetting shows that simultaneous resetting is more efficient in homogeneous networks, whereas independent resetting can outperform it in heterogeneous structures, thereby revealing a trade-off between synchronization and exploration. The framework provides a unified approach to collective search and encounter problems on networks with resetting.

</details>


### [135] [Arrow of Time as an indicator of Measurement-Induced Phase Transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20828)
*Nitay Hurvitz,Alon Kochol,Victor Fleurov,Eran Sela*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于时间箭头（arrow of time）的新诊断方法，用于监测量子系统中的测量诱导相变（measurement-induced phase transitions），并证明了其临界行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 测量诱导相变（MIPTs）通常使用基于纠缠的度量进行诊断。本研究旨在开发一种基于时间箭头（AoT）的热力学互补视角，该视角源于驱动这些相变的量子测量的内在不可逆性。

Method: 研究分析了展示MIPTs的一系列模型中的时间箭头（AoT），定义为前向和后向轨迹概率的对数比。为了确定AoT是否表现出临界行为，研究构建并精确求解了一个包含非投影测量的随机量子电路模型。

Result: 研究发现，与纠缠熵类似，AoT是平均密度矩阵的非线性泛函，但与纠缠不同，它与局部算符相关联。通过解析方法证明了AoT表现出非解析行为，并确定了其临界指数。

Conclusion: 研究结果确立了时间箭头（AoT）作为监测量子系统中相变的一种新型诊断工具，为理解测量诱导相变提供了热力学视角的补充。

Abstract: Measurement-induced phase transitions (MIPTs) in monitored quantum systems are typically diagnosed using entanglement-based measures. Here, we develop a complementary thermodynamic perspective based on the arrow of time (AoT), which arises from the intrinsic irreversibility of the quantum measurements driving these transitions. We study the AoT - defined as the logarithmic ratio of forward and backward trajectory probabilities - across a family of models exhibiting MIPTs. We find that, like entanglement entropy, the AoT is a nonlinear functional of the averaged density matrix; however, in contrast to entanglement, it is associated with a local operator. To determine whether the AoT exhibits critical behavior, we formulate and exactly solve a model of a random quantum circuit with non-projective measurements. This allows us to analytically demonstrate that the AoT displays nonanalytic behavior and identify its critical exponent. Our results establish the AoT as a novel diagnostic for phase transitions in monitored quantum systems.

</details>

### [136] [An analytic formula for surface currents generating prescribed plasma equilibrium fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20713)
*Wadim Gerner*

Main category: physics.plasm-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种解析公式，用于计算线圈绕组表面的电流分布，使得等离子体电流磁场与表面电流磁场的组合能精确产生完整的等离子体平衡场，并可调整电流的环向复杂度而不改变磁场。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在解决等离子体约束装置中磁场生成的关键问题：如何通过线圈绕组表面电流精确产生所需的等离子体平衡磁场。这涉及到等离子体域（plasma domain）P、等离子体平衡场（plasma equilibrium field）B以及环绕P的线圈绕组表面（coil winding surface）Σ之间的精确匹配。

Method: 研究提供了一种解析公式（analytic formula），其输出为表面电流分布（surface current distribution）j。该公式确保毕奥-萨伐尔定律（Biot-Savart law）算子BS满足关系：BS(j) + BS(curl(B)) = B在P内成立，即表面电流磁场与等离子体电流磁场的组合精确产生完整的等离子体平衡场。

Result: 该解析公式能够在不改变磁场的情况下调整电流的环向复杂度（toroidal complexity），这为优化线圈设计提供了灵活性。研究还包含了关于数值近似（numerical approximations）方面的讨论，为实际计算提供了指导。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了一种精确计算线圈表面电流分布的解析方法，能够确保生成所需的等离子体平衡磁场，同时允许调整电流复杂度而不影响磁场分布，为聚变装置中的线圈设计提供了理论工具。

Abstract: Given a plasma domain $P\subset\mathbb{R}^3$, a plasma equilibrium field $B$ on $P$ and a coil winding surface $Σ$ surrounding $P$, we provide an analytic formula whose output is a surface current distribution $j$ on $Σ$ such that $\operatorname{BS}(j)+\operatorname{BS}(\operatorname{curl}(B))=B$ in $P$, i.e. the combination of the plasma current magnetic field and the surface current magnetic field exactly produce the full plasma equilibrium field. Further, our formula allows to adjust the toroidal complexity of the current without changing the magnetic field. Some discussions regarding aspects of numerical approximations are also included.

</details>

*Steven A. Fromm,Vassilios Mewes,O. E. Bronson Messer,Eric J. Lentz,W. Raphael Hix,J. Austin Harris*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 该研究提出了适用于在牛顿核心坍缩超新星模拟中近似广义相对论效应的有效势（effective potentials）公式，并在Chimera和Flash-X代码中实现验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于为牛顿核心坍缩超新星（core-collapse supernovae）模拟提供能够近似广义相对论效应的有效势公式，以在计算效率与物理精度之间取得平衡。

Method: 方法基于球对称时空假设和包含流体与中微子贡献的应力-能量张量，通过对爱因斯坦方程进行欧拉（Eulerian）和拉格朗日（Lagrangian）投影来确定牛顿引力势的广义相对论修正。

Result: 在Chimera和Flash-X代码中实现有效势后，进行了一系列绝热（adiabatic）和核心坍缩模拟，结果显示新有效势公式与多个其他代码的完全广义相对论模拟结果高度一致。

Conclusion: 研究表明新提出的有效势公式能够准确近似广义相对论效应，为牛顿核心坍缩超新星模拟提供了有效的广义相对论修正方案。

Abstract: We present formulations of effective potentials suitable for approximating general relativistic effects in Newtonian simulations of core-collapse supernovae. Assuming a spherically symmetric spacetime and a stress-energy tensor that includes both fluid and neutrino contributions, Eulerian and Lagrangian projections of the Einstein equations are made to determine general relativistic corrections to the Newtonian gravitational potential. We implement the effective potentials in both the Chimera and Flash-X codes, and perform a series of adiabatic and core collapse simulations. The results are compared to Newtonian and fully general relativistic simulations, as well as another widely used effective potential formulation. We find close agreement between our new effective potentials and the fully general relativistic results from multiple other codes.
