### [138] [Melting temperature shifts from quantum fluctuations in generalized Wigner crystals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19870)
*Aman Kumar,Sogoud Sherif,Veit Elser,Hitesh J. Changlani*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究挑战了量子涨落与热涨落总是协同降低相变温度的普遍观点，发现在广义维格纳晶体（GWC）中两者存在竞争关系。通过三角晶格扩展哈伯德模型计算，发现量子效应可显著提高熔化温度，与经典估计偏差超过50%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于对量子涨落与热涨落相互作用的重新审视。传统观点认为两者协同降低相变温度，但该研究基于WS₂/WSe₂异质双层莫尔系统中发现的关联绝缘"广义维格纳晶体"（generalized Wigner crystal, GWC）态，探索两者可能存在的竞争关系。

Method: 研究方法包括：1）在三角晶格扩展哈伯德模型上进行有限温度Lanczos计算，考虑双栅屏蔽势和最近邻模型；2）采用有限温度微扰理论，在经典维格纳晶体基础上微扰处理动能项；3）分析多种电子密度下的量子效应对熔化温度的影响。

Result: 研究结果显示：1）量子效应导致熔化温度相对于经典估计发生显著偏移，某些情况下偏差超过50%；2）量子熔化通过增加带宽软化基态序参量，但不会总是降低熔化温度，反而可能提高它；3）提供了量子涨落与热涨落竞争关系的定性图像。

Conclusion: 该研究颠覆了量子涨落总是降低相变温度的传统认知，揭示了在广义维格纳晶体中量子与热涨落的竞争机制。理论预测可通过调节带宽在未来的实验中验证，为理解量子材料中的相变行为提供了新视角。

Abstract: It is generally believed that quantum fluctuations collaborate with thermal fluctuations, effectively reducing transition temperatures (e.g. for melting of charge order). We show that this is not always the case and that the interplay between quantum and thermal fluctuations can be competitive. We find excellent motivation for addressing this thanks to the discovery of correlated insulating "generalized Wigner crystal" (GWC) states in hetero-bilayer transition metal dichalcogenide (WS$_2$/WSe$_2$) moiré systems [Y. Xu, et al., Nature 587, 214-218 (2020)]. We account for the impact of quantum effects on the melting temperature of GWCs, carrying out finite temperature Lanczos calculations on an extended Hubbard model on the triangular lattice (both with a double-gate screened potential, and the nearest neighbor model) for multiple electron densities. We show that quantum effects capture the shift relative to the classical estimates, which in some cases are more than 50 percent off from the experimental values. Then building on these numerical findings, we provide a qualitative picture that clarifies that while quantum melting of GWC (by increasing the bandwidth) naturally softens the ground state order parameter, it does not always decrease the melting temperature; conversely it can increase it. To do so we employ a finite temperature perturbation theory, treating the kinetic energy perturbatively on top of a classical Wigner crystal. Our predictions should be observable in future experiments where the bandwidth can be tuned.

</details>


### [139] [Field-Induced Selective Spin Gap Closure and Quantum Criticality in BaNd$_2$ZnS$_5$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20173)
*Sangyun Lee,A. J. Woods,B. Billingsley,Shengzhi Zhang,R. Movshovich,S. M. Thomas,C. A. Mizzi,B. Maiorov,Shuyi Li,Chunjing Jia,Tai Kong,Eun Sang Choi,Vivien S. Zapf,Minseong Lee*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究报道了层状稀土磁体BaNd2ZnS5中磁场诱导的模式选择性量子临界性的热力学证据，揭示了不同于传统全局软化的量子相变机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索强各向异性相互作用下稀土磁体的量子临界行为，特别是验证模式选择性（mode-selective）而非全局（global）的量子临界现象，以拓展对量子相变机制的理解。

Method: 通过热力学测量方法，包括交流磁化率（ac susceptibility）测量，分析磁场沿[110]方向时系统的临界行为，并采用标度分析（scaling analysis）验证量子临界点的普适性。

Result: 研究发现低能隙Δ_L在临界场Hc ~ 2 T处连续软化并塌缩，而高能隙Δ_H保持有隙，形成部分临界相；交流磁化率呈现普适标度行为χ_ac ~ T^-0.2，且存在有限残余索末菲系数γ_0，表明在量子临界点附近仅单一对称扇区出现无能隙激发。

Conclusion: BaNd2ZnS5作为自旋轨道耦合稀土磁体，其量子临界性具有模式选择性特征，各向异性相互作用使得不同激发扇区能够独立达到临界状态，这区别于基于低能激发全局软化的传统量子临界理论框架。

Abstract: We report thermodynamic evidence for field-induced mode-selective quantum criticality in the layered rare-earth magnet BaNd2ZnS5 (BNZS). Below the Neel temperature TN = 2.9 K, spin-orbit-entangled Nd3+ moments form two symmetry-inequivalent low-energy spin-excitation modes arising from Kramers doublet physics under a magnetic field, with distinct gaps Delta_L and Delta_H. For magnetic fields applied along the [110] direction, the lower-energy gap Delta_L softens continuously and collapses at a critical field Hc ~ 2 T, while the higher-energy gap Delta_H remains gapped, leaving the system in an intermediate partially critical phase. Despite the partial nature of the criticality, thermodynamic measurements reveal a continuous quantum phase transition. The ac susceptibility shows universal scaling behavior, with chi_ac(T, H) collapsing onto a single scaling function and following chi_ac ~ T^-0.2 at criticality. A finite residual Sommerfeld coefficient gamma_0 further indicates the emergence of gapless excitations confined to a single symmetry sector near the quantum critical point. In contrast to conventional quantum criticality based on global softening of low-energy excitations, BNZS exhibits a selective breakdown of Kramers-doublet excitations due to its strong anisotropic interactions. Our results establish BNZS as a spin-orbit-coupled rare-earth magnet where quantum criticality is not global but mode-selective, with anisotropic interactions enabling independent criticality in distinct excitation sectors.

</details>


### [140] [Symmetry breaking phases and transitions in an Ising fusion category lattice model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20201)
*Soumil Roychowdhury,Chenjie Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文研究了一个具有伊辛融合范畴（Ising fusion category）对称性的任意子链状晶格模型，揭示了包含对称临界相和两个范畴对称破缺相的丰富相图。对称相与常规临界伊辛模型属于同一普适类，而两个对称破缺相分别被命名为范畴铁磁相和范畴反铁磁相。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索具有伊辛融合范畴对称性的任意子链状晶格模型，以理解非可逆对称性（non-invertible symmetry）在相变和相结构中的独特行为。特别关注范畴对称破缺相的性质及其与常规对称破缺相的区别。

Method: 研究方法结合了数值模拟和解析分析，通过研究具有伊辛融合范畴对称性的任意子链状晶格模型，探索其相图结构和相变行为。数值方法用于分析不同相之间的转变和临界性质。

Result: 研究发现了包含三个相的丰富相图：一个对称临界相和两个范畴对称破缺相。对称相与常规临界伊辛模型属于同一普适类；范畴铁磁相完全破缺伊辛融合范畴，表现出三重基态简并；范畴反铁磁相破缺晶格平移和部分伊辛融合范畴，由四重简并的伊辛共形场论描述。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，与破缺非可逆对称性相关的反铁磁态具有指数增长的低能态流形，这是由于畴壁的量子维度大于1。相变分析显示，对称相与范畴铁磁相之间的转变由c=7/10的三临界伊辛CFT描述，而对称相与范畴反铁磁相之间的转变可能是连续的，由中心荷c=3/2的共形场论描述。

Abstract: An anyon-chain-like lattice model with symmetry described by the Ising fusion category is studied. Combining numerical and analytical studies, we uncover a rich phase diagram that contains three phases: a symmetric critical phase and two categorical symmetry breaking phases. The symmetric phase lies in the same universality class as the usual critical Ising model. The first symmetry-breaking phase, dubbed the \emph{categorical ferromagnetic} phase, has the Ising fusion category fully broken and exhibits a threefold ground-state degeneracy, as expected from the generalized Landau paradigm. The other symmetry-breaking phase is analogous to a conventional antiferromagnet: it breaks lattice translation and part of the Ising fusion category, and therefore is termed the \emph{categorical antiferromagnetic} phase. Unlike ordinary antiferromagnetic states associated with finite invertible symmetry breaking, this phase itself is critical, being described by a fourfold degenerate Ising conformal field theory. We argue more generally that antiferromagnetic states associated with broken non-invertible symmetries have a large low-energy manifold that grows exponentially in system size, due to the greater-than-one quantum dimension of domain walls. We also numerically study the transitions between the three phases. The transition between the symmetric and categorical ferromagnetic phase is described by the $c=7/10$ tricritical Ising CFT, while the transition between the symmetric and categorical antiferromagnetic phases is less understood. Our numerical data suggest that the latter transition is continuous and described by a conformal field theory with central charge $c=3/2$.

</details>


### [141] [Disorder-driven coexistence of distinct dynamical states in frustrated Sr$_3$CuNb$_2$O$_9$: a microscopic $μ$SR and $^{93}$Nb NMR study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20337)
*M. Biswas,K. Bhattacharya,K. M. Ranjith,S. M. Hossain,S. S. Islam,M. Naskar,R. Sarkar,B. Büchner,T. Shiroka,H. -J. Grafe,M. Majumder*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究通过μSR和NMR技术证实了Sr₃CuNb₂O₉中随机单态（RS）和量子自旋液体（QSL）样相的微观共存，为三维无序阻挫磁体中相关相的研究提供了重要案例。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管在无序阻挫磁体中识别奇异随机单态（random singlet, RS）作为独特相关相方面已有进展，但三维（3D）实现仍然稀少。Sr₃CuNb₂O₉被认为是一种具有磁性位点无序的3D阻挫系统，可能承载RS基态。

Method: 采用μ子自旋弛豫（muon spin relaxation, μSR）和⁹³Nb核磁共振（nuclear magnetic resonance, NMR）技术对Sr₃CuNb₂O₉进行详细微观研究。通过核磁化恢复的逆拉普拉斯变换（inverse Laplace transform, ILT）分析自旋-晶格弛豫测量数据。

Result: μSR零场弛豫率显示弛豫率随温度呈幂律发散，纵向场弛豫率也呈现幂律发散，与RS相形成一致。NMR谱明确解析出两种具有不同局域磁环境的组分，ILT获得的弛豫率分布显示快速和慢速两个分离通道，分别遵循不同的幂律温度依赖关系（T^α，α=0.6和1.1）。

Conclusion: 综合光谱和弛豫数据表明，快速通道定性代表RS样态，而慢速通道表现出量子自旋液体（quantum spin liquid, QSL）样行为，从而在Sr₃CuNb₂O₉中建立了RS和QSL样相的微观共存。

Abstract: Despite recent progress in identifying the exotic random singlet (RS) state in disordered frustrated magnets as a distinct correlated phase, three-dimensional (3D) realizations remain scarce. Sr$_3$CuNb$_2$O$_9$ was proposed to be one of such 3D frustrated systems with magnetic site disorder hosting an RS ground state. Here, we report a detailed microscopic investigation of Sr$_3$CuNb$_2$O$_9$ employing muon spin relaxation ($μ$SR) and $^{93}$Nb nuclear magnetic resonance (NMR) techniques. The $μ$SR zero-field relaxation rate reveals a power-law divergence of the relaxation rate as a function of temperature. Also, a power-law divergence is present in the relaxation rate as a function of applied longitudinal field, consistent with the formation of an RS phase. The $^{93}$Nb NMR spectra unambiguously resolve two components with distinct local magnetic environments, whose nature is further elucidated through spin-lattice relaxation measurements analyzed via an inverse Laplace transform (ILT) of the nuclear magnetization recovery. The relaxation-rate distribution obtained from ILT reveals two well-separated channels: a fast component, $(1/T_1)_{\mathrm{fast}}$, and a slow component, $(1/T_1)_{\mathrm{slow}}$. Both components follow distinct power-law temperature dependences ($T^α$), with $α= 0.6$ and $1.1$ for the fast and slow channels, respectively. The combined spectral and relaxation data demonstrate that the fast channel qualitatively represents an RS-like state, whereas the slow channel exhibits quantum spin liquid (QSL) like behavior, thereby establishing the microscopic coexistence of RS and QSL-like phases in Sr$_3$CuNb$_2$O$_9$.

</details>


### [142] [Interaction-induced asymmetry in infinite-temperature dynamical correlations of hard-core anyons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20697)
*Doru Sticlet,Ovidiu I. Pâţu,Balázs Dóra,Cătălin Paşcu Moca*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究分析了无限温度下一维晶格上相互作用硬核任意子（hard-core anyons）的动力学关联函数，揭示了分数统计（fractional statistics）对单粒子相干性和密度输运的不同影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索分数统计在高温量子系统中的动力学表现。虽然多体谱与统计相位θ无关，但动力学关联函数通过非局域的Jordan-Wigner弦（Jordan-Wigner strings）保持对θ的敏感性，这为在高熵环境中探测分数统计提供了可能。

Method: 方法包括计算单粒子格林函数（single-particle Green's functions）、谱函数（spectral functions）和密度-密度关联函数（density-density correlators）。研究比较了无相互作用（V=0）和有限最近邻相互作用（finite nearest-neighbor interactions V）的情况，分析了不同耦合强度下的动力学行为。

Result: 结果显示：无相互作用时，高温平均导致所有θ的格林函数具有反演对称性。有限相互作用在0<θ<π时产生显著的左右不对称性，最强手性出现在中间耦合V∼J处，此时格林函数以统计角依赖的衰减率指数衰减。强耦合时，动力学过渡到原子极限区（atomic-limit regime），格林函数普遍以t^{-1}衰减，谱函数显示三带结构。密度-密度关联则对统计不敏感，恢复XXZ链的已知输运行为。

Conclusion: 结论表明动力学关联函数可作为高熵量子系统中分数统计的直接探针。分数统计主要影响单粒子相干性而非密度输运，这为在高温量子系统中探测和表征任意子统计提供了理论框架。

Abstract: We study dynamical correlations of interacting hard-core anyons on a one-dimensional lattice at infinite temperature. This is a setting in which the many-body spectrum is independent of the statistical phase $θ$, while dynamical correlators remain sensitive to $θ$ through nonlocal Jordan-Wigner strings. We compute single-particle Green's functions, spectral functions, and density-density correlators, thereby separating the effects of fractional statistics on one-body coherence from those on density transport in a maximally mixed ensemble. In the noninteracting case $V=0$, high-temperature averaging leads to inversion-symmetric Green's functions for all $θ$ despite the presence of anyonic strings. Finite nearest-neighbor interactions $V$ generate, however, a pronounced left-right asymmetry in the Green's functions for $0<θ<π$, with the strongest chirality appearing at intermediate couplings $V\sim J$ where interactions and hopping compete most effectively. In this regime, the Green's function decays exponentially in time with a statistical-angle-dependent decay rate. At strong coupling, the dynamics crosses over to an atomic-limit regime in which the dependence on $θ$ is reduced. Here the Green's function decays universally as $t^{-1}$ and the corresponding spectral function displays a three-band structure. In contrast, density-density correlations are insensitive to statistics and recover the known infinite-temperature transport regimes of the XXZ chain, including ballistic, superdiffusive and diffusive behaviours. These results identify dynamical correlation functions as direct probes of fractional statistics in high-entropy quantum systems.

</details>

*Ali Rayat,Yaohang Li,Gia-Wei Chern*

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种规范等变（gauge-equivariant）图神经网络，将非阿贝尔（non-Abelian）规范对称性直接嵌入到消息传递中，为具有局域规范对称性的系统提供了通用的机器学习框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 局域规范对称性（local gauge symmetry）是基础相互作用和强关联量子物质的基础，但现有的机器学习方法缺乏处理位点依赖对称性（site-dependent symmetries）的通用框架，特别是对于本质非局域可观测量（intrinsically nonlocal observables）。

Method: 引入一种规范等变图神经网络（gauge-equivariant graph neural network），通过矩阵值、规范协变特征（matrix-valued, gauge-covariant features）和对称兼容更新，将非阿贝尔对称性直接嵌入到消息传递（message passing）中，将等变学习从全局对称性扩展到完全局域对称性。

Result: 在该框架中，消息传递实现了晶格上的规范协变传输（gauge-covariant transport），允许非局域关联和环状结构从局域操作中自然涌现。该方法在纯规范、规范-物质和动力学体系中得到验证。

Conclusion: 规范等变消息传递被确立为受局域对称性支配系统中学习的通用范式（general paradigm），为处理具有规范对称性的复杂量子系统提供了原则性机器学习框架。

Abstract: Local gauge symmetry underlies fundamental interactions and strongly correlated quantum matter, yet existing machine-learning approaches lack a general, principled framework for learning under site-dependent symmetries, particularly for intrinsically nonlocal observables. Here we introduce a gauge-equivariant graph neural network that embeds non-Abelian symmetry directly into message passing via matrix-valued, gauge-covariant features and symmetry-compatible updates, extending equivariant learning from global to fully local symmetries. In this formulation, message passing implements gauge-covariant transport across the lattice, allowing nonlocal correlations and loop-like structures to emerge naturally from local operations. We validate the approach across pure gauge, gauge-matter, and dynamical regimes, establishing gauge-equivariant message passing as a general paradigm for learning in systems governed by local symmetry.

### [144] [Unconventional Quantum Criticality in Long-Range Spin-1 Chains: Insights from Entanglement Entropy and Bipartite Fluctuations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20831)
*Justin Tim-Lok Chau,Jiarui Zhao,Nicolas Laflorencie,Zi Yang Meng*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索具有交错长程相互作用的spin-1海森堡链的基态相图，特别关注从短程区域的有隙Haldane相到长程区域的无能隙反铁磁有序Néel相之间的量子相变特性。

Method: 采用基于分裂自旋表示（split-spin representation）的量子蒙特卡洛方法，将spin-1模型映射到具有局域投影约束的spin-1/2自由度上，从而实现了高效的大规模模拟。通过有限尺寸标度分析和交叉点分析确定临界参数。

Result: 确定了连续量子相变的临界点位于α_c=2.48(2)，并提取了相关的临界指数，表明该相变具有非常规临界性。特别地，相变是非共形的，其特征是动态指数z≠1。进一步分析了纠缠熵和二分涨落（bipartite fluctuations）在相变过程中的标度行为。

Conclusion: 该研究成功解析了spin-1海森堡链中长程相互作用诱导的量子相变，揭示了从有隙Haldane相到无能隙Néel相的非共形相变特性，并确定了临界点和相关标度行为，为理解长程相互作用系统中的非常规临界现象提供了重要见解。

Abstract: We study the ground-state phase diagram of a spin-1 Heisenberg chain with staggered long-range (LR) interactions decaying as $\propto r^{-α}$ using a quantum Monte Carlo approach based on the split-spin representation. This formulation enables efficient large-scale simulations by mapping the spin-1 model onto spin-$1/2$ degrees of freedom with local projection constraints. We resolve the continuous quantum phase transition between the gapped Haldane phase at large $α$ (short-range regime) and a gapless antiferromagnetically ordered Néel phase at small $α$ (LR regime), where the continuous SU(2) symmetry is broken. From finite-size scaling and crossing point analyses, we determine the critical point to be at $α_c = 2.48(2)$ and extract the associated critical exponents, which indicate unconventional criticality. In particular, the transition is found to be nonconformal, characterized by a dynamic exponent $z \neq 1$. We further analyze the scaling of entanglement entropy and bipartite fluctuations across the transition, and determine the corresponding universal scalings in both phases and at criticality.

### [145] [Observation of impact parameter dependent modifications of nuclear parton distributions in photonuclear Pb+Pb collisions at $\sqrt{s_\mathrm{NN}} = 5.02$ TeV with the ATLAS detector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20559)
*ATLAS Collaboration*

Main category: nucl-ex

TL;DR: 该研究通过分析超周边重离子碰撞中的光子-核（γ+A）喷注产生，首次实验观测到核部分子分布函数（nPDF）的修正随碰撞参数（impact parameter）变化的现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超周边重离子碰撞中的高能光子-核散射为研究核结构提供了独特探针。本研究旨在探究γ+A喷注产生与核前向中子发射之间的关联，以理解碰撞参数对核部分子分布的影响。

Method: 使用ATLAS探测器在LHC上采集的5.02 TeV Pb+Pb超周边碰撞数据（积分亮度1.72 nb⁻¹）。通过反-kₜ算法重建R=0.4喷注，利用粒子级光子动量分数（z₋）或核部分子动量分数（x₊）表征硬γ+A过程的运动学。

Result: 在低z₋区域（非衍射成分主导），未伴随前向中子发射的碰撞中核部分子分布可被清晰探测，且靶核基本保持完整。γ+A截面作为x₊函数的形状在有无前向中子发射的碰撞中存在显著差异（6.0σ显著性）。

Conclusion: 大x₊区域的结果表明，大碰撞参数（b_A）的碰撞中未观察到通常核硬散射过程中部分子分布的修正，而小碰撞参数的碰撞则存在修正。这首次实验证实核部分子分布函数的修正随碰撞参数变化。

Abstract: High-energy photonuclear ($γ+A$) scattering in ultra-peripheral heavy-ion collisions provides a unique probe of nuclear structure. This Letter studies the dependence of $γ+A$ jet production in ultra-peripheral Pb+Pb collisions at $\sqrt{s_{_\text{NN}}} = 5.02$ TeV on the presence of forward neutron emission from either nucleus. The data was taken in 2018 with the ATLAS detector at the LHC and corresponds to an integrated luminosity of $1.72$ nb$^{-1}$. The kinematics of the hard $γ+A$ processes, expressed via the particle-level photon ($z_{-}$) or nuclear parton ($x_{+}$) momentum fractions, are determined from $R = 0.4$ jets reconstructed using the anti-$k_t$ algorithm. At lower $z_{-}$, where the non-diffractive component dominates, the nuclear parton distribution can be cleanly probed in collisions that leave the struck nucleus essentially intact. Such collisions are expected to probe larger impact parameters ($b_\text{A}$) within the target. The shape of the $γ+A$ cross-section as a function of $x_{+}$ in such collisions is found to differ from that in $γ+A$ collisions accompanied by forward neutron emission, with an observed significance of $6.0σ$. These results are consistent at large $x_{+}$ with large $b_\text{A}$ collisions exhibiting no modifications to the parton distributions that are usually observed in hard scattering processes involving nuclei, relative to collisions with smaller $b_\text{A}$. Thus, these measurements provide an experimental observation that the modifications to nuclear parton distributions vary with impact parameter.

### [146] [Broadband dielectric permittivity tensor of muscovite for next-generation all van der Waals photonic components](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20023)
*Meri Hayrapetyan,Maksim Sargsyan,David Karakhanyan,Ani Khachatryan,Maria Levonyan,Dmitrii Litvinov,Maciej Koperski,Artsruni Margaryan,Makars Šiškins,Kostya S. Novoselov,Davit A. Ghazaryan*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过解析云母的各向异性振动响应，在宽带紫外（ultraviolet, UV）到近红外（near-infrared, NIR）光谱区域提取精确的介电常数张量分量，并基于其特性设计范德华异质结构。

Result: 研究发现范德华云母具有一致的低折射率、可忽略的消光系数和弱的面内各向异性，在薄膜极限下可有效视为单轴介电材料；基于此设计的分布式布拉格反射镜（distributed Bragg reflectors, DBR）和二向色分束器（dichroic beam splitters, DBS）在近红外光谱区域表现出高效率的稳健光学性能。

Conclusion: 该研究突出了低折射率、无损耗范德华晶体的重要性，将云母定位为下一代宽带全范德华纳米光子组件的极具前景的原子级平坦构建模块。

Abstract: We report a comprehensive determination of the broadband dielectric permittivity tensor of van der Waals (vdW) muscovite also referred to as mica, establishing it as a low-index low-loss platform for ultrathin nanophotonics. Resolving its anisotropic vibrational response and extracting accurate tensor components across broadband ultraviolet (UV) to near-infrared (NIR) spectral region, we show that vdW muscovite exhibits consistently low refractive indices negligible extinction and weak in-plane anisotropy allowing its effective treatment as a uniaxial dielectric in thin-film limits. Leveraging these properties, we design muscovite based vdW heterostructures pairing it MoS2, engineering few-layer distributed Bragg reflectors (DBR) and dichroic beam splitters (DBS) with high efficiency robust optical performance in a broad NIR spectral region achieved with sub-micron thicknesses. Our findings spotlight the high significance of low-index extinctionless vdW crystals, positioning muscovite as a highly perspective atomically flat building block for next-generation, broadband, all-vdW nanophotonic components.

### [147] [Control Over Fano Parameter in Grating and One-Dimensional Photonic Crystal Cavity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20451)
*Pratip Ghosh,Akshay K. Naik*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文展示了一种在硅波导-光栅平台上集成的一维光子晶体腔中，通过热光效应动态调控法诺共振（Fano resonance）不对称参数的方法，实现了从-3.2到+1.7的调谐范围，最高消光比达21.6 dB，光谱斜率达108 dB/nm。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 法诺共振（Fano resonance）的尖锐不对称光谱峰对系统参数高度敏感，已被用于增强光-物质相互作用及传感、滤波等应用。然而，若能动态改变法诺斜率和光谱相位，将能在器件制造后针对不同应用优化参数。

Method: 研究采用集成在硅波导-光栅平台上的一维光子晶体腔（one-dimensional photonics crystal cavity），其中法诺共振源于腔模与光栅耦合器产生的振荡背景之间的干涉。通过硅的热光效应（thermos-optic effect）实现了法诺不对称参数的动态调谐。

Result: 实验成功将法诺参数从约-3.2调谐至+1.7，实现了最高21.6 dB的消光比（extinction ratio）和108 dB/nm的光谱斜率（spectral slope）。该设计具有超紧凑、制造简单、可集成多个腔或反馈元件的特点。

Conclusion: 陡峭的斜率相比传统腔在传感和调制应用中具有明显优势，而可调谐性使得能够动态控制增益、动态范围、带宽和噪声耦合，为优化器件性能提供了灵活手段。

Abstract: Fano resonances are sharp asymmetrical spectral peaks which are now ubiquitous in nanophotonics. The high sensitivity of these resonances to system parameter has been exploited to improve light matter interaction and in applications such as sensing, filters and on-chip processing. The ability to dynamically change the Fano slope and spectral phase would enable optimization of the device parameters post fabrication for various applications. Here we demonstrate such a control over the Fano resonance in a one-dimensional photonics crystal cavity integrated on a silicon waveguide -grating platform. In our device, Fano resonance arises due to interference between cavity mode and an oscillatory background due to grating coupler. The dynamics tuning of Fano asymmetric parameter is achieved using thermos-optic effect in silicon. We experimentally tune the Fano parameter from ~-3.2 to +1.7 achieving a highest extinction ratio of 21.6 dB and spectral slope of 108dB/nm. All the above is achieved in an ultra-compact design with simple fabrication and with multiple cavities or feedback elements. The steep slope offers distinct advantage over conventional cavity for sensing and modulation applications and the tunability enables dynamic control over gain, dynamic range, bandwidth and noise coupling.

</details>


### [148] [Toward nanophotonic platforms for solid-state $^{229}$Th nuclear clocks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20687)
*Sandro Kraemer,Karen Mamian,Toby Bi,Shun Fujii,Jan de Haan,Harshith Babu,Arno Claessens,Rafael Ferrer Garcia,Fedor Ivandikov,Piet Van Duppen,Andreas Dragoun,Christoph E. Abstract: While the $^{229}$Th nuclear isomer has recently been observed and laser-excited, converting optical nuclear manipulation into a chip-scale solid-state frequency standard remains an open challenge. Here, we present a nanophotonic platform to realize an all-solid-state nuclear clock based on the low-energy isomeric transition of $^{229}$Th embedded in high-$Q$ fluoride photonic resonators. By coupling ensembles of thorium nuclei to confined optical modes, we show that resonant field build-up in the cavity can substantially enhance the nuclear excitation rate, enabling optical interrogation at practical laser intensities. As an initial proof of concept, we implant a crystalline fluoride whispering-gallery-mode resonator with $^{229}$Th and assess the impact of implantation-induced damage on resonator performance. Our platform leverages recent advances in materials integration and nanophotonics to chart a realistic route toward compact and scalable nuclear frequency standards.

### [149] [Universal $2$-parameter $\mathcal{N}=2$ supersymmetric $\mathcal{W}_{\infty}$-algebra](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20750)
*Thomas Creutzig,Volodymyr Kovalchuk,Andrew R. Linshaw,Arim Song,Uhi Rinn Suh*

Main category: math.RT

TL;DR: 本文将顶点代数（vertex algebra）的$\mathcal{W}_\infty$理论推广到$\mathcal{N}=2$超共形（superconformal）情形，证明了Gaberdiel-Candu猜想，建立了$\mathcal{N}=2$超对称$Y$-代数（$Y$-algebra）及其对偶性，并由此得到$\mathcal{W}^k(\mathfrak{sl}_{n+1|n})$的强有理性和模范畴描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于将$\mathcal{W}_\infty$顶点代数理论推广到$\mathcal{N}=2$超共形情形。具体包括：证明Gaberdiel和Candu在2013年关于存在普遍$\mathcal{N}=2$超共形顶点代数$\mathcal{W}^{\mathcal{N}=2}_\infty$的猜想；验证Procházka和Rapčák在2018年提出的$\mathcal{N}=2$超对称$Y$-代数对偶性猜想；以及证明Ito在1992年提出的主$\mathcal{W}$-代数（principal $\mathcal{W}$-algebra）$\mathcal{W}^k(\mathfrak{sl}_{n+1|n})$的coset实现。

Method: 方法基于构建$\mathcal{N}=2$超共形代数（$\mathcal{N}=2$ superconformal algebra）的扩展——普遍二参数顶点代数$\mathcal{W}^{\mathcal{N}=2}_\infty$，该代数对每个整数$i>1$包含四个额外生成元（generator）。通过研究其一参数商代数（即$\mathcal{N}=2$超对称$Y$-代数），并证明这些代数之间的对偶关系（duality）。

Result: 主要结果包括：证明了Gaberdiel-Candu猜想，即存在普遍$\mathcal{N}=2$超共形顶点代数$\mathcal{W}^{\mathcal{N}=2}_\infty$；证明了Procházka-Rapčák关于$\mathcal{N}=2$超对称$Y$-代数对偶性的猜想；作为特例，证明了Ito关于主$\mathcal{W}$-代数$\mathcal{W}^k(\mathfrak{sl}_{n+1|n})$的coset实现猜想。

Conclusion: 结论表明，$\mathcal{N}=2$超共形顶点代数理论成功推广了经典$\mathcal{W}_\infty$框架。作为推论，获得了$\mathcal{W}_k(\mathfrak{sl}_{n+1|n})$在参数$k = -1 + \frac{1}{n+a+1}$下的强理性（strong rationality），并描述了其模范畴（module category），这推广了Adamovič在1999年关于$\mathcal{N}=2$最小模型（minimal model）的结果（$n=1$情形）。

Abstract: The universal $2$-parameter vertex algebra $\mathcal{W}_{\infty}$ of type $\mathcal{W}(2,3,\dots)$ is a classifying object for vertex algebras of type $\mathcal{W}(2,3,\dots,N)$ for some $N$; under mild hypotheses, all such vertex algebras arise as quotients of $\mathcal{W}_{\infty}$. In 2017, Gaiotto and Rapčák introduced a family of such vertex algebras called $Y$-algebras, and conjectured that they fall into groups of three that are mutually isomorphic. This is a common generalization of both Feigin-Frenkel duality and the coset realization of principal $\mathcal{W}$-algebras in type $A$, and was proven in 2021 for the simple $Y$-algebras (i.e., one label is zero) by the first and third authors. In this paper, we extend this entire story to the $\mathcal{N}=2$ superconformal setting. First, we prove the 2013 conjecture of Gaberdiel and Candu that there exists a universal $2$-parameter vertex algebra $\mathcal{W}^{\mathcal{N}=2}_{\infty}$ which is an extension of the $\mathcal{N}=2$ superconformal algebra, and has four additional generators in weights $i, i + \frac{1}{2}, i + \frac{1}{2}, i+1$, for each integer $i > 1$. This admits many $1$-parameter quotients which we call $\mathcal{N}=2$ supersymmetric $Y$-algebras, and we prove the dualities among these algebras which were conjectured in 2018 by Prochazka and Rapčák. A special case is the coset realization of the principal $\mathcal{W}$-algebra $\mathcal{W}^k(\mathfrak{sl}_{n+1|n})$ which was conjectured in 1992 by Ito. As a corollary, we obtain the strong rationality of $\mathcal{W}_k(\mathfrak{sl}_{n+1|n})$ for $k = -1 + \frac{1}{n+a+1}$ for all positive integers $n,a$, and we describe its module category. This generalizes Adamović's 1999 result on $\mathcal{N}=2$ minimal models, which is the case $n=1$.

Abstract: Releasing shell-shaped Bose-Einstein condensates from their confinement produces a spherically symmetric density distribution characterized by concentric ripples surrounding a central peak.   <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 方法基于Jacobson的热力学引力解释，从克劳修斯关系推导场方程，并将范德瓦尔斯状态方程（van der Waals equation of state）的非理想热力学效应引入引力理论，获得修正的引力场方程。

Result: 研究结果表明，修正后的引力场方程中有效引力耦合不再是常数，而是随时空系统性质演化。这种动力学行为在高能区域产生重要后果，特别是为规避标准大爆炸宇宙学的初始奇点提供了自然机制，并产生了非奇异黑洞解。

Conclusion: 结论指出，将非理想热力学特征纳入时空描述，可能为解决经典引力理论中的基本奇点问题提供一致途径，表明热力学方法在引力理论修正中具有重要潜力。

Abstract: In this study, we propose an extension of general relativity inspired by the van der Waals equation of state, incorporating non-ideal thermodynamic effects into the gravitational sector. Our approach is based on the thermodynamic interpretation of gravity introduced by Jacobson, in which the field equations arise from the Clausius relation. Within this framework, we obtain modified gravitational field equations in which the effective gravitational coupling is no longer constant, but instead evolves with the properties of the underlying spacetime system. This dynamical behavior leads to significant consequences in high-energy regimes. In particular, it provides a natural mechanism for avoiding the initial singularity of standard Big Bang cosmology and gives rise to non-singular black hole solutions. These findings indicate that incorporating non-ideal thermodynamic features into the description of spacetime may offer a consistent route toward resolving fundamental singularities in classical gravitational theory.

### [152] [Greybody Factor, Resonant Frequencies, and Entropy Quantization of Charged Scalar Fields in the Kerr-EMDA Black Hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19848)
*Nazım Sertkan,İzzet Sakallı*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究分析了爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-伸缩子-轴子（EMDA）理论中旋转黑洞（Kerr-EMDA BH）背景下带电有质量标量场的扰动。通过规范协变克莱因-戈尔登方程（KGE）的变量分离，得到了角向和径向部分的合流Heun函数（CHFs）精确解，并推导出共振频率谱和熵量子。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-伸缩子-轴子（Einstein-Maxwell-Dilaton-Axion, EMDA）理论中旋转黑洞背景下带电标量场扰动的物理特性。与先前Senjaya和Ponglertsakul处理的中性标量场不同，电磁耦合参数q从根本上改变了Heun参数的结构并产生新的物理现象。

Method: 从规范协变克莱因-戈尔登方程（gauge-covariant Klein-Gordon equation, KGE）出发，进行完全的变量分离，获得角向和径向部分的合流Heun函数（confluent Heun functions, CHFs）精确解析解。应用CHF多项式条件推导共振频率谱，并通过Maggiore方法和黑洞热力学第一定律计算熵量子。

Result: 共振频率谱的虚部以|Δω_I| = 1/(2M)等间距分布，该间距仅由黑洞质量决定。熵量子δS_BH = 4πr_+/(r_+ - r_-)依赖于参数，在Schwarzschild情况下简化为4π，但在极端情况下发散。在无质量无电荷极限下，CHF退化为高斯超几何函数，首次计算了Kerr-EMDA几何的解析灰体因子（greybody factor, GF）。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了Kerr-EMDA黑洞背景下带电标量场扰动的完整解析处理，揭示了电磁耦合对Heun参数结构的根本性改变。伸缩子变形参数D将Kerr-EMDA谱与标准Kerr和Kerr-Newman情况区分开来，无质量带电标量情况下的闭合形式灰体因子捕捉了超辐射放大效应。

Abstract: We study charged massive scalar field perturbations on the rotating black hole (BH) background of Einstein-Maxwell-Dilaton-Axion (EMDA) theory, known as the Kerr-EMDA BH. Starting from the gauge-covariant Klein-Gordon equation (KGE), we perform a full separation of variables and obtain exact analytical solutions for both the angular and radial parts in terms of confluent Heun functions (CHFs). Unlike the earlier neutral scalar treatment by Senjaya and Ponglertsakul [Eur. Phys. J. C \textbf{85}, 352 (2025)], the electromagnetic coupling $q$ fundamentally alters the structure of the Heun parameters and produces qualitatively new physics. Applying the CHF polynomial condition, we derive the resonant frequency spectrum whose imaginary parts are equispaced with $|Δω_I| = 1/(2M)$, a universal spacing determined solely by the BH mass. Via the Maggiore prescription and the first law of BH thermodynamics, this yields a parameter-dependent entropy quantum $δS_{\text{BH}} = 4πr_+/(r_+ - r_-)$, which reduces to $4π$ for Schwarzschild but diverges at extremality -- {\color{black}in contrast to the universal $2π$ obtained for the rotating linear dilaton BH (RLDBH).} We construct the effective potential governing scalar wave scattering and analyze its dependence on the dilaton parameter $D$, rotation $a$, and scalar charge $q$. In the massless uncharged limit, the CHF reduces to the Gauss hypergeometric function, {\color{black}enabling us to compute the first analytical greybody factor (GF) for the Kerr-EMDA geometry; we show that this reduction extends to massless charged scalars, yielding a closed-form GF that captures superradiant amplification.} We examine how the dilaton deformation distinguishes the Kerr-EMDA spectrum from the standard Kerr and Kerr-Newman cases.

</details>

Relativ. Gravit.} \textbf{38} (2006), 1285; \textit{Eur. Phys. J. C} \textbf{77} (2017) 528], using Hubble's horizon cutoff in $f(R,T)=μR+νT$ model considering pressureless dark matter. We have examined the equation of state (EoS) parameters in this scenario. The deceleration parameter has been evaluated for this interacting model to justify the late-time acceleration of the expanding universe. We have also studied the cosmological consequences of Statefinder pair, $O_{m}(z)$ diagnostics, $r-q$ plane, and $w_{DE}-w^{'}_{DE}$ pair for interacting THDE in $f(R,T)=μR+νT$ model. We have also illustrated the cosmology of the interacting THDE using Hubble's horizon cutoff in $f(R,T)=R+γR^2+ξT$ model. The EoS parameter, deceleration parameter and Statefinder pair are studied in this interacting scenario. Attainment of $Λ$CDM fixed point has been observed for both models. ### [154] [Two-Point Padé Approximants for the Deflection of Light in the Schwarzschild Black Hole Metric](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19952)
*Don N. Page*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了两种近似方法来计算史瓦西黑洞（Schwarzschild black hole）附近光线的偏转角（deflection angle）：一种是精确覆盖全范围参数的[2,2]阶帕德两点逼近（Padé 2-point approximants），另一种是在中间范围有效的简化二次逼近（quadratic approximation）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管史瓦西黑洞的光线偏转角计算已有Darwin（1959）的椭圆积分精确解及多种近似方法，但现有近似要么适用于参数不太小的情况，要么仅适用于接近临界参数的情况。本文旨在提供覆盖全范围参数（大于临界参数）的更精确近似。

Method: 本文提出了两种近似方法：1）使用[2,2]阶帕德两点逼近（Padé 2-point approximants），即具有二次分子和分母的有理函数，将临界参数与实际参数之比关联到偏转角负指数的指数函数；2）一种更简单的二次逼近（quadratic approximation），在参数范围中间部分表现良好。

Result: [2,2]阶帕德两点逼近能够相当精确地覆盖所有大于临界参数（critical impact parameter）的完整参数范围，对应所有保持在黑洞外部的光子轨迹。简化二次逼近在参数范围中间部分表现同样良好，但在极端参数值处精度较差。

Conclusion: 本文提供了两种改进的近似方法用于计算史瓦西黑洞的光线偏转角，其中[2,2]阶帕德两点逼近能够精确覆盖全参数范围，而简化二次逼近则为中间范围提供了有效的计算方案。

Abstract: The deflection angle of a light ray passing the Schwarzschild (spherically symmetric vacuum) black hole was calculated by Charles Galton Darwin in 1959 in terms of the elliptic integral of the first kind. This calculation has been repeated many times and has also been given approximately in terms of elementary functions for impact parameters that either are not too small or are close to the critical impact parameter. Here I present Padé 2-point approximants of order [2,2] (quadratic numerators and denominators), relating the critical impact parameter divided by the actual impact parameter to the exponential of the negative of the deflection angle, that fairly accurately cover the full range of impact parameters greater than the critical impact parameter, which is the case for all photon trajectories that remain outside the black hole. I also present a simpler quadratic approximation that works as well in the middle of the range but not so well at the extremes.

</details>


### [155] [Regular Black Holes in General Relativity from Nonlinear Electrodynamics with de Sitter Cores](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20066)
*A. A. Araújo Filho,Ednaldo L. B. Junior,José Tarciso S. S. Junior,Francisco S. N. Lobo,Jorde A. A. Ramos,Manuel E. Rodrigues,Diego Rubiera-Garcia,Luís F. Dias da Silva,Henrique A. Vieira*

TL;DR: 该研究在广义相对论（GR）框架下构建了新的正则黑洞（regular black hole）解，这些解由非线性电动力学（NLED）的纯磁单极子（purely magnetic monopole）物质支持，并通过事件视界望远镜（Event Horizon Telescope）对Sgr A*的观测数据约束模型参数，同时分析了其动力学稳定性。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索广义相对论框架下由非线性电动力学物质支持的正则黑洞解。这类解能够避免传统黑洞解中的奇点（singularity）问题，同时需要与天体物理观测（特别是事件视界望远镜对Sgr A*的观测）相符合。

Method: 采用静态球对称框架和可变状态方程（variable equation of state）方法，明确重构了对应的非线性电动力学拉格朗日量（NLED Lagrangian）。通过分析度规函数、克雷奇曼标量（Kretschmann scalar）的正则性、能量密度和压力分布来检验几何结构，并利用有效几何（effective geometry）概念考虑光子传播。

Result: 成功构建了新的正则黑洞解，其中心区域行为正则（regular）。通过比较预测的中心暗区尺寸与Sgr A*的观测图像，约束了模型参数。通过计算准正规模谱（quasinormal mode spectrum）和进行时域分析（time-domain analysis），研究了这些构型在标量扰动下的动力学稳定性。

Conclusion: 该研究在广义相对论中建立了由非线性电动力学支持的正则黑洞解，这些解在几何上正则且与当前观测数据相容。动力学稳定性分析为进一步研究这类天体物理对象的可行性提供了重要依据。

Abstract: We present new regular black hole solutions in general relativity (GR) within a static, spherically symmetric framework governed by a variable equation of state, following the approach of [Class. Quant. Grav. 42, 025024 (2025)]. The matter supporting these geometries is identified as a purely magnetic monopole configuration of the Maxwell-Faraday tensor in the context of nonlinear electrodynamics (NLED). We explicitly reconstruct the corresponding NLED Lagrangian and analyze the asymptotic and central behaviors of the solutions. The geometric structure is examined through the metric functions, the regularity of the Kretschmann scalar, and the profiles of energy density and pressures, including a discussion of the resulting energy conditions. Using Event Horizon Telescope observations of Sgr A$^*$, we constrain the model parameters by comparing the predicted size of the central dark region with the inferred observational images, taking into account the effective geometry experienced by photons in the presence of NLED. Finally, we investigate the dynamical stability of these configurations under scalar perturbations by computing the quasinormal mode spectrum and performing a time-domain analysis.

</details>


### [156] [Thermodynamics and phase transitions of nonlinearly scalarized black holes in Einstein-scalar-Gauss-Bonnet theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20153)
*De-Cheng Zou,Xu Yang,Meng-Yun Lai,Hyat Huang,Yun Soo Myung*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探究爱因斯坦-标量-高斯-博内理论中具有多项式耦合函数的静态非线性标量化黑洞的热力学特性，特别是这些黑洞解的热力学行为。

Method: 基于先前构建的标量化解，计算了这些标量化黑洞的热力学量，并检验了黑洞热力学第一定律，同时考虑了史瓦西黑洞与标量化黑洞之间的相变。

Result: 研究结果表明，从史瓦西黑洞到标量化黑洞的相变是一级相变（first-order phase transition），且伴随非零潜热（non-zero latent heat）。

Conclusion: 该研究成功分析了爱因斯坦-标量-高斯-博内理论中静态非线性标量化黑洞的热力学性质，揭示了史瓦西黑洞向标量化黑洞转变的相变特性为一阶相变。

Abstract: We investigate the thermodynamic properties of static nonlinearly scalarized black holes in Einstein-scalar-Gauss-Bonnet theory with polynomial coupling functions. Based on the scalarized solutions constructed previously, we compute thermodynamical quantities of these scalarized black holes. Moreover, we examine the first law of black hole thermodynamics and consider the phase transitions between Schwarzschild and scalarized black holes. It shows that a phase transition from Schwarzschild black hole to scalarized black hole is a first-order with non-zero latent heat.

### [157] [Quantum description of gravitational waves generated by a classical source](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20228)
*Felix Laga,Teruaki Suyama*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了由经典能量-动量张量产生的引力波（gravitational waves）的量子特性，证明量子场论计算能精确重现经典推迟解，并发现引力子（graviton）发射符合泊松过程（Poisson process），建立了经典波描述有效性的定量判据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解经典源产生的引力波的量子特性，探讨量子场论描述与经典描述之间的关系，并评估经典近似在不同尺度物理系统中的有效性。

Method: 将引力波场视为与经典源耦合的量子场，计算引力波算符的期望值，分析发射引力子的平均值和方差，建立经典波描述有效性的定量判据。

Result: 引力波算符的期望值精确重现了经典推迟解，发射引力子的平均值与方差相等，表明引力子发射符合泊松过程，对应相干态（coherent state）。经典近似对天体物理源极为精确，但实验室尺度系统可能进入引力子发射离散性显著的区域。

Conclusion: 经典源产生的引力波量子描述与经典解一致，引力子发射表现为相干态的泊松过程。建立了区分经典与量子引力波描述的有效判据，为不同尺度系统的引力辐射研究提供了理论框架。

Abstract: We investigate the quantum properties of gravitational waves (GWs) generated by a classical energy-momentum tensor. Treating the GW field as a quantum field coupled to a classical source, we evaluate the expectation value of the GW operator. We demonstrate that this expectation value exactly reproduces the classical retarded solution. Furthermore, we show that the mean and variance of the number of emitted gravitons are equal. This suggests that the graviton emission is a Poisson process, as expected for a coherent state. We establish a quantitative criterion for the validity of the classical wave description. By applying this criterion, we find that the classical approximation is remarkably accurate for astrophysical sources, but laboratory-scale systems may reside in a regime where the discrete nature of graviton emission becomes significant.

</details>


### [158] [Reshaping the inner shadow of a Kerr black hole by a torn accretion disk](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20499)
*Shiyang Hu,Dan Li,Chen Deng,Kejian He*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过构建撕裂吸积盘（torn accretion disk）模型，数值模拟了Kerr黑洞的内阴影（inner shadow）形态演化，发现撕裂盘几何结构会导致内阴影严重侵蚀并产生分叉阴影、新月状结构等多重奇异形态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当吸积流延伸至事件视界时，其交汇处定义了内阴影轮廓，但这一关键特征在撕裂吸积盘系统中的形态演化尚未得到充分探索。撕裂吸积盘由倾斜盘被参考系拖曳（frame-dragging）破坏形成的不同子盘构成。

Method: 本文现象学地构建了撕裂吸积盘模型，并采用相对论性反向光线追踪（relativistic backward ray-tracing）方法数值模拟了Kerr黑洞的内阴影。

Result: 研究发现撕裂盘几何结构显著改变了黑洞的观测特征，导致内阴影严重侵蚀，并产生分叉阴影（bifurcated shadows）、新月状结构（crescent-like structures）以及多重阶次的阴影环（multiple orders of shadow rings）等新颖特征。

Conclusion: 这些奇异形态主要受子盘间的空间不连续性以及外子盘的倾斜角控制，难以在标准赤道吸积范式中复现。这些独特的阴影结构可作为撕裂吸积环境的稳健诊断探针，同时表明仅依赖内阴影测试引力理论是根本不足的。

Abstract: When an accretion flow extends to the event horizon, their intersection defines the contour of the inner shadow. However, the morphological evolution of this critical feature remains largely unexplored within a torn accretion disk system, a configuration comprising distinct sub-disks formed when a tilted disk is disrupted by frame-dragging. To address this, we phenomenologically construct a torn accretion disk model and numerically simulate the inner shadow of a Kerr black hole using relativistic backward ray-tracing. We discover that the torn disk geometry profoundly alters the black hole's observational signatures, inducing severe erosion of the inner shadow and generating novel features such as bifurcated shadows, crescent-like structures, and multiple orders of shadow rings. These exotic morphologies, which are predominantly governed by the spatial discontinuity between the sub-disks and the tilt angle of the outer sub-disk, are exceedingly difficult to replicate within standard equatorial accretion paradigms. Our findings demonstrate that these distinctive shadow structures hold significant potential to serve as robust diagnostic probes for torn accretion environments, simultaneously implying that relying solely on the inner shadow to test gravity theories is fundamentally insufficient.

</details>


### [159] [Astrophysically Realistic Secondary Spins Trigger Chaos in Schwarzschild Spacetime and Discernible Gravitational Wave Signatures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20533)
*Dan-Dan Yuan,Jia-Geng Jiao,Yu-Qi Lei,Jun-Xi Shi,Jing-Qi Lai,Caiying Shao,Yu Tian*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 研究发现，极端质量比旋近（extreme-mass-ratio inspirals）中的混沌现象在次级天体（secondary）的自旋处于天体物理现实范围内时依然存在，这种非可积动力学在引力波信号中留下清晰特征，次级自旋仅改变其最大允许值的1%即可驱动系统从规则运动转变为混沌运动。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点认为极端质量比旋近中的混沌需要不切实际的大次级自旋，使其天体物理相关性存疑。本研究旨在探索在次级自旋处于天体物理现实范围内时，混沌现象是否依然存在及其可观测特征。

Method: 研究分析了自旋次级天体绕史瓦西黑洞（Schwarzschild black hole）的轨道动力学，通过比较邻近的规则和混沌轨迹在时域和频域的特征差异，并引入了局部谱平坦度（local spectral-flatness）测量方法。

Result: 混沌在次级自旋的天体物理现实范围内持续存在，混沌信号在频域呈现更不离散的结构，具有密集的峰间功率；局部谱平坦度测量显示混沌信号比邻近规则信号大数百倍；次级自旋仅改变其最大允许值的1%即可触发从规则到混沌的转变。

Conclusion: 极端质量比旋近中的混沌现象具有天体物理现实性，其非可积动力学在引力波中产生可探测的独特特征，特别是通过谱平坦度测量和次级自旋微小变化引发的动力学转变，为引力波天文学提供了新的探测可能性。

Abstract: Chaos in extreme-mass-ratio inspirals is often thought to require unrealistically large secondary spins, making its astrophysical relevance uncertain. However, we find that chaos persists across the astrophysically realistic spin range for a spinning secondary orbiting a Schwarzschild black hole. This nonintegrable dynamics leaves clear signatures in the emitted gravitational waves. Nearby regular and chaotic trajectories can remain similar in the time domain and retain broadly aligned dominant spectral peaks, yet chaotic signals develop a much less discrete frequency-domain structure with dense inter-peak power. Furthermore, we introduce a local spectral-flatness measure and find it to be several hundred times larger for the chaotic signal than for the neighboring regular signals. Finally, a change in the secondary spin by as little as \(1\%\) of its maximal physically allowed value can drive the system from regular to chaotic motion and produce distinctive detector-level waveforms.

### [160] [Time evolution of a Nambu-Goto string coiling around a Kerr black hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20656)
*Hirotaka Yoshino,Kousuke Tanaka*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究通过解析展开和数值模拟分析了Nambu-Goto弦在Kerr黑洞赤道面上的时间演化，发现弦被黑洞拖拽旋转并缠绕，短期内发生能量提取过程，随后系统趋于Boos和Frolov发现的静态构型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然刚性旋转弦与Kerr黑洞相互作用的能量提取特性已被充分研究，但非刚性旋转弦的行为尚不清楚。本文旨在研究Nambu-Goto弦在Kerr时空赤道面上的时间演化过程，以填补这一知识空白。

Method: 采用两种互补方法：对时间t的级数展开（适用于t≲4M）和数值模拟（适用于t≲38M），其中M为黑洞质量。研究设定弦一端固定在视界上并延伸至空间无穷远。

Result: 弦必须与视界角速度一致以保持类时特性，因此被拖拽旋转并缠绕黑洞。观察到负能量首先落入黑洞，随后正能量跟随，表明短期内发生能量提取。外部区域产生波并携带提取能量向远处传播。

Conclusion: 波传播后系统趋于Boos和Frolov发现的静态构型，总提取能量估计为E_ext≲μM，其中μ为弦张力。该研究揭示了非刚性旋转弦能量提取的瞬态动力学过程。

Abstract: The interaction between a Nambu-Goto string and a Kerr black hole gives one of the methods of energy extraction from a rotating black hole. Although the properties of such processes have been well studied for rigidly rotating strings, little is known for non-rigidly rotating strings. In this paper, we study time evolution of a Nambu-Goto string on the equatorial plane of a Kerr spacetime, which sticks on the horizon and extends to spatial infinity. The time evolution is studied by the series expansion with respect to $t$ and the numerical simulations, which give reliable results for $t\lesssim 4M$ and $t\lesssim 38M$, respectively, where $M$ is the black hole mass. Since the angular velocity of the string on the horizon must coincide with the horizon angular velocity to keep the timelike property, the string is dragged into rotation and coils around the black hole. The negative energy is observed to fall into the black hole, but the positive energy follows after that, meaning that the energy extraction occurs for a short period of time. In the outside region, a wave is generated and propagates to the distant region carrying the extracted energy. After the propagation of the wave, the system approaches the time-independent configuration found by Boos and Frolov, and the total extracted energy is estimated as $E_{\rm ext}\lesssim μM$, where $μ$ is the tension of the string.

</details>


### [161] [Time Like Geodesics of Regular Black Holes with Scalar Hair](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20661)
*P. A. González,Marco Olivares,Eleftherios Papantonopoulos,Yerko Vásquez*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究分析了由幻标量场（phantom scalar field）支撑的渐近平坦正则黑洞（regular black holes）中的类时测地线（timelike geodesics）。通过引入标量荷（scalar charge）参数A消除中心奇点，研究其对粒子轨道的影响，包括稳定/不稳定圆轨道、ISCO（innermost stable circular orbit）以及散射阈值的变化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索由幻标量场支撑的正则黑洞中类时测地线的性质。这类黑洞通过标量荷参数A消除中心奇点，同时保持渐近平坦性（asymptotic flatness），为研究黑洞几何修正对粒子轨道的影响提供了理论框架。

Method: 研究方法包括推导大质量试验粒子（massive test particles）的运动方程，根据守恒能量和角动量对束缚轨道（bounded trajectories）和非束缚轨道（unbunded trajectories）进行分类。通过分析确定圆轨道（circular orbits）、临界轨道（critical orbits）和ISCO的位置，并研究捕获与散射（capture and scattering）之间的转变。

Result: 研究结果显示标量荷显著改变了不稳定和稳定圆轨道、ISCO以及散射阈值角动量（threshold angular momentum for scattering）的位置，这些变化对径向坐标呈现非平凡依赖关系。在弱场区域（weak-field regime），计算得到近日点进动（perihelion precession）的修正项与标量荷成正比，为利用太阳系观测约束标量荷提供了可能。

Conclusion: 结论表明标量荷参数A虽然保持了与史瓦西极限（Schwarzschild limit）的定性结构联系，但定量偏差编码了标量毛（scalar hair）的几何效应。物理尺度自然由不变面积半径（invariant areal radius）R(r)=√(r²+A²)描述，为零角动量运动分析提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We investigate timelike geodesics in asymptotically flat regular black holes supported by a phantom scalar field characterized by a scalar charge $A$. This parameter removes the central singularity and continuously deforms the Schwarzschild geometry while preserving asymptotic flatness. We derive the equations of motion for massive test particles and classify bounded and unbounded trajectories in terms of the conserved energy and angular momentum. We determine circular and critical orbits, including the innermost stable circular orbit (ISCO), and analyze the transition between capture and scattering. We show that the scalar charge modifies the location of the unstable and stable circular orbits, the ISCO, and the threshold angular momentum for scattering, exhibiting a nontrivial dependence on the radial coordinate. Their physical scales are naturally described in terms of the invariant areal radius $R(r)=\sqrt{r^2+A^2}$. In the weak-field regime, we compute the perihelion precession and obtain corrections proportional to the scalar charge, allowing us to constrain the scalar charge from Solar System observations. We also analyze the motion with vanishing angular momentum and show that, while the qualitative structure of the trajectories remains connected to the Schwarzschild limit $A\to 0$, the quantitative deviations encode the geometric effects of the scalar hair.

</details>


### [162] [General Relativity via differential forms -- explorations in Plebanski's Formalism for GR](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20772)
*Adam Shaw*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文采用手性（chiral）表述研究广义相对论（general relativity），利用四维洛伦兹群（Lorentz group）分解为自对偶（self-dual）和反自对偶（anti-self-dual）扇区的优势，发展新的分析和数值工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在利用手性表述揭示爱因斯坦方程（Einstein's equations）的额外结构，这些表述将广义相对论表达为使用2-形式（2-forms）而非度规（metric）的Plebanski表述或纯联络（pure connection）方法。

Method: 研究分为四个部分：第一部分使用纤维丛（fibre bundles）建立几何基础，其中2-形式作为SO(3,C)丛上的焊接形式（soldering forms）；第二部分研究手性框架下爱因斯坦方程的线性化形式及其规范固定（gauge fixings）；第三部分将分析扩展到非线性区域并研究黑洞时空（black hole spacetimes）的复几何结构；第四部分转向数值相对论（numerical relativity），探索基于手性表述的演化方案。

Result: 手性表述为爱因斯坦方程提供了新的分析视角，特别是在线性化处理、规范固定选择以及黑洞时空的复几何结构理解方面。这些表述还启发了数值相对论中新的演化方案构建。

Conclusion: 手性表述为广义相对论研究提供了强大的框架，不仅揭示了爱因斯坦方程的深层结构，还为分析和数值方法的发展开辟了新途径，特别是在黑洞时空的几何理解和数值演化方面。

Abstract: This thesis studies general relativity (GR) using chiral formulations, which take advantage of the decomposition of the four-dimensional Lorentz group into self-dual and anti-self-dual sectors. Within this framework, GR can be expressed using Plebanski's formulation, where the basic variables are triples of 2-forms rather than a metric, or alternatively through pure connection approaches. These viewpoints expose additional structure in Einstein's equations (EEs) and offer new analytical and numerical tools. Part I develops the geometric foundations using fibre bundles, where the 2-forms arise as soldering forms on an SO(3,C) bundle. Part II investigates the linearised form of EEs in the chiral setting, with particular attention to their gauge fixings. Part III extends this analysis to the nonlinear regime, and also examines the complex-geometric structure underlying black hole spacetimes. The final part turns to numerical relativity, exploring evolution schemes built from the chiral formulations and their associated gauge choices.

</details>


### [163] [Geodesic Completeness in General Cosmological Scenarios](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20809)
*William H. Kinney*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: Borde-Guth-Vilenkin定理表明暴胀时空通常具有测地线过去不完备性，需要某种暴胀前边界。该定理可推广至非均匀和循环模型，例如Ijjas-Steinhardt循环模型也被证明是测地线不完备的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: Borde-Guth-Vilenkin定理可成功推广至更广泛的时空模型。具体而言，Ijjas-Steinhardt循环模型被证明是测地线不完备的，这支持了定理的普遍适用性。

Abstract: The well-known Borde-Guth-Vilenkin Theorem shows that inflationary spacetimes are generically geodesically past-incomplete, necessitating the existence of a pre-inflationary boundary of some sort, possibly singular. I discuss the generalization of the BGV theorem to spacetimes beyond inflation, including inhomogeneous and cyclic models. As an example, I show that the cyclic model proposed by Ijjas and Steinhardt is geodesically incomplete.

### [164] [Interplay of Flat-band and Anderson localizations in disordered moire superlattices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20272)
*Qian Liu,Xiaoshuang Xia,Junjie Wang,Peilong Hong,Lei Xu,Lujun Huang,Daohong Song,Yi Liang*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该研究通过结合局域化长度标度与微分概率密度分析，揭示了部分无序一维硅莫尔晶格中平带局域化与安德森局域化的竞争机制，为设计鲁棒的非理想莫尔光子器件提供了指导原则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 莫尔超晶格中的无序同时削弱平带局域化并诱导安德森局域化，但这两者如何相互作用尚不清楚。研究旨在揭示无序莫尔系统中竞争局域化机制的直接证据。

Method: 引入了一个结合局域化长度标度（localization-length scaling）与微分概率密度分析（differential probability density analysis）的框架，用于映射部分无序一维硅莫尔晶格中的局域化转变。

Result: 研究发现：带隙内的平带即使无序增强仍保持强局域化；与色散带相交的平带则呈现丰富行为：低频分支经历逆安德森转变（inverse Anderson transition），高频分支在强无序下支持平带与安德森局域化的共存。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了无序莫尔系统中竞争局域化机制的直接证据，并为设计鲁棒的非理想莫尔光子器件（moire photonic devices）提供了指导原则。

Abstract: Disorder in moire superlattices simultaneously degrades flat-band localization and induces Anderson localization, yet how these two regimes interact has remained unclear. Here, we introduce a combined framework linking localization-length scaling with differential probability density analysis to map localization transitions in partially disordered one-dimensional silicon moire lattices. It is found that flat bands confined within the interband gap keep their strong localization even as disorder grows. In contrast, flat bands intersecting dispersive bands exhibit rich behaviors: the low-frequency branch undergoes an inverse Anderson transition, while the high-frequency branch supports coexisting flat-band and Anderson localization at strong disorder. Our results deliver the direct evidence of competing localization mechanisms in disordered moire systems and offer guiding principles for engineering robust, nonideal moire photonic devices.

</details>


### [165] [Autonomous Emergence of Hamiltonian in Deep Generative Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20821)
*Wenjie Xi,Wei-Qiang Chen*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种代数框架，用于提取生成模型学习到的隐含物理相互作用。通过将黎曼扩散分数场（Riemannian diffusion score field）的零噪声极限与热力学恢复力建立精确等价关系，利用训练好的神经网络作为直接力估计器。应用于受挫的一维O(3)自旋玻璃系统，成功恢复了微观哈密顿量参数，与真实参数达到99.7%的余弦相似度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 深度生成模型（如AlphaFold3）在复杂多体系统中的预测成功引发了一个认识论问题：这些网络仅仅是记忆数据分布，还是自主推导了底层物理定律？本研究旨在定量检验生成模型是否真正学习并内化了物理规则。

Method: 引入严格的代数框架，建立黎曼扩散分数场（Riemannian diffusion score field）零噪声极限与热力学恢复力的精确等价关系。将训练好的神经网络作为直接力估计器，应用于序列依赖的受挫一维O(3)自旋玻璃系统。使用O(3)-等变注意力架构，仅基于热平衡快照进行训练，通过超定线性反演恢复微观哈密顿量参数。

Result: 在没有引入任何能量先验的情况下，成功恢复了自旋系统的微观哈密顿量参数。推断出的哈密顿量参数与真实相互作用参数达到99.7%的余弦相似度。这些稀疏的局部参数单独解释了神经网络预测的连续力场中87%的方差。

Conclusion: 研究结果为深度生成架构不仅仅是进行统计模式匹配，而是自主发现并内化了底层物理规则提供了定量、可证伪的证据。这表明生成模型能够从数据中提取物理定律，而非仅仅记忆数据分布。

Abstract: The unprecedented predictive success of deep generative models in complex many-body systems, such as AlphaFold3, raises an epistemological question: do these networks merely memorize data distributions via high-dimensional interpolation, or do they autonomously deduce the underlying physical laws? To address this, we introduce a rigorous algebraic framework to extract the implicit physical interactions learned by generative models. By establishing an exact equivalence between the zero-noise limit of a Riemannian diffusion score field and the thermodynamic restoring force, we utilize the trained neural network as a direct force estimator. Applying this framework to a sequence-dependent, frustrated 1D $O(3)$ spin glass, we probe the latent representations of an $O(3)$-equivariant attention architecture trained solely on thermal equilibrium snapshots. Without incorporating any energetic priors, an overdetermined linear inversion successfully recovers the microscopic Hamiltonian parameters of the spin system. The inferred Hamiltonian parameters exhibit a $99.7\%$ cosine similarity with the ground-truth interaction parameters. Furthermore, these sparse local parameters alone are sufficient to explain $87\%$ of the variance in the continuous force field predicted by the network. Our results provide quantitative, falsifiable evidence that deep generative architectures do not merely perform statistical pattern matching, but autonomously discover and internalize the underlying physical rules.

</details>
